Likhansela leliWadi ngilo lelimele liwadi kumkhandlu kantsi tonkhe tincumo tetinchubomgomo netinhlelo tentiwa ngumkhandlu . Imfundvo nekucecesha lokuchubekako ( FET ) . Luhlelo lwe-FET alusebenti . Luncane kakhulu kantsi nelizinga lemiphumela walo liphasi . Kudzingeka kutfutfukiswa kwelizinga lokuchubekako njengobe luhlelo lukhula . Lizinga nekufaneleka kwetifundvo kudzinga kubukwa ngekushesha . Uma lizinga licala kuba ncono nekucasheka kwalabaneticu kucala kwenyuka , sidzingo setinhlelo te-FET nato titawenyuka ngalokutentakalelako . Kukhulisa imboni nje ngaphandle kwekugcila ezingeni kungenteka kubite kakhulu kucedze nemoya kubantfu labasha , kuphindze kunike luhlelo ligama lelibi . Nga-2030 , umkhakha we-FET kumele ube sewuhlanganise emaphesenti langema-25 eminyaka yebudzala lefanele , lokusho kwenyuka kusuka ema-300 0 lamuhla kuye esigidzini lesi-1.25 nga-2030 . Lutjalomali eNingizimu Afrika lwehle kusukela ezingeni lelisemkhatsini lelicishe libe ngemaphesenti langema-30 e-GDP ngasekucaleni kweminyaka yabo-1980 kuyewufinyelela kumaphesenti lali-16 e-GDP ngasekucaleni kwabo-2000 . Kuchitjwa kwemali kusakhiwonchanti sesive nako kusemazingeni laphasi nakubukwa emazinga emlandvo . Ngalokungiko , iNingizimu Afrika ilahlekelwe kakhulu ngekutjala imali kutemgwaco , loliwe , emachweba , gezi emanti , tinhlelo tekuhambisa emangcoliso , tekutfutsa tesive kanye netetindlu . Kukhula ngekushesha nangendlela lehlanganisa konkhe , lelive lidzinga lizinga lelisetulu lekuchitfwa kwemali . Kuhleleka kwemali lesimile kudzinga kufinyelela kumaphesenti langema-30 e-GDP nga-2030 , nekusisa emkhakheni wahulumende lokufinyelela kumaphesenti lalishumi e-GDP , kute kube nemtselela losimeme etinhlelweni tekukhula netasekhaya . Kumsebenti lolandzelako emalunga emmango aphakamisa umncamulajucu wesikhatsi lovumbulula umlandvo walommango . Ngekuphawula emaphethini nemikhuba lephindzaphindzekako lomsebenti kumele utibise kuvisisa kwemmango mayelana nesimo sawo futsi kuwente ucabange mayelana nekuphumelela kwekungenelela kwangaphambilini . Kuze kufike 1970 , i-Seymour kwakuyindzawo lenemphucuko yekulima . Umnotfo wawusimiswe yinkapani yemapulango , neyekwenta lugwayi mango edolobheni . Lugwayi , emazambane netitselo betilinyelwa kutsengiswa kulendzawo . Kwakha umbuso lokhonako nalotfutfukisako . Tinsayeya letinyenti tidzinga kunakwa , kufaka ekhatsi kunganeli kwemakhono lokujulile , luhlelo lwekusebentisana kwabohulumende lolunkimbitekile , emazinga enkhohlakalo lasetulu , butsakatsaka bekutiphendvulela , kunganaki kushaywa kwemtsetfo longakeneli kanye nemlandvo wesikhatsi lesidze wekuhudvulelana phasi emkhatsini welicembu kanye nahulumende . Leti tindzaba letimatima , letidzinga kubukwa ngekwetsembeka , kuhlelwa ngekucophelela kanye nebuholi lobucinile . Khetsa lababili labangadlala umdlalwana wemamintisi lamatsatfu , banikete sikhashana kutsi bacabange kutsi batawenta njani lomdlalwana . Cinisekisa kutsi labanye bafundzi niyabafihlela lokutawudlalwa . Batise bonkhe bafundzi kutsi batawubukela umdlalwana . Bakhumbute kutsi kulemidlalo , badlali batabe bakhombisa imicondvo lebacelwe kutsi bayidlale , hhayi yabo . Kutiphendvulela ngulomunye wemigomo lebalulekile yemaKomidi eLiwadi , njengemakhansela lakhetsiwe , atiphendvulela emmangweni labawusebentelako . Kulandzelela nekuhlola imiklamo yemmango , ngekumikisa imibiko njalo njalo njalo emmangweni ngenchubo yekusebenta , yindlela lekahle yekuhlola . Kuchumana kwemaciniso ngelwati emkhatsini kwemkhandlu nemmango , nasemkhatsini kwemmango nabobonkhe labatsintsekako kubalulekile . Kungaletsi lwati lolufanele kungaholela encabanweni emkhatsini kwawo onkhe emacembu . Kungagcugcutela kwandza kwemanga , kwakhe kungevani phatsi kwetakhamiti . Loku kungabambelela tintfutfuko nobe inchubekelaphambili mayelana ne-IDP nobe leminye imiklamo . EmaKomidi eLiwadi asebentisana netigaba letibanti talabatsintsekako . Loku kufaka ekhatsi likhansela leliwadi , tisebenti tamasipala ngisho nemeya lombala , imenenja yamasipala , tisebenti tentfutfuko yemmango , baholi bendzabuko nemmango , lababuya emacenjini lamanyenti lehlukene njengetinhlangano tetenkholo , ummango wetemabhizinisi , emacembu elusha , emacembu ebesifazane , tinhlangano tebalimi , nemacembu emikhakha netinhlangano . Bunguwe - imimango ingehluka mayelana nekudzabuka kwetive , tenkholo , indzawo letibuya kuyo , lokungenta kuhishana . Kuchamuka kwebantfu labanyenti labavela kulelinye live labakhuluma lulwimi lolwehlukile labanemasiko lehlukile nobe labavela kulesinye sifundza nobe lidolobha kungabanga kucabana . Lemimango ' ingabonakala nobe iviwe ' ngemalunga emmango ngendlela lembi . Kakhiwa kwetindlu : Sicelo setimali eBhodini yeTindlu yaVelonkhe kucedza tinkinga tekweswelakala kwetindlu kulendzawo siphasisiwe . Kepha , kubambelela kukhipha imali , tikhalo temhlaba endzaweni yekwakha nekwenta kancane kwekukhiswa kwemhlaba wahulumende uye emmangweni wenta lomklamo ungakhoni kuphumelela . Emakomidi emaWadi kumele agcugcutele umdladla kubemdzabu kutsi batingenele letintsintsa kuphatfwa kwabo . Ngibo labachumanisa ummango nekhansela yamasipala . Emakomidi emaWadi angatenta tincomo kumconzisitinkhulumo wamasipala ngemitsetfo letsintsa imihambo yeliWadi labo . Nga-2030 , luhlelo lwetemphilo kumele lunikete kwelapha lokusezingeni kuwo wonkhe umuntfu , lolumahhala endzaweni lokutfolakala kulo lusito , nobe lolukhokhelwe ngumshwalense wahulumende nobe wangasese . Luhlelo lwetemphilo lwekucala nelwesigodzi kumele lufinyeleleke ngalokufanako , ngekugcila ekuvimbeleni , emfundvweni , ekusingatfweni nasekwelapheni tifo . Tibhedlela kumele tisebente ngalokuphumelelisako , tinikete kwelapha kwesibili nalokusetulu lokusezingeni kulabo labakudzingako . Letinye tisebenti tetemphilo leticeceshiwe kumele tibe khona , ikakhulukati emimangweni lephuyile . YINCHUBO YEKUKALA IMITSELELA LETABAKHONA KUBAFATI NASEMADVODZENI LELETFWA NGUNOMA NGUSIPHI SINYATSELO LESIHLELIWE , LOKUFAKA EKHATSI UMTSETFO , IMIGOMO , NOMA TINHLELO , KUNOMA NGIYIPHI INDZAWO NAKUTO TONKHE TIGABA . KUYINDLELA YEKWENTA LOKUKHATSATA BAFATI NEMADVODZA NALOKUBEHLELE EMPHILWENI KUBEYINCENYE YAFUTSI EKWAKHENI , KWENTA LOKUHLELIWE , KULANDZELALA NEKUBUKETA IMIGOMO NETINHLELO KUTOTONKHE TINHLANGOTSI TEMBUSAVE , TEMNOTFO , NENHLALO YEMMANGO KUTE KUTSI BAFATI NAMADVODZA BAZUZE NGEKUFANA NEKUTSI KUNGALINGANI KUNGABHEBHETELEKI . INHLOSO YEKUGCINA KUTSI KUBE NEKULINGANA NGEKWETEBULILI . Ekwetfuleni kwalokuhamba embili kwalesakhiwonchanti , kubalulekile kucinisekisa kutsi imimango yasetindzaweni tasemakhaya iyazuza kusakhiwonchanti salokutsengwa ngebunyenti neseluhlelochumano kanye nekutsi nemanani alesakhiwonchanti ayavelana netidzingo temimango yasetindzaweni tasemakhaya . Bachubisifundvo kumele basekelwe bochwepheshe beCBP . Labochwepheshe batawuniketa kwesekela kwesithekniki nekwetisetjentiswa futsi batawuniketwa umtfwalo macondzana nemawadi latsite . Isayensi nethekhinoloji kuyachubeka nekugucula indlela imphahla netinsita lokukhicitwa nalokuhwebelwana ngayo . Njengelive lelinemali lengenako lesemkhatsini , iNingizimu Afrika idzinga kusebentisa lwati lwayo kanye nemikhicito wayo lecanjwe kabusha kute ikwati kucudzelana . Ngekutimela , tindleko lekungacudzelwana ngato tekukhicita ngete tenela ekwandziseni kuba khona kwetimboni taseNingizimu Afrika emaveni emhlaba . Loku kucondziswe kuyo yomibili imkhakha lemisha yetimboni nalesebenta ngendlela leyetayelekile , lenjengetimayimi . Kucamba kabusha kuyadzingeka eliveni lelingenisa imali lesemkhatsini kute likwati kutfutfuka . WONKHE UMMANGO EMHLABENI WONKHE UBEKA UMCABANGO WAWO WAHULUMENDE KUBUNJALO NASEZINGENI LEMISEBENTI LOYITFOLAKO ETISEBENTINI TAHULUMENDE . ' BUSO ' BAHULUMENDEUBUSO KANYE / NOME LIVI LEBETFULIMISEBENTI LABASEMBILI . LOKU NGIKO KONKHE BANTFU LABAKUTFOLAKO KANTSI UMA IMISEBENTI IYELIZINGA LELIPHANSI NOBE ITE BUNGANI , HULUMENDE USHESHE ABONWE ANGULOHLULEKAKO NALONGASEBENTI . UMA IMISEBENTI IMIBI , HULUMENDE MUBI KANTSI UMA UMSEBENTI UMUHLE , HULUMENDE MUHLE , KUNGALEYONDLELA . LOKU KUNJALO EMHLABENI WONKHE KANTSI AKUNAMEHLUKO ENINGIZIMU AFRIKA . Kuhlela KwaMasipala neMitsetfo yeKusebenta , 2001 ubeka luhlobo lweTinhlelo teKulawula kuSebenta . Njengoba eMaKomidi eLiwadi adlala indzima ekulandzeleni kusebenta kwamasipala , emalunga kumele ati lokucuketfwe yimitsetfo . Iminyaka lelishumi nesiphohlongo yangena embusweni wentsandvo yelintenti , iNingizimu Afrika solomane ingummango lonekungalingani lokusetulu lapho linyenti lebantfu liphuyile futsi kusebenta lidlanzana . Lizinga lemfundvo yelinyenti lebafundzi labamnyama liphasi . Kwehlukana kwebantfu lokwabangwa lubandlululo kusachubeka nekubusa kulelive . Linani lelisetulu lebantfu labasha libona kutsi alinawo ematfuba . Lifa lelashiywa lubandlululo liyachubeka nekuncumela linyenti ematfuba emphilo . Letinsayeya letinkhulu nakangaka tingalungiswa ngesinyatselo lesigucula kusebenta kwalelive . Kumele kunakekelwe kutsi kufakwe umphumela longucalangaye lovela emacenjini lancisheke ematfuba kakhulu . Kusungula luhlelochumano lwemucu lwavelonkhe , lwesigodzi nelwamasipala kute kube nendlela yekufinyelela luhlelochumano lolubanti . Lutjalomali lwangasese ludzinga kuhola embili kulomkhakha , lwelekwe timali tesive letidzingekako kute kuhlangatjetanwe nalenjongo yetenhlalo . Kudzingeka ngekushesha tinchubomgomo letifanele , imitsetfo leshayiwe kanye nekuhlelwa kwetikhungo kute kutewuzuzwa loku . Kugucula lomnotfo ngumklamo lonetinsayeya newesikhatsi lesidze . Ngalokufisha , siphakamisa kukhutsatwa emakhono ebantfu , emandla ekukhicita kanye nesakhiwonchanti kute kwenyuswe kutfunyelwa ngaphandle kwemphahla , lokutawenyusa imitfombolusito yelutjalomali kuphindze kunciphise kwetsembela emalini levela ngaphandle . Lutjalomali lolusetulu , luhambisana nesakhiwonchanti semmango kanye nemakhono lancono , kutakwenta umnotfo ukhule ngekushesha futsi ube ngulokhicitako . Kwenyusa ematfuba emsebenti nemkhicito kutawuholela ekwenyukeni kwemali lengenako nasemazingeni ekuphila kunciphe kungalingani . Kugucula umnotfo uye eluhlangotsini , wekutjalwa kwemali kanye nekusebentisa kwetinsita lokuphasi kuyadzingeka ekuchubekeleni embili kwemnotfo kwesikhatsi lesidze . Ingacedvwa i-IDP , itfunyelwa kumkhandlu wamasipala kute ibukisiswe iphasiswe . Umkhandlu kumele ubuke kutsi i-IDP iyatikhomba yini tinkinga letibhekene nendzawo , nekutsi emacebo nemiklamo atawukhona kanganani kufaka sandla ekulweni netinkinga . Umkhandlu kumele wente siciniseko kutsi i-IDP ihambisana netidzingo temtsetfo ingakaphasiswa . Kuchumana kuyindlela lekabili . Kuchumana kugijima nekuniketana lwati nemibono kusuka kumunye umuntfu kuya kulo munye . Yinchubo lapho khona umuntfu , lokusho UMTFUMI , sitfuma umlayeto kulomunye umuntfu lowamukela lomlayeto , lokutsiwa NGUMAMUKELI . Uma singachumani ngalokuphumelelisako , kubanekuhishana , nekungevani , kungasusa nencabano . Ngoba eMakomidi eLiwadi ayindlela lemcoka yekuchumana kuhulumende wasekhaya , kumele ente siciniseko kutsi lwati labaluniketa ummango lungemaciniso , luviwa nguye wonkhe muntfu , nabo ngakulolunye luhlangotsi , bamikisa lwati lolungemaciniso kumkhandlu nakumakhansela . Khumbuta labatimbandzakanyile kutsi luhlaka lwekwentiwa kwemisebenti lilithebula lelingabancedza hhayi kubavimbela . Kufanele libukwe njengemculu lophilako longaguculwa uphindze ulungiswe ngekuhamba kwesikhatsi . Ngendlela lebonakalako IBatho Pele itakuba nemtselela endleleni lokwentiwa ngayo umsebenti ngekucinisaLuhlelo Lwekulawula Kusebenta lokungiyo lebeka tinkhomba tekusebenta ngaloko yenta hulumende wasekhaya kanye netakhamiti bakale imphumelelo basebentisa letinkhomba . Lapho kukhombisa kungasebenti , ichuba kungenelela lokudzingekako . Ifaka ekhatsi tigaba tekuhlela , kulandzelela kanye nekubuyeketwa kwekusebenta kwemnyaka . Kutfutfuka kweNingizimu Afrika kutsintfwa nguloko lokwenteka kulesigodzi kanye nasemhlabeni . Imphumelelo itaweyama ekuvisiseni kwalelive nasendleleni lelitawuphendvula ngayo kuleto tintfutfuko . Ngetulu kwekubukisiswa kabanti kubekwa kwebantfu , loluhlelo lukhuluma ngetinkhambiso letisihlanu letigcamile : kuntjintja kwetemnotfo wemhlaba , ithekhinoloji , tintfo letitsintsa umhlaba , kugucuka kwebunjalo besimo selitu kanye nekukhula kwetemnotfo wase-Afrika . UMSEBENTI 2 Ngutiphi tindlela tekusebentisana nalabadlala tindzima labavela ngephandle ? Imitsetfo leminyenti ishaywe yiPhalamende , emva kwelukhetfo lwentsandvoyelinyenti lwanga 1994 lolusekela luphindze lucinise likhono labomasipala kuphatsa tindzaba tabo nekwenta imisebenti yabo ngendlela yekutibandzakanya nekufaka linyenti . Kwakha kuhlanganyela kwemmango . Tinhlangano temmango nekuhlanganyela kwemmango kuyadzingeka kute kwakhiwe imimango lephephile . Tikhungo tekuphepha kwemmango kumele ticatjangwe . Timvula letinemandla tishiye kuguguleke wonkhe umhlaba etingadzini . Emanti bewakhelelwa emathangeni latawusebenta etinyangeni letitako kodvwa umsebenti lomnyenti kusafuneka wentiwe kute kubuyiselwe umklamo endzaweni yawo . Kukhipha umnotfo wetimbiwakute kukhicitwe imitfombolusito letakwenyusa emazinga ekuphila , emakhono kanye nesakhiwonchanti ngendlela lesimeme . Lenkholelo iphindze yemukele ' ekusimameni ngekwendalo ' kwabo bonkhe bantfu . Loku kusho kutsi wonkhe umuntfu unesandla langasifaka kuto tonkhe tincenye temphilo yakhe . Iphindze ikhutsate emaKomidi emaWadi njengesikhungo lesichumanisa baholi labakhetsiwe kanye nebantfu . Kumele kwetfulwe luhlelo lolucubile lwekucasha tinhloko tematiko , loluhlanganisa tincenye tetembusave kanye netekuphatsa . Ngumaphi Emalunga eKomidi yeliWadi lekufanele atfweswe umtfwalo wekwenta imisebenti letsite ? Uma loku kwentiwa kwekucala , kutawucukatsi tinhlangotsi tenchubo letinyenti . Nanobe kunjalo , uma umsebenti wekusabalalisa kulowo nalowo mhlangano weliKomidi leWadi kutawuhamba kuba selubala njengobe umsebenti ucala . Kute umklamo uphumelele kubalulekile kutsi lichaza nemsebenti welilunga ngalinye lelicembu uchazwe ngekunakekela lokukhulu . Lilunga ngalinye lelitimbandzakanye nalomklamo linemsebenti wekwenta umsebenti walo ngendlela lechubekelisa tinhloso temklamo phambili naleticinisekisa kuphumelela kwawo . Simo sekwakhiwa : Kumele balandzele imibandzela yavelonkhe ngetifundvo nangekusebenta phambilini . IBatho Pele ibeka kutsi ematiko ezingeni lavelonkhe neletifundza kumele abe netinhlelo tekulawula kusebenta letitawufaka ekhatsi kubekwa kwetinkhomba tekwetfulwa kwetinsita kanye nekukala kwekusebenta . INingizimu Afrika kumele yente ngekulandzela kutsi tigidzi tebantfu letikwatiko kusebenta tifuna kusebenta . Esikhatsini lesifisha , umnotfo udzinga kwakhiwe imisebenti yebahlali baseNingizimu Afrika labangasebenti , linyenti labo lokungulabasha labanemakhono laphasi , babe batfutfukisa emakhono nelwati bentela sikhatsi lesitako setemnotfo lowehlukile . Kwenyusa emazinga ekusebenta kutakuba netimbuyeketo ngetulu kwelwati loluhlomisako lwekuba nemsebenti . Kutawusita bantfu kutsi basise emfundvweni yebantfwana babo , bente ncono emakhaya abo babuye basingatse tingoti temphilo . Umsebenti nemfundvo kutakwenta kutsi bahlali bente ncono timphilo tabo . Simo siyavela , siphendvulwa ngekutiphatsa lokusuka emicabangweni nasemiveni . Ingabe luhlolo lwetidzingo / nelucwaningo lwangempela luyakufaka luhlolo-mibuto lwebesilisa nebesifazane futsi ingabe lumele yonkhe imiphakatsi ( labancane / nalabadzala , basemaphandleni / nasemadolobheni , ngetebuhlanga ? ) Ingabe bobabili bomake nabobabe batayentalungenela yini loluhlolo-mibuto bese bagcogca lwatiso ? Kulondvolota : Ngabe linani lemhlaba wetiganga nobe wemvelo liye lenyuka nobe lehla ? Kungani ? Ngabe tikhona tindzawo letivikelekile letiye tasungulwa ? Ngabe kunetindzawo letinemanti lanelinani lelisetulu kutemagugu , kulodvolota nobe kukhibika , sib. titete , emachibi , ema-eshuwari , emadamu , imifula ? Kubalulekile kunciphisa tindleko tekuphila temakhaya laphuyile . Letinye tincenye teluhlelo titakuba nemtselela wekwenyusa tindleko emnotfweni . Ikakhulukati , kwenta sakhiwonchanti sibe sesimanje ngemuva kweminyalishumi yekungatjalwa kahle kungadzinga emanani lasetulu . Kumelana nalokwenyuka , inchubomgomo kumele igcile ekwenyuseni kucudzelana nekusisa kusakhiwonchanti lesisha emikhakheni letsintsa ngco labaphuyile , lenjengemjikeleto wekudla , tekutfutsa temmango , temfundvo netemphilo kanye netekuchumana . Kusebenta kahle kwemkhakha wahulumende kutawuphindze kuholelele esakhiweni lesibita kancane setemnotfo . Bani nesiciniseko kutsi lemiklamo lekhonjiwe icondze ngco etintfweni letimcoka nemigomo lekhonjiwe esigabeni lesendlulile . Kulawula umsebenti kuhambelana nekwetfulwa kwetinsita , kokubili kuchazwa yindlelasu yeBatho Pele leyangeniswa nga-1997 . Kwenta ncono kukhutsala kwebahlali ngenhloso yekucinisa intfutfuko , intsandvo yelinyenti kanye nekutiphendvulela . Umhlangano welicembu lelikhulu nelicembu lemmango lobanti lapho imiphumela yemsebenti weliviki lofaka ekhatsi uMvila-balave , imiphumela lehlanganisiwe kanye nemininingwane ngalowo nalowo mphumela kube sekuyadzingidvwa bese kuvunyelanwa ngabocalangaye bemmango . Chaza kutsi uma loku kwentiwa emmangweni lomuntfu losibhalako angasebentisa imizuzu yamabhalane , emarekhodi emmango kanye nemanotsi emhlelembini kutsi atfole imininingwane uma kunesidzingo . Umuntfu lokuchunyanwa naye nemininingwane . Umsebenti 5 Tsatsisa kuMtsetfosisekelo , utfole kutsi yini umsebenti waHulumende waSekhaya . Ungumake lolima tibhidvo kute wondle umndeni wakho . Indvodza yakho isebenta edolobheni lelincane , iphindze ibe lilunga leliKomidi leliWadi . Letibhidvo wondla ngato umndeni wakho , letinye utitsengise emakethe kute utewutfola imali . Ngaphandle kwaloku , ute lenye imali . Indvodza yakho ayikuniki imali , kuphela nje ibuya nekudla kanye nalokudzingekile edolobheni . Uyayidzinga imali longayisebentisa kutsengela bantfwabakho tipho , noma ubhadale tindleko temtfolamphilo nakwentikile waya khona . Indvodza yakho ifika ikutjela kutsi kunemngani wayo lofuna kukutsengisela letibhidvo takho edolobheni lelikhulu . Likomishane lemalunengelo eluntfu linemandla ekuphenya nekubika ngemalungelo eluntfu , kutsatsa tinyatselo kubuyisa emalungelo ebantfu lasekahlukubetiwe , kwenta lucwaningo nekufundzisa ngemalungelo ebantfu . Kwemukela luhlelo loluhlanganisile . Kuzuza ummango lophephile kusho kubukana netimbangela letijulile tebugebengu , lokudzinga imitfombolusito yahulumende neyemmango lehlukahlukene . Kukhutsata kumelana nesimo kwebantfu nekwemnotfo ekugucukeni kwesimo selitulu . Sigaba 29 ( b ) seMtsetfo sichaza tinchubo lokumele tilandzelwe ekutfutfukiseni i-IDP lephawula kutsi kumele kucocisanwe nemmango waSekhaya mayelana netidzingo tekutfutfukisa nabocalangaye be-IDP kanye nekubandzakanyeka ekusukunyisweni kwayo . EmaKomidi eLiwadi kumele akhe indlelasu yekwenta kutsi ummango uyatiswa ngetindzaba temmango khona umkhandlu utokwati ngetindzaba temmango netimphendvulo tabo etinhlelweni temkhandlu netincumo . Kuchumana - loku tincwadzi letitfunyelwe ekomidini nobe leto letibhalelwe likomidi . Yonkhe imibhalo yekuchumana kufanele ibonwe likomidi isatfunyelwa ngeligama lalo . Kokucala , masipala kumele acondzisise kutsi ngutiphi tinsita latiletsako , ngubani lotitfolako , yini simo sato leto . Sibonelo : Tibutfwa kangaki tibi ? Bonkhe bahlali baseNingizimu Afrika kumele bagcugcutelwe kufundza Tilwimi Temdzabu kantsi netinhlelo tahulumende kumele tikucinisekise loko kutsi kuyenteka . Kutfutfukisa timboni letinjengekuhanjiswa kwemkhicito loluhlata , tekuvakasha , tetinhlanti kanye nemabhizimisi lamancane nakukhoneka . Kwabelana imibono nelicembu lonkhe . Kulandzelela kusebenta kwetisebenti . Indlela yekusombulula tinkinga ilithulusi lelisebentako kwelekelela emaKomidi eLiwadi . Ase sibuke nasi sibonelo ngentasi nekutsi ingasetjentiswa njani ngalokuphatsekako . Yenta / phendvula - uphendvule njani kulokushayisana ? Umncamulajucu wesikhatsi ulungiswa nelicembu lelatisako , lokuvamise kuba bantfu labacishe bangu-12 kuya ku-20 lokufaka ekhatsi luchungechunge lolubanti lwemacembu etenhlalakahle - emadvodza , labasikati , labasha , labadzala , basebentisi bemitfombolusito yemvelo , emacembu enshisekelo yetesimondzawo njll . Lomhlangano uvamise kutsatsa cishe ema-awa lamabili . Umgomo welinani lemhlaba nelulwandle lokungaphasi kwekuvikelwa ( kwanyalo cishe ngumhlaba longemahektha latigidzi letiyimfica , umngcengcema welugu longema-848km kanye nema-4 172km2 elulwandle kuvikelekile ) . Ikhansela yamasipala ingayakha imitsetfo kuyisita ekusebentiseni emandla ayo , ne kutsi njeitewusebenta kahle . Khumbula : labatibandzakanyako bangaba yincenye yemacembu langetulu kwalinye , nekutsi labatibandzakanyako akusibo labo lababanga kakhulu umsindvo ! Indzima yeliKomidi leliWadi iphindze ifake kusita nekusekela imitamo yemimango yekufezekisa tinhloso temisebenti yesikhashana lehlele kuyenta ngekwayo . Emacembu ekusebenta nobe emakomidi angazuza ngelwati lolusisekelo lwekulawula umsebenti wesikhashana . Kucinisa emakhono ekuhlela ahulumende . Kuba nesiciniseko salabamele labo labatsintsekako kumakomidi emiklamo yemisebenti . Cwephesha ngetebulili , noma umuntfu lonelwati ngetebulili , akabe yincenye yawo onkhe emacembu lakhelwe kuhlola luhlelo . Imitamo ayentiwe kutsi kube nebafati kanye nemadvodza kulamacembu . Tincenye tekutfutfukisa tahulumende wasekhaya ngekweluhlobo lwemcombelelotimali nemitsetfo yamasipala , kulawula kwetindzawo , kulawula kusebenta kwetisebenti tamasipala kanye neluhlelo lweKutfutfukisa loluBumbene ( IDP ) kukunye kuniketa ematfuba ekutibandzakanya kwemmango eluhlelweni lwamasipala . Kuzuza nekugcina lokulinganisa kudzinga kutselelana kwetincenye letinyenti , lokungasito tonkhe tato letingaphasi kwekuwulwa nguhulumende . Umnotfo lokhulako , kwenyuka kwematfuba emsebenti newemali lengenako , kuphela kwekungalingani , kwenta ncono luhlelo lwemfundvo , timo letifanele temabhizimisi kanye nekuntjintja imisebenti kutawufaka sandla kakhulu ekubumbeni bantfu baseNingizimu Afrika . Ngaphandle kwesimo lesinjalo , letindlela tingenyusa emazinga ekungevani kahle kutenhlalo . Loluhlelo lwenta tiphakamiso letinyenti tekwenta ncono kuphumeleliswa kwetinhlelo tekulungisa tintfo tangaphambilini , ikakhulukati leto letitsintsa kwandziswa kwematfuba etemnotfo kulabo bebancishwe ematfuba ngaphambilini . Kubonisana nekuphendvula - liKomidi leLiwadi lakha tinkhundla , sibonelo , kuhlela umhlangano wemmango , kukhuluma nemhlangano wemshayelwano , kukhuluma nemhlangano welicembu letemdlalo njalo njalo njalo . Kuletsa lwati netimphendvulo emmangweni mayelana netincumo temkhandlu , netintfo letiphakamiswe ngummango letibikelwe likhansela nobe umkhandlu . Licubungula letinhlobo letehlukahlukene temininingwane kumasipala walo letingaba lusito ekuhleleni . Tsatsa timphendvulo utibhale phasi eshadini leliphendvulekako kutsi wonkhewonkhe ayibone . Lomcondvo wekubukela baFati macondzana neNtfutfuo -WID - usuke ubuke bafati njengebantfu labamukela lusito lwentfutfuko ngaphandle kwekutentela lutfo bona , esikhundleni sekubabona njengebantfu labatentelako ekuguculeni timo tabo temnotfo , tenhlalo yemango , tembusave kanye netemasiko . Umphumela lohamba embili waloku kutsi , loko lokukhatsata bafati kwabukeka njengetintfo letitihambela todvwa letehlukile , kwaze kwaholela ekutseni letintfo tibekwe eceleni ngaphandle kweluhlaka lwekusebenta lwesive kanye naleminye imikhakha yesimo semphilo yesive . Ngalokuphatsekako , lomcondvo webaFati macondzana neNtfutfuko - WID - utsatsa tindzaba tebafati njengetintfo letingakaphatselani sanhlobo netinkhinga tentfutfuko letifana netemalungelo eluntfu , umbuso wentsandvo yeliningi , kuvikeleka kwemvelo , tenchubo yemave emhlaba wonkhe , kuthula , nekubeka phansi tikhali , njalonjalo . Kube nenhloko yekuphatfwa kwemisebenti yahulumende , lenesibopho sekuphatsa kuchubekela embili kufaka ekhatsi emacembu laheha bantfu emsebentini , kuhlolwa kwekusebenta kanye netinchubo tekucondziswa kwetigwegwe . Kuta emihlanganweni yemkhandlu - lungisa lubhaliso lwemalunga eKomidi yeLiwadi , niketa ngalinye lilunga umhlangano lotsite latawuhambela . Tinhlelo te-IDP takhiwa ngekubonisana emkhatsini kwematiko , wonkhe muntfu unetifiso kumiphumela . Kutsatfwa kwetincumo kwentiwa ngendlela levulekile neyentsandvo yelinyenti . Tinsita tabelwa imisebenti lesita ekufezeni imigomo yentfutfuko lekuvunyelenwe ngayo kumasipala . Lendlelasu icanjelwe kutsi ibe nemiphumela yemisebenti lefaka sandla ekutfutfukeni kwayo yonkhe indzawo , nenzuzo yakhe wonkhe umuntfu . EMakomidi eLiwadi ayindlela yekuchumana lehleliwe emkhatsini kwemmango kanye nemkhandlu . Ucabanga kutsi emaphakelo etimali amasipala kufanele ngani kutsi akhonjiswe takhamuti ? Tjela babambilichaza banikete tibonelo labangakufaka ekhatsi emalini letawuchitfwa neumholo umangabe benta liphakelo-timali lemndeni . Bhala letintfo eshadini leliphepha wakhe imigca lebhekentansi ibemibili , yibite utsi IMALI LESETJENTISIWE ne LIHOLO . Imali lesetjentisiwe ingafaka ekhatsi , lucingo , gezi , timali tesikolo . Umholo lingafaka ekhatsi emaholo , inkhokhelo ( umangabe banendlu yekucashisa nobe banetakhiwo tabo ) , umsebenti lowengetiwe labawentako loletsa imali . Kulum'uphuphutse - livela egameni lelitsi ' cubuta ' lokusho kwenta shangatsi uyalamula . Umkhandlu ' uvuma nje ngemlomo ' imibono netiphakamiso temmango ngenhloso yekuwujabulisa kodvwa ungenti nobe ungalandzeli imibono nobe tiphakamiso tawo . Linani leliphakelo-timali lamasipala lelisebente ekwenteni luhlelo lwemakhono asemsebentini . Kuyasita kakhulu kuvisisa lulwimi lolusetjentiswako kuPCM , nekwati kutsi ngumaphi lamanye emagama letinye tinhlobo letingawasebentisa , njengoba emalunga ekomidi yewadi atawuhlangabetana nawo lamagama ezingeni tsite . Lolulwimi lolusetjentiswa kulemojuli lulwimi loluvame kusetjentiswa kummongo wabohulumende basemakhaya baseNingizimu Afrika . Buncane bekugcina bemazinga ekuphila lamukelekile kumele kucaciswe , kufaka ekhatsi loko lokudzinga bantfu kute batfutfukise emakhono abo . LEMOJULI yehlukaniswe yaba tehluko letine , ekucaleni kunesehluko lesisetfulo salomcondvo wekulawulwa kwemklamo , bese kuba nesehluko sinye lesiphatselene nelizinga ngalinye kulawa lamatsatfu . Tsatsa timphendvulo letivela emacenjini . Uma ngetulu kwelicembu linye linembuto lofanako yenta sicinisekiso kutsi lelo nalelo cembu lifaka ligalelo . Kwenta sibonelo ungacela licembu linye kutsi liphendvule umbuto munye bese leli lelinye liphendvule incenye yesibili yalowo mbuto nobe umbuto wesibili . Ngakulolunye luhlangotsi ungatsatsa timphendvulo letimbalwa kulelo nalelo cembu bese udlulela ecenjini lelilandzelako . Tekukhangisa - sebentisa luchungechunge kwetindlela tekwatisa emaKomidi emaWadi , imimango , baholi bendzabuko kanye nebaholi bemibono ngekutsi kutawuba khona inchubo yeCBP . Kusebentisana - kuhishana kungavela ngendlelasu lefanele lengasetjentiswa kufinyelela emgomeni lokuvunyelwane ngawo . Sibonelo , bonkhe labatsintsekako bangavumelana kutsi tisebenti tahulumende kumele tinikete kusebenta lokunemphumelelo . Letinye takhamiti tingeva shengatsi timali kumele tisetjentiselwe kuceceshwa , labanye beve shengatsi bongcondvomshini labanyenti batawusita ekusombululeni kwetfula tinsita lokumfimfako . Kuhlanganisa CICBP ne-IDP kusungula litfuba lekucinisekisa kutsi i-IDP itinte kungcikitsi yasekhaya futsi iniketa inchazelo kutimfuno tekubandzakanyeka teMtsetfo wetiNhlelo taboMasipala , 2000 . Kumsebenti lolandzelako emalunga emmango aphakamisa umncamulajucu wesikhatsi lovumbulula umlandvo walommango . Ngekuphawula emaphethini nemikhuba lephindzaphindzekako lomsebenti kumele utibise kuvisisa kwemmango mayelana nesimo sawo futsi kuwente ucabange mayelana nekuphumelela kwekungenelela kwangaphambilini . Kusungulwa kwemikhandlu ye-AIDS yendzawo kubo boyimfica bomasipala bendzawo . Umkhakha wangasese ucasha cishe emakota lamatsatfu etisebenti taseNingizimu Afrika lokumele ngetulu kwalokubili kulokutsatfu kwelutjalomali kanye nemali lesetjentiswa ku-R&D . INingizimu Afrika idzinga umlingani wemkhakha wangasese lochubekela embili lotjala emandleni lakhicitako . Njengobe inhloso yenzuzo kungiyo lehola libhizimisi , tinkampani ngete takhula ngaphandle uma tisebenta esimeni lapho umsebenti nemazinga eliholo enyuka khona . Umtsetfo loshayiwe udzinga kutsi libhizimisi linake kulingana emsebentini , kuhlonyiswa kwalabamnyama kutemnotfo , simo , kutfutfukiswa kwemakhono , nalokucuketfwe lapha ekhaya , kutfutfukiswa kwemabhizimisi lamancane , sibopho semmango kutenhlalo kanye nalokunyenti lokubalulekile kwetindzawo letitsite , letinjengemasu ekutfutfukisa umkhakha wetimayini . Kulesimo lesimankimbonkimbo , kutetinshisekelweni tawo onkhe emabhizimisi elive kutsi akhule ngekushesha nekutsi bantfu labanyenti batfole imisebenti . Letingcikitsi letibalulekile tekusebenta letilandzelako kumele tibe yincenye yePMS yamasipala , kute tikhone kusetjentiswa ngumasipala . Leti tinkhomba tavelonkhe letikhishwa yindvuna emvakwekubonisana nebaphatsiswa betifundza bahulumende wasekhaya naSALGA . Lamaphuzu labhalwe ngephasi . Ngenca yekwehluka kwemiklamo kanye netinsayeya letingahle tivele , lelizinga lilodvwa libalulekile . Imiphumele yalelizinga iba luhlelo lwemsebenti lolusemtsetfweni lolutawuhola licembu lemklamo kuto tonkhe tinyatselo temklamo . Kwehlukahlukana enhlanganweni noma emmangweni kwamukela kwehlukana emkhatsini walabadvuna , nalabasikati , imihambo , nebuhlanga kute kusekeleke kubeketeleleka kwalokwehlukana , khona lokwehlukahlukana kutomukela letindlela tekwehlukahlukana . Loku kukuzama kufinyelela ekusebentisaneni lokunekuthula , kute kutsi inhlangano noma ummango uchubekele ekubambananeni nasekufezeni imigomo yawo lekucondvwe kuyo . . . Kutawudzingeka kutsi kutfolakale umchasi kute kukhokhelwe banakekeli , nekuvala tindleko taleloli . Lomchasi kutawufuneka kutsi abe nemali yekubhadala emaphasela ekudla . Tinsuku , tikhatsi kanye nemicimbi kutawugucuka kuye ngekwetidzingo temmango losebentisana nawo . Ikhansela yamasipala ingalibhidlita likomidi leliWadi nalehluka kufeza imigomo lelibekelwe wona . Tinkhombandlela teKusungulwa neKusebenta kweMaKomidi eLiwadi aboMasipala , Igazethi yaHulumende inombolo 27699 , Inhlaba -2005 Tinkhombandlela tichaza kutsi LiKomidi leLiwadi litimele , ngumtimba wekubonisa , kumele lingatsatsi luhlangotsi umalenta umsebenti walo nangaphandle kokwesaba , kuba nentsandvokati nekubukela phasi , nendzima lemcoka ledlalwa likomidi leliwadi njengesitfunywa lesenta umkhankhaso wekutibandzakanya kwemmango . Kwanyalo indzima yebuholi bendzabuko ngaphasi kweluhlelo lolusha lwahulumende wasekhaya ayikakacasiswa kahle . Takhiwo tendzabuko tisabaluleke kakhulu etindzaweni tasemaphandleni . Kwenta sibonelo , KaZulu-Natali buholi bendzabuko bendzawo budlale indzima legcamile kumklamo we-Isulabasha / Mvunyane wetemanti nekutfutfwa kwemangcoliso , kanye naseKomidini leKuhlela leSigodzi seMaluti . Nanobe tindzima nemisebenti yebaholi bendzabuko kusengakacaci , kumele badlale indzima kuCBP etindzaweni tasemaphandleni . Basebenta njengetikhungo tengucuko kanye nemnyango lobalulekile wekungena emmangweni njengobe bayahlonishwa futsi bayakwati kukhutsata bantfu . KWEHLUKAHLUKANA KUFANA NEMHLOBISO LOWAKHIWE NGETINCETU LETINEMIBALA LEMININGI : bonkhe bantfu labayincenye yenhlangano letsite bafana netincetu letincane letakha lomhlobiso lomabalabala ; bahlukahlukene kodvwa bayabumbaniseka babe yintfo yinye . Kusebenta ngalokuphumelelisako kweluhlelo lwabohulumende kuseludzaba lolushisa libunti . Tinhlaka tahulumende letehlukene tiyasebentisana futsi sidzinga kutfola tindlela tekucinisekisa kutsi tisebenta ngekubambisana kakhulu kunakucala . Loluhlelo luphakamisa kuntjintjwa kwendlela kusukela ekwetameni kutfola tinhlelo letinsha letihlelekile , letiphatamisako , letihlole kukhomba nekusombulula butsakatsaka lobutsite ekusebentisaneni nasekubeni nemandla . Hulumende udzinga kwenta ncono luhlelo lwakhe lwekuphatsa , lolufaka ekhatsi tivumelwano tekulamula emkhatsini wabomasipala besigodzi nebasekhaya lapho kunekuphindzaphindzeka nobe kushayisana ekuniketweni kwemisebenti kanye nemitfombolusito . Tifundza kumele tigcile emisebentini yato leyinhloko tiphindze tente ncono emandla ato ekwesekela nekubeka liso kuhulumende wasekhaya . Lubandlululo lushiye lifa lendzawo lelingasilihle . Njengobe emakhaya latigidzi leti-3.2 azuzile kulolu hlelo lolusha lwetetindlu , [ 1 ] netinhlelo kantsi nesakhiwonchanti siniketwe kumimango leminyenti , yincane kakhulu inchubekelembili leyentiwe ekuncobeni kungalingani ekuniketweni kwetindzawo . Kuletinye tehlakalo , tinchubomgomo tangemuva kwa-1994 ticinise kwehlukana ngetindzawo ngekubeka tindlu talabahola kancane emaphetselweni emadolobha . Umbuto 2 Libhuku lelikhuluma ngemsebenti lomkhulu liyayibeka yini ngalokusobala imigomo lebukele tindzaba tabesifazane , imiphumela kanye netinkhomba tekusebenta kulandzela imigomo yetfutfuko yemava onkhe emhlaba ? Lamanye emaphuzu emphilo yemmango ahambisana nesikhatsi semnyaka , njengemaphethini etifo , kusetjentiswa kwebasebenti , titungeletane tetekulima , kanye nekondleka . Lemisebenti lemibili lelandzelako ikwenta nconokwenta ncono kuvisiswa kwekuhambisana nesikhatsi semnyaka kanye nemikhuba yesikhatsi-dze . Ngekwenta lamaphethini nemikhuba labo labasezingeni lekuhlela ngalokubonakalako bayakhona kucombela tigameko letitsite bese balinganisa emasu nemachinga abo ngalokufanelekile . Usebentisa emanotsi esifundvo kusukela emakhasini 87 kuya ku-92 gcwalisela ngekuniketa imininingwane leyengetiwe . Phawula umehluko emkhatsini kwemchubisifundvo weliwadi , umchubisifundvo wamasipala kanye nelilunga leliKomidi leliwadi futsi ucinisekise kutsi labangenele tifundvo bayayivisisa indzima ledlalwa yICBP kanye nekuhlangana nemaKomidi Komidi emaWadi . Inkhundla yabona kutsi ite emandla ekwanta lekufisile , yatsatsa imiyalo ngaphandle , lusito netimali . Ngemnyaka wa-1992 , bacela iCorplan , inhlangano letimele ( NGO ) yemmango lese-East London , kubelekelela ngekubhala nekusebentisa lisu-ndlela lelifanele leLED . Baphumelela ekulweni netikhala letinyenti tebuchwepheshe nekuphatsa lobekukhona edolobheni nekutfola timali letivela kulamanye emave . Ungabe bonkhe labatawusebenta nalabaphetse kulomklamo sebaceceshiwe ngekusebentisa luhla lwetebulili ? Tjela babambi lichaza bafundze sifundvo ngalokwenteka lesingentasi , bese bayatilungiselela kuletigaba eluhlelweni lwekwehlulela , khuluma ngalokwenteka kusinye ngasinye sigaba ngekusebentisa emanotsi encenye 5.6 . Kwakha simo lesivumela kutibandzakanya kwemmango . Sibonelo , ngekuniketa ummango emagama nemininingwane yebantfu labangatsintsana nabo mayelana netinsita letinjengekutfutfwa kwetibi , imitfolamphilo kanye nemagama etikhulu lokucondziswa kuto letikhalo . Loku kutsatsa cishe li-awa nelicembu lelisembili lelihlanganisele lebelihlala kuleliwadi lokungenani iminyaka lelishumi . Lenjwayelo ngekwehlukana kutebululi itawubhebhetseleka . Kungalingani kwemisebenti emkhatsini kwalabadvuna nalabasikati , kunganakwa . Loku kutawenta kutsi imiphumela yalemiklamo ingabi ngulemihle . Ingcikitsi lesolomane ivela kuloluhlelo ngukutsi kutiphendvulela kumele kuciniswe . Sive sidzinga kucaciselwa kutsi ngubani lobukene nani . Kumele kube netinhlelo tekutsi bonkhe baholi batiphendvulele emmangweni ngekutiphatsa kwabo . Ngesikhatsi semhlangano wonkhe , cela lilunga linye kulinye ngalinye licembu liphendvule munye wemibuto , uma emacembu angetulu kwa-3 , emacembu lasalako kumele angete tintfo letingakavetwa ngaphambilini . EmaKomidi eLiwadi amele inshisakalo lehlukene nemacembu . Sibonelo , lamanye emalunga angamela emacembu alabakhokhela intselo , lamanye licembu labomake , lamanye tinhlangano tentfutfuko lamanye tinhlangano temabhizinisi . Ngakulesinye sikhatsi emaKomidi eLiwadi kumele asebente kanye kanye kanye kwenta siciniseko kutsi imibono yemmango inenkhundla yetinkhulumo nekutsi imibono yabo iyalalelwa ngendlela leletsa inzuzo emmangweni . Kungenteka kungakhonakali kuphendvula tonkhe tidzingo , kepha ngayo yonkhe imetamo , emaKomidi eLiwadi kumele afune umphumela lofanele kakhulu nalonenzuzo kummango . EmaKomidi eLiwadi angatitfola asesimeni lesingagcinela ekuhishaneni nelinyenti lalabatsintsekako kuhulumende labasebenta nabo , kuba nemakhono ladzingekako kucedza nobe kusombulula nobe kunciphisa kushayisana kutawubasita ekwenteni imisebenti yabo . Luhlaka lwenchubomgomo lwetama kukhutsata imimango lekhutsele naletibandzakanya ekuphatfweni kwentfutfuko yayo , lefuna emalungelo ayo ilandzele netibopho tayo , ifake sandla kutakhiwo tekuphatsa emazingene lehlukene , ezingeni leliWadi nelamasipala . Linyenti labomasipala lakhe tinchubomgomo , tihlaka tabo temtsetfo , wemaKomidi emaWadi kubomasipala babo . Tinchubomgomo tinika umtsetfo wekusungula , wemsebenti nekusebenta KwemaKomidi emaWadikumasipala tiphindze tinikete tinchazelo leticace kahle tetinhlelo netinchubo letitawusita emaKomidi emaWadi ikutsi asebente ngalokuyimphumelelo . Tinchubomgomo kumele tiguculwe ngobe masipala ngamunye wehlukile futsi kumele wetame kubeka tinchubomgomo letifanele tidzingo tawo kute bakwati kwetfulela imimango yabo tinsita ngalokuyimphumelelo . HULUMENDE WASEKHAYA UTSATFWA NJENGE sigaba sahulumende lesisondzele kakhulu kubantfu . Kufaka ekhatsi ummango ekukhombeni tidzingo nasekwakheni tinchubomgomo netinhlelo yindlela lephumelelisako ekuphendvuleni tidzingo temmango . Njengoba kungeke sekwenteke kutsi sonkhe sakhamiti sente umsebenti , EmaKomidi eLiwadi abekwe njenge sakhiwo sekuletsa kuchumana . Kepha , tinchubo tekuchumana kumele tenteke ngendlela lehlelekile . Lesahluko sibuketa indzima yemaKomidi eLiwadi kuletinchubo yekwenta tincumo temkhandlu nekutsi bayifeza njani indzima yabo ekwenteni umkhandlu utiphendvulele ekusebenteni nasekuphendvuleni tidzingo temmango . Emakhansela eliwadi akhetselwa kungena kumkhandlu wamasipala bavoti lababhaliswe ewadini , ngeluhlelo lwekumeleka ngalokulinganako lwelicembu , lawa ngemakhansela e-PR , nobe ngemakhansela ewadi . Emakhansela eLiwadi angamela licembu lepolitiki leliphikisako nobe batimele nobe labamele licembu lelinenshisakalo , njengenhlangano yalabakhokhela umtselo . Indlela yeCBP iniketa emaKomidi emaWadi ngenchubo yekuhlelela neluhlelo lwekusebentisa olucacisa tindzima nemitfwalo yawo . Aneluhlu lwakokutawentiwa - Lisu leliwadi - kantsi kusetjentiswa nekulandzelelwa kwekucutjungulwa kweLisu leliwadi kubaniketa indzima lechubekako umnyaka wonkhe . Khansela weliwadi nguye sihlalo weliKomidi leliWadi . Angendlulisela umsebenti wekuba ngusihlalo wemhlangano kukhansela lokhetfwe ngalokulinganako nobe kunome nguliphi lilunga leliKomidi LeliWadi . IBatho Pele iyindlela yekutiphatsa kwemuntfu emkhatsini kwalabanye , kulungela kuvuma emalungelo netidzingo tabo kanye nekutimisela kubasita ekufakeni sandla etimphilweni tabo . IBatho Pele kutibophetela kulabanye bantfu lokuveta lutsandvo lwebuntfu lweminyaka . Kusebenta njengesikhungo sekugcugcutela kushikashika kwemmango , ikakhulukati ngaphasi kwenchubo ye-IDP kanye nenchubo yeliphakelotimali wamasipala . EmaKomidi eLiwadi akatsikameti kusebenta kwemkhandlu , loku kufaka ekhatsi kunganiketi umyaleto etisebentini letisebenta kwenta tincumo tenchubomgomo yemkhandlu . Tikhundla-msebenti titawuhukana kuye ngekutsi lelo khansela lidzingeni . I-IDP ibekelwe kusita Masipala kutsi abhekane netidzingo letimcoka kakhulu temmango . Kumele iphindze ifake ekhatsi tinsita letikhona kuMasipala . Kulibangisa emsebentini lonesitfunti wawo wonkhe umuntfu , lokuhamba embili kwesikhashana kumele kwenyuse imisebenti kuphindze kukhutsate kungena kwebantfu labasha emisebentini , kube kunaka kuvinjelwa kuntjintjwa nobe kuncishiswa kwetimo tekusebenta letikhona njenganyalo . Lamanye ematfuba emsebenti ngete akwati kwenta bantfu ngamunye kutsi baphile imphilo labayifisako ngekushesha . Kute kutfutfukiswe imphilo lesimeme , kubalulekile kutsi umuntfu ngamunye nobe imindeni , kungabukwa liholo lebalitfolako , bakwati kufinyelela tinhlelo letinjengemfundvo lesezingeni , temphilo nobe tekutfutsa temmango . Kubalulekile futsi kutsi umuntfu lolahlekelwa ngumsebenti wakhe akwati kutfola umsebenti etinhlelweni temsebenti wahulumende nobe etinhlelweni temsebenti letisingetfwe tinhlangano temmango . Ngaletindlela , inchubomgomo yesive kanye netento tesive teleka umsebenti wemuntfu ngamunye emkhakheni wetisebenti , tiphindze tinike imphilo lesimeme kulabasebentako labaphuyile . Kuchumana yinchubo lematima ngoba ifaka ekhatsi bantfu labanetimondzawo letehlukene . Ngakoke , simo sekuchumana sibalulekile . Kuchumana kufaka ekhatsi tinhlangotsi letinyenti letehlukene . Kuchumana kunetincenye letinyenti njenge kukhuluma , kubhala , kucocisana kanye nekulalela . LiKomidi leliWadi lingaphakamisa lizinga lentfutfuko yemnotfo wemmango ngekutsi yatise ummango njalonjalo ngemisebenti lesunguliwe kanye namatfuba lakhona . Lingabikela emakhansela ngetinkinga letihlangana nato takhamuti letifuna kucala emabhizinisi lamancane . Kuhlela lokutinte eMmangweni kubukelele emmangweni nemandla / ematfuba kunetinkinga . Loku kusho kutsi emasu atfutfukiselwa imiphumela lengubocalangaye bemmango , hhayi tinkinga letingubocalangaye bawo . Siphakamisomtsetfo siphawula tinkhundla ' letitawuvumela tinhlangano letihlelekile kutsi tisungule tinchubomgomo futsi / nobe tibe neligalelo ekusukunyisweni kwenchubomgomo , kanye nekubandzakanyeka ekulandzeleni nasekuhloleni kanye nasekuhlanganiseni uliphakelotimali lonekubandzakanya lohlose ekuhlanganiseni bocalangaye bemmango macondzana nekutjalwa kwetimali ' . Kulesigaba lesi umehluleli uyatetfula abeke nemitsetfo letawusetjentiswa . Kusebenta nekuhlola - leli lizinga lapho umklamo wentiwa khona ngempelampela futsi kuphindze kwentiwe luhlolo loluphindzaphindziwe nekuhlela kabusha kute kucinisekiswe kutsi kuba neMphumelelo . Emakhansela eliwadi ababosihlalo semihlangano yeKomidi yeLiwadi , baphindze babite imihlangano yemmango . Emakhansela ahlanganisa ummango nemkhandlu , aphindze atiphendvulele emawadini awo . EmaKomidi eLiwadi aletsa kuchumana emkhatsini kwemmango kanye nelikhansela . Kwenta siciniseko sekutibandzakanya lokusezingeni lelisetulu nenchubekela phambili yekufika esisombululweni , umehluleli kumele ahlole kuguculeka kwangasinye sikhundla semacembu : ancume kulandzelana kwekunaka letindzaba , ancume kutsi iyadzingeka yini imihlangano leyehlukene nemehluleli ; acondzane nentsandvo yangalinye licembu netifiso , hhayi sikhundla ( loku , sigaba lebasitsatsako ) ; akhicite tonkhe tindlela letingaba khona atibhale ; akhutsate kuhlanganisa nekusebentisana , sibonelo : kusungula umtfolamphilo wekuchubekisa phambili netindlu tangasese erenkini yemakhumbi kuphela , bese i-IDP lelandzelako ifake ekhatsi ematafula alabatsengisako nemtfolamphilo lophelele ; akhele etindzaweni tekuvumelana . Khumbula kutsi lisu lelibhalwe ngelulwimi lunye kuphela litawufinyelela kubafundzi liphindze isetjentiswe bantfu labalinganisiwe emmangweni . Tinhlelo temnyaka tiyincenye lemcoka emphilweni yeMakomidi eLiwadi . Tisebenta njengesibuyeketo setintfo letiphambili letibekiwe , tinike imininingwane yalokufiswa kwentiwa yikomidi nekutsi loku kutwentiwa njani . Tiniketa indlela yekuhlola kutsi tinjongo lebetihleliwe tifezekile yini . Lenye inzuzo lebalulekile yetinhlelo temawadi kutsi ngemathulusi ekubika , lokwentiwe ngayinye-ngayinye inyanga kungakalwa ngeluhlelo lwemsebenti . Sinyatselo 4 - Ngabe yini lesifuna kuyizuza ? Sihlalo utawuhola umhlangano ngekulandzela luhla lwetindzaba lolwakhiwe bafundzi . Kwenta sibonelo : 54 bantfu babandzakanyeka kunchubo yekuhlela . Emacembu bekafaka ekhatsi labasebentako - labasetimbonini nasemahhovisi , labatisebentako , labangasebenti , bomake labangakashadi kanye nebantfwana . Lilungu leliKomidi leliwadi , Nkst Mofolo kanye nekhansela yendzawo , Nkst Smith , bebakhona kuyo yonkhe imihlangano . Bachubisifundvo bekunguboMnu Jones naNkst Mpefu . UMnu Mars lovela ku-dplg naye bekakhona kantsi nemhleli wemadolobha uMnu M Zungu naye bekakhona . Luhlaka lwesihlahla limathebula lagcwaliswa ngulabo labalawula umklamo . Lawa mathebula aniketa luhlelo lwemklamo ngalokufinyetiwe . Lenchubo yekucedzelela luhlaka lwekwentiwa kwemisebenti ingabukeka ilikhuni , kodvwa iniketa lwatiso lolubalulekile futsi kuyadzingeka kutsi ivisiswe . Loku kubalulekile ekuphumeleleni kwemklamo . Ngaleso sikhatsi futsi luhlaka lwesihlahla lutawusita ekwakheni kucina kwesikhatsi lesidze nekufundza kwalabo labayincenye yemklamo . . . Tinchubo tekuphetsa umsebenti - ticinisekisa kutsi wonkhe umkhicito lobhekekile walomsebenti wesikhashana uyafezeka , utfole sishicilelo sekutsi sewuphetsiwe kubo bonkhe labaphatsekako , kukhombisa ngalokusemtsetfweni kuphetfwa kwalomsebenti ngekukhicita lwati nekulusakata , kucedzela nekugocota tivumelwano lokufaka ekhatsi kugocota tindzaba lebetisele . Umtsetfo welidolobha lohlongotiwe uyashicilelwa kutfola labangaphawula emmangweni . Ngekusinisekisa kutsi labafake sandla eluhlelweni lwe CBP bamelwa etehlakalweni te-IDP kusetjentiswa tinhlaka netinhlelo letiniketiwe tendlela ye-IDP lekhona lecuketfwe kumgodla longumhlahlandlela we-IDP ( kakhulukati Inkhundla Yalabamele i-IDP kanye Nematsimba Emiklamo ) . Ngayinye iKPI kumele ifake ekhatsi tinhloso tekusebenta . Imitsetfo iniketa letinyenti timphawu tetinhloso tekusebenta , ingasita emaKomidi eLiwadi uma ahlola tinhloso tekusebenta teKPI . Letimphawu tigcamisa bumcoka beliphakelomali lelikhona . Loku kwentiwa kutsi iPMS ayimi yodvwa . I-IDP kumele ibe yinkhomba yekubeka emaKPI . Umangabe i-KPI ibeka tinhloso letingeke tifezeke , itawehluleka kutenta . Kutfutfuka kwahulumende wasekhaya kugcizelela sidzingo sekubeka tintfo ebaleni , kutiphendvulela , kubonisana , kuchuba kutibandzakanya kanye nekusebentisana nemmango . Kubalulekile kutsi lisu libhalwe kahle khona kutorekhodwa umbono wemmango kucinisekisa kutsi lingasetjentiswa tiphatsimandla temazinga laphakeme kanye nalabanye baphakeli betinsita . Masipala kumele abonisane nemmango angakakhi tinkhomba tekusebenta , anike litfuba ummango kutsi utibandzakanye nenchubo yekubuyeketa . Nguloyo naloyo mklamo wehlukile , tinkinga lobukene nato atifanani . ngako-ke kute uphumelele kufanele wentiwe ngendlela levuma wona . Kumcoka futsi kutsi nakuhlelwa lomklamo , tebulili tibukwe kutsi tenetiseka ngalokulinganako ngaso sonkhe sikhatsi . Baniketa timphendvulo nekufaka sandla etinchubeni temkhandlu , kwenta siciniseko sekwetfulwa kwetinsita . Lona ngumsebenti lowentiwa lapho bantfu bahlala khona futsi wentiwa ngekuvakashela indzawo . Bachubisifundvo bahola litsimba lebatisi labavela emmangweni labacishe basitfupha . Kungatsatsa cishe li-awa kuya kuma-awa lamabili njengobe bantfu angeke babe nesikhatsi sekuhamba emabanga lamadze . Imiphumela - Kwaba yini imiphumela yendlela lowenta ngayo ? Etigodzini lapho bantfu babanyenti nobe bahlala bagcagcene , emakomidi lamancane angakhiwa kuye ngetikhundla-msebenti letikhona . NgaLeyo ndlela emaKomidi emaWadi angatfola letfuba lekusebenta ngalokujulile tindzaba temimango . Loku kungenta kuhlanganyela emkhatsini wemmango nemaKomidi emaWadi nakwentiwa tincumo kucine . Ummango weSeymour , bewuyincenye yemiklamo yentfutfuko leminyenti kusukela nga-1992 - lenemazinga lehlukene ekuphumelela . Lemikhulu imiklamo leyentiwa kusukela nga-1992 iyachazwa ngentasi . Noma ngabe kungasiyo yonkhe imiklamo lekhulisa umnontfo , kumele ibukwe ngekuletsa imisebenti , nelusito kubantfu labafise kucashwa nobe kucala umklamo wentfutfuko . Khumbula kutsi liphakelotimali lingadzinga kuba nemininingwane leminyenti noma lemincana kuye ngekutsi lentelwe bani . Labanikelako bangahle bangadzingi imininingwane lelinganako naleyo lengadzingwa licembu lemklamo . Letingenteka : Loku kuchaza kutsi sinato tindlela tekuhlolisisa ( lwati lolukhona , kwenteka ngesikhatsi , njll ) ; kutsi tingafezeka futsi tingasetjentiswa-lula bantfu . Bomasipala labanyenti abakhoni kumikisa kubantfu letinsita ngekwabo , loku kungenteka kube abanawo emandla ekwenta njalo nobe abanato timali tekukwenta . Bomasipala-ke kumele bafune tindlela tekumikisela bantfu letinsita . Bangasungula tindlela tekwakha likhono labo lekusebenta ngekucamba tinkaphani tabo tekumikisa linsita kubantfu nobe bakhe budlelwane bekubambisana naletinye tinhlangano nobe imimango . Umtsetfo weTakhiwo taMasipala , 1998 neMtsetfo weTinhlelo taMasipala , 2000 usekela Umtsetfo Sisekelo uphindze ukhombise bumcoka bekutibandzakanya , unike luhlaka lolusemtsetfweni lwekusungula eMaKomidi eLiwadi . Emalunga eKomidi yeLiwadi kumele atejwayete leMitsetfo . Sibonelo , Umtsetfo weTinhlelo taMasipala , 2000 uchaza tinhlelo tekubusa , njengekwakhiwa kweLuhlelo lweKutfutfukisa Lolubumbene ( loluchazwe ngenhla ) neTinhlelo Tekulawula Kusebenta . UMBUTO 4 Yini tindzawo letibalulekile temiphumela ( KRA ) ? EmaKomidi eLiwadi angelekelela emakomidi ngekuniketa lwati etihlokweni letitsite lakufanele khona . Kunesidzingo sekwenta ncono kuphumeleliswa kwaletindlela letibalwe ngenhla , nekuvisisa indlela yekuhwebelana lekhona nyalo . Ngetulu kwaloko , kudzingeka lokunye kugcizelela kute kwelekelelwe emabhizimisi lamancane , kugcugcutelwe hulumende nemkhakha wangasese kutsi banikete imisebenti timboni letincane kanye nekukhutsata kutfutfukiswa kwebaholi netisebenti leticeceshiwe letimnyama kanye nabomake . Umnotfo lokhula ngekushesha lonwebeleka emikhakheni lemisha utawuvula ematfuba etimboni talabamnyama kanye nemabhizimisi lamancane , utfutfukise kukhula lokuhlanganisa konkhe . INingizimu Afrika ayifaki sandla kuphela ekukhishweni kwegesi lengongi imvelo - iphindze ibe sengotini yemitselela yekugucuka kwesimo selitulu kutemphilo , kuphila , emanti nekudla , incenye yemtselela iwele kulabaphuyile , ikakhulukati kubomake nebantfwana . Njengobe kwetayela letingucuko , timboni nemakhaya kumele kunciphise umtselela wako longasimuhle kutemvelo . Loku kutawudzinga tingucuko letinkhulu endleleni yekuphila nekusebenta kwebantfu . UMTSETFO WABOHULUMENDE BASEKHAYA uye wasukunyiselwa kwenta kutsi iNingizimu Afrika ikhone kusebenta ngalokunemphumelelo macondzana nekwetfula tinsita letisisekelo kanye nasekwenteni ncono imphilo yetenhlalakahle netemnotfo yetakhamuti . Njengobe hulumende waSekhaya angumkhakha wahulumende lapho kwetfulwa kwetinsita kwenteka khona ezingeni lemmango , kubalulekile kucinisekisa kanye nekuvikela kwesekela nekubandzakanyeka kwemimango . Lesehluko sendlala imigomo netinchubomgomo tekuhlela lokutinte eMmangweni ( iCommunity based planning - iCBP ) . Babambi lichaza bakha imigca lemibili bayabukana . Munye umugca ubitwa nga A , bambambi lichaza kulolunye luhlangotsi lwemugca bangu Cela babambi lichaza bente bulingani nemuntfu locondzene nabo . Cela bonkhe bo-B kutsi baphume endlini . Kugcogcwa kwemininingwane yekwesekela kumalunga emmango , bachubisifundvo kanye nebameleli bemmango . Loku kungatsatsa emalanga lambalwa nobe kwenabele esikhatsini lesibanti , kepha kungadluli kushejuli lemisiwe . ICBP ilidlelandzawonye emkhatsini kwabo bonkhe badlalindzima . Kuntjintja kwesikhatsi lesidze ekuhwebelaneni nelutjalomali kwemave emhlaba nekumisa kabusha umnotfo wemhlaba kanye netembusave temave emhlaba . Lokuyinhloko kuletintfutfuko kuvela kweminotfo lekhula ngesivinini , ikakhulukati iShayina , iNdiya neBrazil . Cishe iminyakalikhulu lemitsatfu yekuphikisana , kungalingani emkhatsini wetive kuya ngekuncipha . Kutfutseleka emadolobheni nekwakhiwa kwetimboni eShayina naseNdiya kungenteka kugcine sidzingo semitfombolusito yemvelo sisetulu umnyakalishumi munye nobe ngetulu . Kuvela kwebasebentisi labanyenti emaveni lasatfutfuka kutakwenta ematfuba ayo yonkhe iminotfo ibe banti . Umzabalazo wekulwa nelubandlululo kwekucala nje bewumayelana nekwakhiwa kwemmango longabandlululi ngekwebuhlanga nalongabandlululi ngekwebulili , lapho bonkhe bantfu batakuba nemalungelo lalinganako . Ngaphandle kwenchubekelembili lesimeme kusukela nga-1994 , iNingizimu Afrika solomane ingummango lowehlukene , buhlanga busengibo lobehlukanisa kakhulu . Kubuka ngeluhlangotsi lunye kutebuhlanga nekwebuve kwandzile kantsi nekubandlululana kusachubeka . Tinhlaka tetikhungo talelive kanye netinkhambiso tato letibanti tetemnotfo netenhlalo tifake sandla ekuyeni ngekuncipha kwebuhlanga , kepha inchubekelembili leyisentiwe ayikeneli nobe ayikajuli ngalokwenele . Nakhona inchubekelembili yenta ncono timphilo tabomake ; kubandlululana , timongcondvo tekulawulwa kwabomake bobabe kanye nekungakwati kufinyelela emfundvweni lesezingeni kuyachubeka . Loluhlelo lubukana naletintfo ngalokugcwele , lube lubuka kutsi tintfo letihamba embili letinjengemfundvo nobe kutfutfukiswa kwetindzawo tasemakhaya kutakuba nemtselela lomkhulu kubomake labaphuyile . Luhlelo Lwekutfutfukisa Lwavelonkhe lutawucondzisa kuniketelwa kwemitfombolusito kuleminyakalishumi lemibili letako , kepha ngete lwancuma ngelwabiwomali lwemnyaka . Indlela lencono yekutfola imitfombolusito kute kwetfulwe loluhlelo kukhulisa umnotfo ngalokunonophako . Uma umnotfo ukhula ngemaphesenti lasihlanu ngemnyaka , imali lengeniswa nguhulumende kanye netinzuzo tetimboni tangasese titaba ngetulu kwalokuphindvwe kabili kuleminyaka lengema-20 letako . Kuhlanganisa kusabalala kwekungena kwemali kube sikhwama sinye sekwakha kabusha tendzawo . Kubandzakanyeka kwetakhamiti kuphindze kusite ekucinisekiseni kutsi hulumende uyatiphendvulela nekutsi wetfula tinsita ngendlela latfunywe ngayo . kuba takhamiti akugcini nje ngekukhetsa labatawumela ummango . Tikhulu temmango atikalindzeleki kutsi titsatsele takhamiti tincumo letincono uma ngabe takhamiti tingasho kutsi ngutiphi tidzingo tato . Takhamiti tikwati kancono letikudzingako kantsi kubalulekile kutsi tifake sandla ekuletseni tisombululo taletidzingo . Takhamiti kumele tisebente ngekubambisana nahulumende ekusiteni ngentfutfuko . Kulapho kungena khona EmaKomidi emaWadi njengobe adlala indzima lebalulekile ekuchubeni luhlelo lwekutibandzakanya kwemmango . Emakhansela kufanele ati kutsi yini lesebenta kahle kulabanye bomasipala lengasita nakasebenta namasipala wabo ekwakheni emakomidi emaWadi . Kutinikela lokuncono kwebaphatsi nebaholi betinhlelo nekusebentisana ekutfutfukiseni luphenyo nekulawulwa kweluphenyo . I-PMS yamasipala kumele ifake ekhatsi tintfo letikhonjwe ngumkhandlu , leticondzene ngco netindzawo letibalulekile tekusebenta tamasipala wawo . Emazinga ekubeleka alabamhlophe baseNingizimu Afrika acale kwehla ngasekupheleni kweminyaka yabo-1950 nabo-1960 , kantsi alabaMnyama acale kwehla ngasekupheleni kweminyaka yabo-1970 nasekucaleni kweminyaka yabo-1980 . Kuletihlangotsi totimbili , kwenyuka kwekutfutseleka kwebantfu etindzaweni tasemadolobheni kanye nemazinga emfundvo lancono kwaba tincumo letilandzelwako . Lamuhla , linani lebantfu baseNingizimu Afrika likhula ngeliphesenti linye ngemnyaka kantsi kubiketelwa kutsi nga-2030 litawukhula ngemaphesenti lali-0.5 ngemnyaka . EmaKomidi emaWadi aluhlakamsebenti lwenhlangano ( kanye netinhlangano tebabambimsuka ) futsi kumele amelelwe kusiGungu sekuMelela se-IDP kanye nakutsimba lekusebenta lelihambisanako le-IDP . Uma uva ngemagama latsi Luhlelo Lwekulawula Kusebenta kusho kutsini kuwe ? Kuphatsa ngekwentsadvo yelinyenti kudzinga kutibandzakanya ngekwentsandvo yelinyenti ngelivi lawo wonkhe ummango etinhlelweni tenchubomgomo netekuphatsa . Loku kudzinga kutsatfwa kwetincumo lokusebaleni kanye nendlela legcile kubantfu . Kuphindze kudzinge takhamiti letikwatiko kwenta tehlulelo , letifaka sandla etinkhulumiswaneni letinemtselela etimphulweni tabo nekwati ngetincabhayi letikhona emmangweni wato kanye nemakhono nelwati lwekutfola tisombululo taletincabhayi . Kutibandzakanya kuyincenye ledzingekako yekubusa lokuhle njengobe kuvumela kuhanjiswa kwelwati emkhatsini kwetakhamiti kanye nebaholi labakhetsiwe lokufaka ekhatsi kutiphendvulela . Kuphindze kwente takhamiti letitsintseke kakhulu ngenchubomgomo yemmango kutsi tibe nelivi letilibekako . Kwakha sakhiwonchanti lesitawungenisa igesi yemvelo leluketjeti kwenyuswe nekusetjentiswa kute kutfolwe indzawo lephakela ngegesi lapha ekhaya ( kufaka ekhatsi kuphenya ngemarisevu elukhetse lwemitheyini embhedeni welilahle ) kute kuhlukaniswe kuhlanganiswa kwemandla kuphindze kuncishiswe kukhishwa kwekhabhoni . Emacenjini enu khulumani ngetindlela lelitiko lokumele lisebentise ngato IBatho Pele kute kufezeke kwetfulwa kwetinsita ngendlela lehloswe nguhulumende . Ungatsatsi luhlangotsi - mela kutsi yonkhe imibono ivetwe kucala , ungabese uyawengeta wakakho . Lamanye emaphuzu emphilo yemmango ahambisana nesikhatsi semnyaka , njengemaphethini etifo , kusetjentiswa kwebasebenti , titungeletane tetekulima , kanye nekondleka . Lemisebenti lemibili lelandzelako ikwenta nconokwenta ncono kuvisiswa kwekuhambisana nesikhatsi semnyaka kanye nemikhuba yesikhatsi-dze . Ngekwenta lamaphethini nemikhuba labo labasezingeni lekuhlela ngalokubonakalako bayakhona kucombela tigameko letitsite bese balinganisa emasu nemachinga abo ngalokufanelekile . Incenye yebahlali baseNingizimu Afrika labahlala etindzaweni tasemakhaya yehle ngemaphesenti lali-10 kusukela nga-1994 . Lamuhla , cishe emaphesenti langema-60 ebantfu bahlala etindzaweni tasemadolobheni . Ngekuhambisana netinkhambiso temave emhlaba , kutfutseleka kwebantfu kusuka etindzaweni letikhashane nemadolobha baye emadolobheni kulindzeleke kutsi kuchubeke , kantsi nga-2030 cishe bantfu labangemaphesenti langema-70 batawube bahlala etindzaweni tasemadolobheni . IGauteng kanye nemadolobha lanjengaboThekwini neKapa amadolobha lakhula ngesivinini , lokunemtselela ekuhleleni nasekwetfulweni kwetinsitanchanti . Chaza kutsi sigaba sesibili sifaka ekhatsi luhlatiyo lolutibile kanye nekuhlanganiswa kwemininingwane legcogcwe kuSigaba 1 . EmaKPI abuyeketwa njalo ngemnyaka ngumasipala , njengencenye yenchubo yakhe yekubuyeketa kusebenta . Umangabe masipala agucula i-IDP kumele aphindze abuyekete emaKPI . Timphendvulo letibuya emmangweni , ngemaKomidi eLiwadi , kumele tibukisiswe umakubuyeketwa emaKPI . Ngalendlela lena iPMS ibonakala yetsenjwa ngummango . Kuhleleka ngelibalave kuphindze kunikete sitfombe semmango mayelana netindzaba tekuhleleka nekuma kwendzawo , tindzaba letitsintsa ticheme letehlukahlukene , imitfombolusito yemvelo , simondzawo sasemadolobheni kanye nekutikhetsela lokungahle kube khona kwekukwenta nconokwenta ncono simondzawo sabo sekuhlala . EmaKomidi emaWadi kudzingeka atejwayete lamathulusi kanye netindlela letingabasita kuhlela tekulingana kutebulili . Kwenta umbutfo wemaphoyisa ungabi ngumbutfo wetemphi . Sincumo sekwenta umbutfo wemaphoyisa ungabi ngumbutfo wetemphi , kusuka emlandvweni wekubulala ngesihluku , kube yinhloso yengucuko lehamba embili ngemuva kwa-1994 . Kubuyiselwa kwemaphoyisa njengembutfo wetemphi kwakamuva nje akumange kuletse kuhlonishwa kwemaphoyisa nobe emazinga lasetulu alababanjiwe . Kahle kahle lesimo sifake sandal eludlameni . Emaphoyisa kumele ungabi ngumbutfo wetemphi futsi uphatfwe njengembutfo loceceshiwe lovikela bahlali . Masipala wase ABC ulungiselela i-IDP . Likhansela leiwadi neLiKomidi leLiwadi selatise ummango kutsi umhlangano utawubanjwa mhlaka 20 Kholwane nga 7.00 pm ehholeni lelidolobha . Satiso sikhishwe emavikini lamabili lendlulile umhlangano ungakefiki nemaphuzu lamcoka latakuphakanyiswa emhlanganweni njengetintfo letimcoka ku-IDP . Emhlanganweni likhansela leliwadi liniketa sibuyeketo se-IDP , bese licela timphendvulo nalabafise kuphawula . Umhlangano uvumelane kutsi emacembu lanenshisakalo lefanako kumele ahlangane kukhuluma nge-IDP nebalandzeli babo bese ayabuya evikini lelilandzelako netimphendvulo tabo . Lusuku nesikhatsi kuvunyelwana ngako emhlanganweni . Umtsetfo utsi emaKPI kumele akalwe , afanele , acondze angagegi . Asebenta etigungwini tekuphatsa nasetisebentini tamasipala , sonkhe sakhiwo samasipala nebetfuli tinsita labanetivumelwano namasipala . Bantfu babandzakanyeka ngekutjelwa loko lokuncunyiwe nobe losekuvele kwentekile . Kufaka ekhatsi timemetelo tacala-linye ngalabo labengamele nobe labaphetse umklamo ngaphandle kwekulalela imiva nemibono yebantfu . Nanobe inchubo yekuhlela isukunyiswa futsi ihlelenjiswa ngumasipala , CICBP ilidlelandzawonye emkhatsini kwewadi namasipala . Bunikati belisu busewadini , lemelwe liKomidi leWadi . Masipala uhlomisa emakhansela akhe emawadi kanye nemakomidi kutsi ahlelembise inchubo yekuhlela letawenta kutsi lelo nalelo komidi litfole ligunya ngesikhatsi sekusebenta kwalo ehhovisi . Kuphawula nekucondzanisa ngetisombululo tetidzingo nabocalangaye bemmango kusita emakhansela nemaKomidi emaWadi ekwenteni imisebenti yawo . Kuhlela lokutinte emmangweni kungafaka ligalelo kunchubo yekuhlelela kutfutfukisa lokuhlanganisele . UMTSETFO WETAKHIWO TAMASIPALA , 1998 udzinga kutsi bomasipala babuyekete konkhe kusebenta kwamasipala njalo ngemnyaka . Sehluko 6 seMtsetfo weTinhlelo taMasipala , 2000 uniketa luhlaka lwemtsetfo lwekulawula kusebenta kubomasipala . Kulawula kusebenta kumele kube yincenye yeLuhlelo lweKutfutfukisa Lolubumbene . Kulalelwa kweliphakelo-timali kwenta siciniseko kutsi tidzingo teMFMA , 2003 tiyahlangabetwa mayelana nekutibandzakanya kwemmango enchubeni yekuphakela timali . Kulalelwa kweliphakelo-timali kwamasipala kuvumela eMakomidi eLiwadi kutsi atibandzakanye entfutfukweni yeliphakelo-timali lamasipala . Kumcoka ngani kutsi emaKomidi Emawadi acondze aphindze asebentise lenchubo ? Kulandzelela imibiko yekwetfulwa kwetinsita - iMFMA idzinga kutsi bomasipala babhale imibiko ngenchubo yekwetfulwa kwetinsita etindzaweni tabo . Lemibiko iniketa imimango litfuba lekulandzelela kutfutfuka . Ngesikhatsi setinkhulumo temcombelelo timali , emakhansela , ngelusito lweMaKomidi eLiwadi , kumele ayale ummango kutsi tincumo letibalulekile titakuba nayiphi imiphumela kubo . Kunesidzingo lesibalulekile sahulumende welubambiswano kanye nekubambisana kwetimboni . Lemibandzela yakhelwe kwenta siciniseko sendzawo yetigungu levumela kwetfulwa kwetakhiwonchanti tamasipala , letakhela etingungwini indlela yekubambisana . Yini lengentiwa sive ngaloku , nekutsi wena njengelilunga lekomidi yeliWadi ungentanjani ? Tinhlelo letibutsakatsaka , letingasebenti kahle tenta kube matima kwenta umsebenti , umphumela lohlala uba khona njalo ngewekutsi akekho lotiphendvulelako . Loluhlelo lubeka sibonelo saloko lokwenteka ngesikhatsi emanti edolobheni lelitsite atfolakale anganatseki . Betindzaba bagceka iNdvuna Yetemanti . Ummango ugceka sodolobha . Sodolobha ugceka inhloko yesikhungo setemanti . Inhloko yesikhungo setemanti igceka njiniyela wemisebenti . Njiniyela utsi lwabiwomali lwekulungisa lucanyuliwe kuleminyaka lemitsatfu leyengcile kantsi nyalo emanti awanatseki . Inhloko yetetimali kumasipala itsi lwabiwomali lwancanyulwa ngobe tindleko tetisebenti tente kwacinana imali yekulungisa . Sodolobha ubeka kutsi luhlelo lwemiholo kucociswana ngalo ezingeni lwavelonkhe lokwentiwa yiNhlangano Yabohulumende Basekhaya baseNingizimu Afrika . Inhlangano itsi bomasipala bangatikhipha kuletivumelwano uma ngabe bayehluleka ngekwetimali njalo njalo njalo . Baholi bemmango bamele bahlali etindzabeni letibatsintsa kakhulu kantsi kumele tinakwe kakhulu . Labaholi babukene nekucinisekisa kutsi kugcekwa nekushuca kwentiwa ngesitfunti nangekukhombisa kukhula engcondvweni . Nanobe baholi bemmango ngalesinye sikhatsi bamela tinshisekelo letimbalwa lencane emmangweni lobanti nalowehlukene , kepha bayincenye lebalulekile yentsandvo yelinyenti lekhutsele lehlanganisa bantfu entfutfukweni yabo . Kuvumelana nobe indlela lesukela enshisakalweni - lendlela lena itsatsa kushayisana njengencenye yemvelo yebudlelwane bebantfu . Lendlela lena ayibuki kutsi ngubani ' lokahle ' ' nalonemaphutsa ' esimeni sekuhishana , kepha itfola sisombululo lesitawuletsa inzuzo kuwo onkhe emacembu . Lendlela lena ilwela simo sewin / win . Isebentisa kusombulula tinkinga , nekucabanga , nekubuka indlela yekusombulula kuhishana leholela emphumeleni lomuhle wabo bonkhe . Cinisekisa kutsi tinhlangotsi tetenhlalakahle , tetemnotfo , tetesikhungo netesimondzawo tendlaliwe . Inhlosonchanti yahulumende yekutfutfukisa hulumende wasekhaya kwakha masipala losimeme kutetimali lolungiselelwe kuhlangabetana netidzingo tetenhlalakahle , ttemnotfo kanye netidzingonchanti tebantfu bakhe ngendlela lebandzakanyako nalesimeme . Indzima yekutfutfukisa yahulumende wasekhaya ifakwe yaciniswa kuMtsetfosisekelo kanye nemiculu yetinchubomgomo nemitsetfo , lokukhulunywe ngako kulesehluko . Ngekubona kwaNkosi bantfu balapha esabelweni bayatatisa abacabangelani . Banfu basesabelweni nabo babona kutsi Umnu Nkosi unelunya futsi uyatitisa . Imihlangano yemmango - Leti tinkhundla letibalulekile tekuhlephulelana imibono nelwati . Imikhandlu ingabita umhlangano wemmango ngetintfo letitsite , nobe kwetfula umbiko ngemphumela wemhlangano nobe umcimbi ; kubika umbiko lojwayelekile ngetikhatsi letibekiwe ngemihlangano yemkhandlu nemihlangano yemaKomidi eLiwadi , ngakulolunye luhlangotsi , likhansela leliwadi , ngekumelela liKomidi leLiwadi , lingawubita umhlangano wekunika umbiko ummango kutfola imibono yetakhamiti ngeludzaba lolutsite . Umklamo ngunoma nguyiphi intfo yekutfutfukisa tinsita noma intfo ngesikhatsi lesitsite lesibekiwe . Kufanele ingete kubaluleka noma iletse ingucuko leyakhako ngandlela tsite . Umklamo unesikhatsi lesincane lobekelwe sona , awusiyo intfo letawuhlala ichubeka yenteka njalo , uneliphakelo lolutsite lwemali futsi uvamise kuba yintfo leyenteka kanye vo . Hulumende ngete akwati kumela tidzingo tato tonkhe takhamiti . Nanobe Nanobe Nanobe bantfu baya kuyewuvotela licembu labalitsandzako kute limele tifiso tabo , bantfu abafani , futsi banetidzingo letingafani . Nanobe Nanobe Nanobe hulumende angetama kanjani akusimalula kufinyelela kuto tonkhe takhamiti . Kubandzakanyeka kwetakhamiti kungasita kuvala ligebe njengobe ummango ungasita ekugcwaliseni imitamo yahulumende ngemitamo yabo kantsi lendlela yenta livi labo liye embili . Ngulesizatfu lesente kusungulwe EmaKomidi emaWadi kute atewusita hulumende ekucinisekiseni kutsi takhamiti tifaka sandla etincumeni letitintsako . Umtsetfo weMalungelo ufaka ekhatsi emalungelo emnotfo nenhlalakahle , ekuhlala endzaweni lehlobile , kutfola indzawo leyanele yekulala , kuba dvute netinsita temtfolamphilo , kudla lokwenele , nemanti . Kuta emihlanganweni yemkhandlu - lungisa lubhaliso lwemalunga eKomidi yeLiwadi , niketa ngalinye lilunga umhlangano lotsite latawuhambela . Sehluko 1 kanye neSehluko 4 tiniketela ngemininingwane yetinhlobo tebachubisifundvo lababandzakanyekako ekutfutfukisweni kweMvila-balave weCBP kanye nebabambimsuka lokumele kuchunyanwe nabo . Bahlali labakhutsele nekukhutsala kutenhlalo kuyadzingeka kuntsandvo yelinyenti nasentfutfukweni kute igcame . Umbuso ngete wamela bantfu kalula nje - kumele ente ngekuhlanganyela nebantfu , kusebenta ngekubambisana naletinye tikhungo kuniketa ematfuba ekuchubekela embili ayo yonkhe imimango . Kuba nesiciniseko kutsi imibono yemmango iyafakwa elushinjtweni . EmaKPI abuyeketwe ngumasipala njalo ngamnyaka njengeluhlelo lwekubuyeketa kusebenta kantsi uma masipala achibiyela i-IDP yakhe kumele futsi kubuyeketwe nemaKPI akhe . Loluhlelo lucinisekisa kutiphendvulelaluphindze lukhutsate kuvumelana emkhatsini kwemmango kanye nemkhandlu . Luphindze lusebentele kucinisekisa kutsi i-PMS ibonwa ngummango njengentfo lekholekako . Lokukhishwa sikhutsa kanye nalamanye emagesi lonakalisa imvelo agucula simo selitulu semhlaba , abange tindleko letinkhulu leticindzetelako letitawugcina tinemtselela longasimuhle kulabaphuyile . Emazinga ekushisa lenyukako , imvula lengani kahle kanye netehlakalo tetimo telitulu letenteka ngalokwecile kungenteka tibe nemtselela lomkhulu e-Afrika , kwandze netifo letibangwa kushisa kukhule nekulahlekelwa ( bantfu nemali ) lokubangwa somiso kanye netikhukhula . Kugucuka kwesimo selitulu kunemandla ekunciphisa umkhicito wekudla nekuba khona kwemanti , lokunemphumela wekutfutseleka kwebantfu kanye nemazinga ekungcubutana . Kumsebenti lolandzelako emalunga emmango aphakamisa umncamulajucu wesikhatsi lovumbulula umlandvo walommango . Ngekuphawula emaphethini nemikhuba lephindzaphindzekako lomsebenti kumele utibise kuvisisa kwemmango mayelana nesimo sawo futsi kuwente ucabange mayelana nekuphumelela kwekungenelela kwangaphambilini . Bhala lemibuto lelandzelako eshadini leliphendvulekako bese labangenele tifundvo bayicedzela emacenjini abo lamancane basebentisa imininingwane leemanotsini esifundvo . Imikhakha wahulumende newangasese ingadlala indzima lebalulekile ekwakheni sakhiwonchanti , kufaka ekhatsi sakhiwonchanti lesikhulu . Ekucaleni kwekuhhohloka kwemnotfo kwanga-2009 , umkhakha wangasese bewungabata kusisa encenyeni yemali lengenako enzuzweni lenkhulu kutemnotfo . Ngalokunjalo , umkhakha wahulumende uvune kusetjentiswa endzaweni yekusisa ngalokwecile . Kuvuma loku , hulumende umemetele kugucuka ekwakhekeni kwemali lecitfwako yelutjalomali , umgomo lohamba embili lodzingekako ekucedzeni lokuma ndzawonye . Ngekuhamba kwesikhatsi , lutjalomali lwemkhakha wahulumende lungasita kugcwala elutjalwenimali lwangasese . Masipala wendzawo kuWadi ABC unephosita lenkhulu lebala tinhlelo latetfulako . UMnu . Mamba kamuva nje ute kutewuhlala kulomasipala uya ehhovisi kuyewukhonona kutsi tibane esitaladini sakhe atikhanyi ngalokwenele . Utjelwa kutsi kumele abonge nekutsi unendlu nekuba nendlu . Lamacembu etenhlalakahle kumele abe aphawulwe ngesikhatsi sekuhlelela kwangaphambilini aphindze acinisekiswa emhlanganweni wekwetfula emmangweni , kepha emacembu langetiwe angaphawulwa ngesikhatsi sekuhlela . Fundza lesimo wakhe umbono nemgomo wamasipala wakho ulungise inkhombandlela yekudlala indzima kwemmango kutsi ufeze lombono . Kufanele kubhalwe luhla lwetihloko tetindzaba letitawukhulunywa emhlanganweni . Loku ngumsebenti wasihlalo welibandla lekhansela bakanye namabhalane . Kusebentisa netinhlaka tembuso letifanele kute kubikwe ngenchubekelembili yetinjongo . I-MFMA , 2003 idzinga kutsi bomasipala bakhiphe imibiko yenchubo yekwetfulwa kwetinsita etindzaweni tabo . Lemibiko inika imimango emandla ekulandzelela intfutfuko . Tindzawo tasemakhaya tiletsa tinsayeya letitsite . Ngetulu kwalokukodvwa kulokutsatfu webantfu baseNingizimu Afrika bahlala etindzaweni lebetatiwa ngekutsi " tabelo " , kantsi incenye lenkhulu yalabantfu incishwe ematfuba . Kudzingeka tinchubomgomo kute emakhaya lakuletindzawo aletfwe kutemnotfo lomkhulu . Kunetindzawo tasemakhaya , kepha , lapho kuchumana kwetekutfutsa kukuhle khona nalapho kuminyana kwenteka khona ngekungabikho kwekuphatfwa kahle kusetjentiswa kwemhlaba kanye nekuphatfwa kwetindzawo tasemadolobheni . Loku kudzinga kungenelela lokuphutfumako . Bantfu babandzakanyeka ngekugalela ngemitfombolusito , sibonelo , kusebenta ngekulangatelela kutsi utfole kudla , imali lengukheshe nobe letinye tibonelelo letiphatsekako . INingizimu Afrika ibe nenchubekelembili lemangalisako ngesikhatsi igucuka isuka embusweni welubandlululo iya embusweni wentsandvo yelinyenti . Lengucuko kube ngulenekuthula nanoma nje lelive linemlandvo wekungcubutana lokuneludlame kanye nekwemukwa imphahla . Kucecesheka lokufanele : Litsimba lebantfu lababili ngeliwadi kumele baceceshwe kutsi batawusebenta ngekubambisana neliKomidi leliwadi laSekhaya . Ngekuya ngekwelwatinchanti sangaphambilini nemakhono ekuhlelembiseni , luhlelo lwekucecesha lungatsatsa tinsuku letingu-15 . Ngekwetibalo letisuselwe eluphenyweni , bafati benta umsebenti longema-67% kwemsebenti lowentiwa mhlaba wonkhe , Kantsi bahola 10% kwemiholo yonkhe yemhlaba ekhulwinime . Rekhoda ngekubhala lokuvunyelwene ; onkhe emacembu akasayinde ; yetfula matfupha enkhundleni yebameli be-IDP . Sakhiwonchanti asikabaluleki kuphela ekukhuleni kwemnotfo lokushesha nasekwenyukeni kwematfuba emisebenti . Kutfutfukisa kukhula lokuhlanganisa konkhe , kunike bahlali tindlela tekwenta ncono timphilo tabo kuphindze kwenyuse nemiholo yabo . Sakhiwonchanti sibalulekile ekutfutfukeni . Umtselela wekugucuka kwesimo selitulu ubanti emhlabeni kantsi kumele kutfolakale tisombululo temhlaba ngekubuka lokufanele etimeni tesigodzi netavelonkhe . Umsebentil Tsatsisa kuMtsetfosisekelo , tfola letigaba tawo letiphatselene nekutfutfukiswa kwahuluende welinyenti , bese uyachaza kutsi sigaba ngasinye siwutfutfukisa njani umkhankhaso wekubusa ngelinyenti . Kutiphendvulela emabhizimisini ahulumende kwentiwe kwangacaci ngeluhlelo lwekucasha lolunkimbitekile , lolungakacaci encenye lolunekungenelela kwetembusave lokungadzingeki . Siphakamisa kucaciswa kwetindlela tekutiphendvulela ngekutfutfukisa kutfunywa kwetinshisekelo tesive lokubeka kutsi emabhizimisi ahulumende kumele asisebentele kanjani sive , kucinisekisa kutsi tinhlelo tekucasha tinguletifanele naletingagodli , kutfutfukisa kusebentisana emkhatsini wenchubomgomo kanye nemkhakha webaniyo bemasheya . Lokubaluleka lokubili kutidzingo lekumele tihambe embili kute kube nemphumelelo yentfutfuko kuvelonkhe . Kwenta iNingizimu Afrika ibumbane kubalulekile ekufakeni ligalelo eluhlelweni lwekunciphisa buphuya nekungalingani nasekutfoleni umphumela locondzile wekunciphisa buphuya . Kute kwakhiwe ummango lobumbene , iNingizimu Afrika idzinga kunciphisa buphuya nekungalingani ngekwandzisa ematfuba nemisebenti ngekuhlanganisa wonkhe umuntfu kutemnotfo , imfundvo nemakhono , netindlela leticondzile tekulungisa kwangaphambili ; kukhutsata kuhloniphana nekuhlanganisa wonkhe ngekulandzela ticondziso teMtsetfosisekelo tekutsi iNingizimu Afrika yawo wonkhe lohlala kuyo , nekutsi bonkhe bayalingana embi kwemtsetfo ; nekujulisa kubonga kwemisebenti netibopho tetakhamiti ekusitaneni bodvwana . Lamshejuli etindleko aniketa kuhlolwa kwekusetjentiswa kwetimali ( kufaka ekhatsi iminikelo yelabatibandzakanyako labahlukene ) , kanye nebuka bubanti Betivumelwano Tekuniketwa Kwetimali . Kuhlatiya ngetebulili lithulusi lekutfola umehluko emkhatsini webesifazane nebesilisa mayelana ne misebenti letsite , timo , tidzingo , kufinyelela ne kuphatsa iminotfo , kanye nekufinyelela kutinzuzo tentfutfuko nekwenta tincumo . Luphenya kabanti kuchumana emkhatsini waloku kanye ne tekuphila , temnotfo , tembusave kanye netendalo . Kuhlatiya ngetebulili kufaka ekhatsi kubutsa lwati ngekuhlelwa kwetebulili kanye netintfo sive lesingakhululeki ngato letiphetselene netebulili . Kuhlatiya ngetebulili kusinyatselo sekucala nakwentiwa luhlelo lwetintfo bantfu labangakhululeki ngato kutebulili kute kutfutfukiswe kulingana ngetebulili . Yenta lomsebenti ngentasi nebabambi lichaza , chuba inkhulumo lesuselwa kulemibuto . Kutibandzakanya kwemmango akufuneki kubonakale shengatsi nguwo wodvwa umgomo . Takhamiti kudzingeka tibonakale njenge ' bammeli labakhutsalele ingucuko nentfutfuko ' . Ngekutibandzakanya nekuhlela nekwenta intfutfuko , bantfu baba netisombululo ngekwabo , ngako-ke batfutfukisa kwetfulwa kwetinsita netakhiwonchanti . Babambilichaza baphendvule imibuto lengephasi kwesigaba lebaniketiwe . Tinkhomba letibalulekile tekusebenta tisita hulumende wasekhaya netakhamiti kukala letikuzuzile . Ema-KPI yimigomo ' leyentakalako ' nalekalekako , masipala lavumelane kutsi angakhona kuyizuza ngesikhatsi lesibekiwe . Tisita kwatisa nekukala kutsi ngabe umkhandlu namasipala bakhone kangakanani kwetfula ngekusho kwetinhlelo letichazwe ku-IDP , ngaloku takhamiti tiyakhona kwenta masipala atiphendvulele . Loluhlaka lwekwentiwa kwemisebenti luniketa sisekelo sekwentiwa kwetigontileka ngekubeka kucace tinhloso letilindzelekile . Luphindze luncedze kubona lizinga lekusebenta nekuphendvula kwebalawuli bemklamo nalabanye labadlale indzima . Bachubisifundvo kumele batilungiselele mayelana nekubukana nekubika mayelana neliphakelotimali wekutikhetsela lovela kumkhandlu . Ummango ungativa ukhatsatekile uma labanye bocalangaye labasembili bangakakhetselwa kuniketwa kwesekelwa ngetimali . Ngabe tinsita letikhona tiyafinyelela kulamacophelo ? Ngutiphi tinsuku letibekelwe tekucedza ngato imisebenti ? Kwati ngekuhlangana kwe ikhansela : Tincumo ngetindzaba temimango tijutjwa emihlanganweni yekhansela . Imimango ingabuta kutsi lemihlangano yenteka nini kutse batoyingenela . Umtsetfosivivinyo weTibopho , lowentiwe Litiko Letemfundvo Lesisekelo kanye nalabanye kumele wentiwe watiwe , kugcugcutela wonkhe umuntfu kutsi aphile ngekulandzela imigomo yeMtsetfosisekelo . Uyindvodza . Usebenta edolobheni lelincane . Umkakho ulima tibhidvo . Umngani wakho utsi angasita kutsengisa letibhidvo edolobheni lelikhulu ngemali lencono . Uyalufuna lolusito lwakhe ngoba uyayidzinga lemali kutsenga insudu lotayigcoka emhlanganweni lotako wamasipala . Khomba licembu lelifanelekile , indzawo yemklamo , utawucala nini , uphele nini , ngubani lotawube ayiphetse , itawubita malini nekutsi imali itawubuya kuphi . Ngetulu kwaloko , emagoli netinkhomba tiyakhiwa kukala umsebenti nengucuko leletfwa ngumklamo . Kuniketelwa kwetindlu kumele kuhlanganise neticelo tekusitwa ngetimali , kukhulimsana lokusemtsetfweni kanye nekwetfulwa kwetindlu emgodleni munye , ngaloko kusitakale likhasimende ekufinyeleleni etinhlelweni ngalokuphelele kungabi ngeticephu netincetu letehlukene . Kuhlanganisa temnotfo tesigodzi kungenyusa kukhula kwemnotfo kuwo onkhe emave lase-Afrika leseningizimu . Lesigodzi sikhule ngekushesha kulomnyakalishumi lowengcile , sasebenta ngemandla kumaminerali , kutekulima , tekuchumana netekuvakasha . Kutfola kuhlanganiswa kwetemnotfo kudzinga kukhomba ematfuba labonakalako lapho kusebentisana khona kungazuzisa khona wonkhe ; kusisa kusakhiwonchanti ; kucinisa kuhwebelana ngalokutsite esigodzini ; kwehlisa imali lekhokhwako ; kanye nekulungisa tivimbela tekungakhokhwa kwemali , letinjengeminyele yemave lengasebenti kahle . Lomdvwebo lolandzelako ukhombisa kutsi leso naleso sigaba sekulawulwa kwemklamo siveta tindlela letinye tekuhlolwa kwemsebenti , lokwenta kutsi indlela yekuchuba lomsebenti kungabi ngulecondzile kodvwa ibe ngilokujikeletako . Luhlelo lwekucamba kabusha lolukhulu nalolusebenta ngalokuphumelelisako , loluhambisana netimboni letisebenta emikhakheni lehambisana nelisu lekukhula kwemnotfo . Babambilichaza basebenta kulawo macembu njengaku- Msebenti 1.1 babuke sifundvo ngalokwenteka bese bakha indlelasu yekuchumana . Kutfutfukisa imigomo kusinyatselo lesilandzelako njengobe loku kwendlala kutsi ngabe ummango utawuzuza njani umbono wawo . Imigomo kumele ibe ngulenembako , ngulenekuphumelela futsi ibe ngulemifisha ngalokwenele kutsi bantfu bakhone kubona tinzuzo . Luhlakamsebenti lwesikhatsi lesinekuphumelela lwekumisa imigomo lusikhatsi seminyaka lemitsatfu . Loluhlelo lunembononchanti weNingizimu Afrika lapho wonkhe umuntfu ativa akhululekile kepha abambelele kulabanye ; lapho wonkhe umuntfu afezekisa khona likhono lakhe leliphelele , live lapho khona litfuba lingancunywa ngekutalwa , kepha ngelikhono , imfundvo kanye nekusebenta ngekutikhandla . Kufezekisa ummango lonjalo kutawudzinga ingucuko yetemnotfo kanye nekugcila emitameni yekwakha emakhono alelive . Kute kucedvwe buphuya kuncishiswe nekungalingani , umnotfo kumele ukhule ngesivinini nangetindlela letitawuzuzisa bonkhe bahlali baseNingizimu Afrika . Kushayisana kwembono - khomba kushayisana lokuke kwakuvelela , emsebentini , ekhaya , nobe ngusiphi lesinye simo . Tindzaba lokumele kubukanwe nato - ngaphasi kwalesihloko - hlelisa loko lofuna kwenta . Kutfutfukisa emasu etindlu latinhlobo letahlukene kanye nekutfutfukiswa kwetindzawo tasemadolobheni lokuhlangene kute kusite bantfu kutsi bafinyelele etindzaweni nasetikhungweni tesive , etinhlakeni tembuso kanye nakumatfuba emsebenti newemabhizimisi . Lesahluko sicala ngekubuka tinchazelo tekwehlukahlukana . Sichubeka sicubungule tinhlangotsi tendlela leyimphumelelo yekulawula kwekwahlukahlukana kanye naletinye tindzaba letimcoka letinemtselela ekulawuleni kwehlukahlukana . Lesahluko siphetsa ngeluhla lwekucinisekisa kwakhiwa kweluhlelo lwetinyatselo letingatsatfwa macondzana nekwehlukahlukana . INingizimu Afrika ingazuza kulokukhulula lokusheshisako emaveni latfutfukako lokuholela esidzingweni lesenyukako semphahla kuphindze kwandzise timakethe tebatsengi . Ngalokunjalo , letinkhambiso tiphosa insayeya emaveni langenisa imali lesemkhatsini ngenca yekwandza kwekuncintisana ekwakheni kanye nakuletinye tinhlelo tethekhinoloji yelwati .
