Kuvela kwetimakethe letisacala kuphindze kwenyuse kucudzelana kwemave emhlaba , kufake kucindzeteleka lokukhulu emiholweni yetisebenti letinemakhono laphasi emikhakheni lokuhwebelwana kuyo . Inkinga yagezi yanga-2008 kanye naletinye tintfo letentekile takamuva tikhombise butsakatsaka betikhungo letihambisana netinkampani letingahasi kwahulumende letibukene nesakhiwonchanti seluhlelochumano . Kugwema tinkinga letinjalo kudzinga kuhlelwa kwetikhungo lokucacile , kuhlangana kwebanini bemasheya lokungagodli , kutiphendvulela lokuvakalako kanye netindlela tetimali letivakalako kute kukucinisekiswe kusimama . Senta tiphakamiso emkhakheni ngamunye yalena lebaliwe . Imitsetfo lephetse kulawula ivame kudidana , kushayisana kwenchubomgomo nemtsetfo loshayiwe . Siphakamisa kutsi kulungiswe loku . Kweswelakala kwetinsita - sibonelo , simo lesichazwe ngetulu . Ngekubete kwemanti lenele impompi yafakwa yase icansula wonkhe muntfu . Nobe sibonelo , kute tindlu letanele , kushayisana kungasuka ngekwabiwa kwetindlu nendlela lesetjentiswako makwabiwa tindlu . Ngoba liphakelo-timali linemandla ekwabiweni kwetinsita kuwo wonkhe masipala , kumele litsatfwe njengenchubo lemcoka kakhulu ekwenteni tincumo kuhulumende wasekhaya . Umphatsiswa loyimeya ( nobe likhansela leliphetse timali umakute imeya ) nguye lolungisa liphakelo-timali tamasipala wakhe . Kungumsebenti welihhovisi lamasipala kusekela lenchubo yekulungisa liphakelo-timali ngekuniketa lwati lwetemafa nebuchwepheshe loludzingekako . Kuchubeka nekwenta inchubekelembili ekwenyuseni imihilo nemazinga ekuphila , nekhukhicita nako kumele kwenyuke . Imakethe yetisebenti eNingizimu Afrika ivame kuba nekucudzelana emkhatsini wetimboni letenta inzuzo kanye netisebenti letihola kahle . Imiphumela lencunywe etinhlelweni tekucocisana ngemiholo tishiya indzawo lencane yalabasha labangenako kutsi bangene emisebentini . Kute kubukanwe nalamazinga lasetulu ekungasebenti , ikakhulukati emkhatsini welusha , kudzingeka tindlela letingetulu kwekwenta . Buholi betinhlangano tetisebenti bunendzima lebalulekile ekucinisekiseni kutsi lokuzuzwa ngemalunga ato kuyasimama esikhatsini lesidze . Kute kutfolakale loku , kukhicita kanye nemsebenti kumele kwenyuke ngalokuchubekako . Sebentisa i-PowerPoint uma une-data projektha , kantsi uma ingekho ungabhala leso naleso sigaba eshadini leliphendvulekako uphindze ukhombise labangenele tifundvo umdvwebo losekhasini 35 emanotsini esifundvo . Hulumende lotfutfukisako kumele ube nekukhona , kepha hulumende lokhonako akenti ngesehluleko , futsi ashayelwa umtsetfo nobe entiwe kuba khona ngetinkhulumo . Kumele akhiwe , sitini ngesitini , sikhungo ngesikhungo asimame futsi ahlelwe kabusha ngekuhamba kwesikhatsi . Udzinga buholi , tinchubomgomo letivakalako , baphatsi netisebenti letinemakhono , kulandzelana kwekutiphendvulela , tinhlelo letifanele kanye nekulandzelwa kwemtsetfo lokufanako nalokufanele . Kumele bakhe luhla lwetintfo letingenisa UMHOLO LEKUSEBENTA neluhla lwetintfo letakha kusetjentiswa kwemali . Kumele badvwebe lelithebula lelilandzelako eshadini leliphepha bese bayaligcwalisa . Sigaba 2 siphela ngemhlangano lomkhulu lapho ummango utfola khona litfuba lekubuyeketa , uhlolisise uphindze ucinisekise imininingwane lehlanganisiwe . Yonkhe imininingwane legcogcwe ngesikhatsi senchubo kumele ibekelwe ummango kutsi uyibone . Ummango ube sewucelwa kutsi ubeke bocalangaye bemiphumela lesihlanu yekuhlela ngesikhatsi senchubo yekuhlela . Beka lelithebula lelilandzelako etulu kumshina wekukhombisa elubondzeni . Uma ute lemishina , bhala lelithebula eshadini lelikhulu . Loku kungadzinga kutsi labachubisifundvo beCBP babambe imihlangano lembalwa namasipala kusenesikhatsi kute kutovunyelanwa kuphindze kubonisanwe ngalemininingwane lengenhla . Lesibutsetelo sisifinyento seluhlelo lesisezingeni lelisetulu . Letehluko leti-15 tikhuluma ngalokugcwele ngemikhakha lenetindzima letibalulekile , tiniketa bufakazi , tiphakamiso kanye netinhlaka leticacile tekwetfula loluhlelo . Emacophelo etinsita atisa takhamiti tinhlobo tetinsita letingabhekwa takhamiti , ayachaza kutsi umletsi msebenti kumele etfule njani tinsita kulabo labafanele . Ngaleyo ndlela , emacophelo etinsita ayincenye lengumgogodla we-SDIP . Emakomidi Eliwadi kumele aciniseke kutsi emacophelo etinsita labekwe etindzaweni tabo akhombisa tidzingo netifiso temmango wabo , khona bakhone kubaphendvulisa umangabe kunetinkinga ngemphumelelo . Njengoba lesigaba lesilandzelako sitjengisa , emacophelo etinsita asebenta umangabe akhona kuletsa lwati lolufanele mayelana netinsita letetfulwako . Kwengca kubonisana nekutibandzakanya kuya ekwakheni budlelwane bekulingana lobusimeme , ngekusungula budlelwane lobuchubekako , kanye nekubambisana lokunenhlakanipho lokufaka ekhatsi labanengi labadlala indzima . Kubindza , nobe kwenta ubindzile nako yindlela lesebentako kwendlulisa umlayeto kubantfu . Kulesisigaba luhlolo lwemakhono kufanele lwentiwe kanye netinsita letikhona kuyo imimango . Ngekubukisisa kukhulisa emakhono emimango kute imimango isombulule tinkinga tayo , imiklamo lehlala sikhatsi lesidze iyasungulwa bese emakhono ebantfu basekhaya ayakhuliswa . Khulumani ngekutsi kuya ngani inkhulumo-mphendvulo ibe lithulusi lelimcoka nekutsi ingasetjentiswa kuphi kulenchubo yekuhlela . Tinkhulumo kumele tivete kutsi inkhulumo-mphendvulo ingasita kutfola emaciniso ngetimo , tinkinga , imihambo , emasiko , tinhlelo kanye nalokwatiswako . Loku kungangena kunobe ngukuphi kuhlatiya kwesigaba . Imiklamo lehlulekako kubona tingoni tebulili etindzabeni letifaka ekhatsi kweswela , iHIV / AIDS , kanye nekukhahlabeteka kwabomake , noma kufinyelela kwabo etintfweni lebatidzingako , iminotfo , imisebenti noma umhlaba , angeke ikhone kucondzisisa lenkhinga lekubukene nayo . Kute imiklamo ibe yimphumelelo , kudzingeke kutsi yati kutsi sisusa saletinkinga sihambelana nebudlelwane kulabaphetse kanye nekungalingani endleleni bantfu labaphila ngayo lekudzingeka kubukisiswe kute lenkinga isombululeke . Bita linye licembu kutsi letfulele wonkhe umuntu lithebula labo . Bese ucela lamanye emacembu kutsi engete nobe abeke imibono . Liphepha Lelimhlophe lingumculu loyinchubomgomo lokhombisa kutsi ungafezeka kanjani umbono wekutfutfukisa hulumende wasekhaya lotibophetele ekwenteni ncono timphilo temmango wendzawo kanye nekuhlangabetana netidzingo tabo ngekutsi usebentisane nabo kute kutfolakale tindlela letisimeme tekwenta loku . Bomasipala balindzeleke kutsi balawule kuphatsa kwabo , tinhlelo tekuhlela nekwenta umcombelelotimali ngendlela lebeka etulu tidzingonchanti temmango . Kufanele kubhalwe phansi emagama alabo labacolisile ngekungaphumeleli emhlanganweni . ( Emalunga eKomidi kufanele ngaso sonkhe sikhatsi atjele nobe ngubani lolilunga lekomidi kutsi angeke aphumelele kuta emhlanganweni . Loku kwatiwa ngekutsi kucolisela kungaphumeleli . Ezingeni lesikhungo , kuphatfwa kwekunakekelwa kutemphilo kusenkingeni . Litiko Letemphilo kamuva nje letfule luhlelo lwekuhlola likhono lekuphatsa . Lokunye kuhlelwa kabusha kumele kufake ekhatsi kuniketelwa kwemandla kutisebenti , kuletinye tinhlaka nasekuniketweni kwemisebenti lokuvamile . Leti tinhlobohlobo tetindlela tekwenta letingenako ekulawulweni kwemklamo tingahlukaniswa tibe macembu lasihlanu labalulekile , labhalwe kulelithebuli ekhasini lelilandzelako . Veta inftukutselo kwakho uma ngabe kufanele , nobe kulungile phindze kufanele kutsi ungenta njalo . Ungajaki kukuveta , uma kutakwenta inkinga kutsi yandze nobe kwakhe lenye . Tfola tindzawo letiphephile tekukhipha inftukutselo yakho . Akukafaneli kutsi utjengise inftukutselo ngaso sonkhe sikhatsi nobe kubhekana nako , ngalesinye sikhatsi imiva yendlula masinyane . Kwenta ncono lizinga lemfundvo etikolweni letingasebenti kahle nasemakolishi emfundvo nekucecesha lokuchubekako . Bukisa emanotsini esifundvo ( emakhasi 56 kuya ku-64 ) macondzana nethuluzi yakho bese ulandzela inchubo . Uma kuphumeleleka condzisa timphendvula takho kuloko lokulwatinchanti seliwadi yakho . Ngutiphi tinhlangano temmango nobe tinhlangotsi tamasipala lekufanele timenywe kutewukhuluma ngemisebenti yato eKomidini leliWadi nobe emhlanganweni wesigodzi ? Lizinga lelisetulu lelutjalomali , ngekugcwala kwelutjalomali lwesive elutjalwenimali lwangasese . Loku kutawuncika ebudlelwaneni bekusebentisana nemkhakha wangasese , kucinisekiswa kwenchubomgomo kanye nekwakha litsemba ekukhuleni kwemnotfo kwesikhatsi lesidze . Kuphindze kube yindlela yekucondzisisa ngetidzingo letehlukene temmango . Kuhlatiya ngetebulili akubahlukanisi bantfu ngekutsi ' bayimiti ' noma ' bangulabaphuyile ' ngoba bahlala emndenini munye , kodvwa kusebentisa indlela leveta emaciniso ngemuntfu , ngamunye . Yehlukanisa kuhlatiya emadvodza nebesifazane - tinkinga tabo , tidzingo tabo , kanye nekufinyelela eminotfweni nekuphatseni . Nga-2030 , iNingizimu Afrika kumele ibe ineluhlelo loluphelele lwekuvikeleka kutenhlalo lolufaka ekhatsi tibonelelo tahulumende , kongela umhlalaphasi lokuphocelekile , timbuyeketo tetingoti ( letinjengetimbuyeketo tekungasebenti , kufa nekukhubateka ) kanye nekongela umhlalaphasi kwekutitsandzela . Kwakha leminye imisebenti ngekutfutfukisa tekulima , lokwesekelwe ekuhlelweni kabusha kwemhlaba kanye nekhululiswa kwalokulinywako lokuniselwako kanye nalokukhicitwa emhlabatsini . Linani leliphakelo timali letakhiwo-sicalo lamasipala lelisetjentswa emiklameni-sicalo lekhonjiwe kuloyo mnyaka wetimali , ngephasi kwe-IDP yamasipala . Umphatsi weCBP ufundzisa labangenele tifundvo ngeLisu , achate kutsi ngabe Lisukunyiswe njani abuye acacise aphindze enabe uma kunesidzingo . Masipala kumele ente siciniseko kutsi lemiklamo icondzene nemigomo yamasipala nemacebo , kanye nesakhiwo setinsita , aphindze ahambisane netidzingo temtsetfo . Lesigaba litfuba lamasipala kutsi ahlanganise imiklamo ngalokucuketfwe , indzawo netikhatsi kute afike eluhlelweni loLubumbene futsi loluhlanganisiwe , njengeluhlelo lwekutfutfukisa umnotfo wendzawo . Kuya emihlanganweni yemkhandlu - Inchubo yemkhandlu yekwenta umtsetfo kumele ibe nguletiphendvulelako , ivuleke , iphendvule emalunga emmango . Sive sinelilungelo lekuya emhlanganweni wemkhandlu . Kute sive sente lelilungelo kudzingeka sati kutsi unini nekutsi ubanjelwa kuphi umhlangano wemkhandlu . Kumele baphindze bati kutsi umhlangano wemkhandlu ungani . Emakomidi eliwadi angasita sive ekubanikeni lwati . Emalunga eKomidi yeLiwadi kumele aye emihlanganweni yemkhandlu kute bahlale bati njengebameli bemmango nekubenta banikete timphendvulo ummango . KUFAKA BULILI EKUHLELISENI INTFUTFUKO KUSHO KUTSI NOMA NGABE NGISIPHI SINYATSELO LESITSATFWAKO NOMA UMKLAMO NOMA LUHLELO LOLUHLELWE NGEMAKOMIDI EMAWADI , UMZAMO WEKUBAMBISANA UYENTIWA KUCINISEKISA KUTSI BULILI BUYAMBANDZAKANYWA KULETINHLELO . Kuhlelela kusebenta - loku kufaka ekhatsi kuhlela kabanti indlela lokufanele umklamo wenteke ngayo . Kubandzakanyeka yingcikitsi lengumnyombo . Cela labangenele tifundvo kutsi batehlukanise ngemacembu abo lamancane bese ubabukisa iSWOT yemacembu etenhlalakahle ekhasini 66 emanotsini esifundvo . Kwenyuka lokusimeme ekwakheni imisebenti kutawudzinga kukhula kwemnotfo lokunonophako kanye nekucedvwa kwetivimbela , letinjengemfundvo lesezingeni leliphasi nobe tindlela tekuhlalisa bantfu letikhiphela ngaphandle linyenti . Letintfo tibalulekile ekuzuzeni emazinga lasetulu elutjalomali nekuncintisana , kwandzisa umkhicito kanye nekutfumela imphahla kulamanye emave . Bemabhizimisi , tetisebenti , imimango kanye nahulumende kutawumele basebente ngekubambisana kute kuzuzwe kukhula kwetemnotfo lokunonophako . Kukholwakala nekuphumelela kwanoma ngumuphi umklamo kusime ekutsini labo labatawuzuza ngalomsebenti bawusekele . ngako-ke kumcoka kutsi imibono yabo bonkhe labatsintsekako ivakale , kute kube nesiciniseko sekutsi loluhlelo lutawusekelwa . Ngekwati kutsi imvamisa labasikati babekwa esimeni lesibucayi nakwakhiwa tinhlelo noma kuvetwa tintfo labanye labangakucabanga kutsi ngito tidzingo tabomake . Kumcoka kutsi kuviwe imibono nemicondvo yabo kute ummango utewusekela lomklamo . Kutilungiselela kahle kungasita ekucedzeni lenye yenkhatsateko yekwetfula inkhulumo . Watini ngemaKomidi emaWadi ? Imihlangano yekucecesha ibalulekile ngoba inika lwati , iphindze yatise ngetintfo letitsite , phindze iletse litfuba lekutfuftukisa inchubomgomo nekwentiwa kwetincumo . Avamise kwentiwa emacenjini lamancane khona babambi lichaza kulomhlangano wekucecesha batokhona kubuta intfo letsite ngekujula . Babambi lichaza behlukaniselwa emacenjini bese babuka timo letingenteka ekhasini 68 . Lemibuto lelandzelako itawubumba lesikhatsi . Buta umbuto ngamunye sikhatsi sinye , vumela inkhulumo kumunye ngamunye ngaphambi kwekuya kulolandzelako . Bhala emaphuzu lamcoka eshadini . Etukwekwenta imisebenti yaMasipala , boMasipala ngekweMtsetfo kumele bahole , baphatse baphindze bahlele kute kube nentfutfuko , ngendzima ledlalwa Luhlelo Lwekutfutfukisa loluhlanganisiwe . BoMasipala kumele bente umsebenti wekufaka sandla ekutfutfukiseni umnotfo wemmango , kwakha ematfuba emisebenti nekucedza buphuya ngekutibandzakanybandzakanya naletinhlelo . Kwelula tinhlelo tetenhlalakahle kanye netinhlelo temisebenti yesive , letenta kutsi umbuso ukwati kwetfula tinhlelo uphindze wesekele imimango lephuyile , ikakhulukati leyo lenemazinga lasetulu ebugebengu neludlame . IBatho Pele iniketa luhlaka kwekuntjintja umkhakha wahulumende wekwetfula . Batho Pele kusho kutsi ' beka bantfu ekucaleni ' yakhelwe kutsi tisebenti tahulumende tinake tinsita tiphindze tilwelwe emalengiso ekwetfuleni umsebenti wato . Yenta emakhasimende kutsi ente tisebenti tahulumende titiphendvulele ngendlela letetfula ngato tinsita . Kukala kusebenta kungalinganiswa ngekubuka kutsi ngabe imigomo yeBatho Pele isetjentiswa kangakanani uma tisebenti tahulumende tisebenta nemmango . Umholi ekufundza kumele abenesiciniseko kutsi tincumo tiyatsatfwa , tinhlelo tekusebenta tiyentiwa , nekutsi bantfu bayatibophelela kusebenta . Umholi lomuhle ngulotihluphako ngekutsi kucociswana ngani emhlanganweni nekutsi kufundvwa ngani , futsi kufundvwa njani . Kwenta sibonelo : 54 bantfu babandzakanyeka kunchubo yekuhlela . Emacembu bekafaka ekhatsi labasebentako - labasetimbonini nasemahhovisi , labatisebentako , labangasebenti , bomake labangakashadi kanye nebantfwana . Lilungu leliKomidi leliwadi , Nkst Mofolo kanye nekhansela yendzawo , Nkst Smith , bebakhona kuyo yonkhe imihlangano . Bachubisifundvo bekunguboMnu Jones naNkst Mpefu . UMnu Mars lovela ku-dplg naye bekakhona kantsi nemhleli wemadolobha uMnu M Zungu naye bekakhona . Tindzawo letibalulekile tekusebenta ewadini nguleto letikhonjwa yi-IDP nenchubo yekusebenta . EMakomidi eMawadi kumele ente siciniseko kutsi tidzingo tetindzawo tawo tiyahlangabetwa ngekutsi abe yincenye yenchubo ye-IDP . Etinkhulumeni nemakhansela amasipala netisebenti tahulumende tifiso tetindzawo tawo kumele tishiwo tiphindze tigcamiswe . Ngabe yini lesiyidzingako kuteute sitolungiselela kuhlela ? Loluhla lwekusebenta indzaba yekwehlukahlukana ludzinga imininingwane leminingi netinchubo leticabangiseseke ngalokukhanyako . Loluhla kufanele lutfole tindlela tekugcugcutela kuhlonishwa kwekwehlukahlukana , kulinganiseka kwematfuba nekuphatsana kahle kusasetjentwa indzaba yekubandlululana . Umtsetfosisekelo waseNingizimu Afrika uphindze ubeke tigungu leticinisa intsandvoyelinyenti . Leti tatiwanjengekutsi tigungu te'Sehluko 9 ' , njengoba tichazwa kumtsetfosisekelo Sehluko 9 . Kuhlela lokutinte eMmangweni lokunemphumelelo lidlelandzawonye emkhatsini kwabo bonkhe babambimsuka . EmaKomidi emaWadi asakhiwo lesemukelwe lesisebenta njengemgudvu wekwenta livi lemmango kutsi liviwe . Bachubisifundvo beCBP kumele basebente nabo bonkhe babambimsuka kwenta lenchubo isebente . EmaKomidi eLiwadi angatitfola asesimeni sekubhekana nekushayisana . Bukisisa letimo letilandzelako nendlela lesetjentisiwe . Lemigomo lesiphohlongo seyakhe sisusa se-PMS kuhulumende wasekhaya . EmaKomidi eLiwadi achuba kutibandzakanya kwesive enchubeni yentfutfuko , kubuyeketwa nekusebenta kwekuphatfwa kwe-IDP . Ngakoke emaKomidi eLiwadi kumele abe nesibindzi , lwati nelikhono khona batofeza lomsebenti . Lelithebula lesifinyeto sebadlali-tindzima , imisebenti yabo kanye nebudlelwane eKomidini leLiwadi . Umehluko ngekwebulili usho umehluko lokhona emkhatsini kwebafati nemadvodza lebatikhetsele wona futsi longahunyushwa ngendlela letsite . Kepha , ' kwehlukana ' lokuningi emkhatsini kwemadvodza nebafati , noma ngulapho kufaka khona ingoni yekutikhetsela ( sibonelo , kwekugcoka ) , noma kunjalo kuseyincenye yetimiso tekungalingani , letinganiki bumcoka lobungakanani etintfweni lebatikhetsele tona bafati tiphindze tichubekisele embili kufinyelela ngalokungalingani emandleni netintfo letiyincenye yemnotfo . Yindlela lehleleke kakhulu leyenteka enkantolo yemtsetfo , nelijaji nobe imantji lengatsatsi luhlangotsi , lobeka sincumo sekugcina emva kwekulalela bufakazi nenkhulumo-mphikiswano kuwo onkhe emacembu . Sincumo sakhe sisuselwa emtsetfweni welicala , umtsetfo loshayiwe nemihambo yemitsetfo . Ngulowo nalowo msebenti wesikhashana wehlukile kuleminye ngulowo unetinsayeya netindzaba lecondzene nawo lekufute utisebente . Ngaloko ke - luhla loluhlukile ludzingekile kute kube nesiciniseko kutsi lomsebenti uphetseka ngemphumelelo . Umkhandlu ungenta indlela yekutsi satiso saloyo mtsetfo sifika njani esiveni , kumbe ngemaphosta nobe imisakato . Emalunga emmango angabhala phasi imibono labayimikisa ehhovisini lamasipala . Umkhandlu kumele wente indlela lesipesheli yemalunga emmango lokungenteka awuyanga esikolweni , nobe letinye tici letenta kube lukhuni kubo kuletsa imibono . UMSEBENTI LOBALULEKILE WEKOMIDI YELIWADI kwenta siciniseko kutsi takhamiti ewadini labo tiyincenye futsi tiyatiswa ngetincumo temkhandlu letiphatselene netimphilo tato . Emakomidi eliwadi angemehlo netindlebe temmango aphindze abe luhlangotsi lolumcoka lwekutfutfukisa kuvana kabubili emkhatsini wemmango nemkhandlu . Loku kusho kutsi likomidi leliwadi kumele libonisane nemmango mayelana nentfutfuko netinhlelo tetinsita . Kuchumana kumcoka ekwenteni siciniseko sekutsi imibono , netinhloso temmango tiba yincenye yekwenta tincumo tekwetfulwa kwetinsita nentfutfuko . Tinhlelo tebuncusa letitfutfukisa tentsengiso kute kwelekelelwe kwandza kwesabelo seNingizimu Afrika etimakethe temhlaba . Insayeya yekucala ekulawulweni kwemklamo kucinisekisa kutsi umklamo utfulwa ngendlela lobekwe ngayo . Yesibili , lekuyinsayeya lebukwe kakhulu , kucinisekisa kutsi kwentiwa lokunyenti ngemali leniketiwe nangaletinye tinsita letikhona tekuphumelelisa tinhloso temklamo . Kuhlela kutsi umklamo utawusebenta njani - Loku kubuye kwatiwe ngekutsi silinganiso sekwenta intfo noma lizinga lekwenta noma sigaba sekulandzela luhlelo lwekusebenta . Timo netidzingo tingagucuka njengoba bantfu labanyenti beta kulendzawo , tidzingo letindzala kungenteka kutsi setibukiwe bese kutfutfukiswa leti letinsha . Umsebenti lomkhulu wemaKomidi emaWadi kusita emakhansela emawadi lakhetfwe ngentsandvo yelinyenti kutsi ente umsebenti latfunywe wona ngalokuyimphumelelo wekumela bantfu beliwadi . Tonkhe takhamiti kumele tiphatfwe ngekunakekela nekuba neluvelo . Imphendvulo : esikhundleni sekubita ithenda , umkhandlu uncome kucasha inkontileka X ngoba itsi inemagunya ekwenta loko . Yini indlela lesetjentiswe ngumkhandlu ? Tinhlelo tetimali leticinisiwe kute kwehliswe tindleko tato kuphindze kwentiwe ncono kufinyelela kuto kwemabhizimisi lamancane nalasemkhatsini . Leso naleso sigaba sakhiwe linani letigameko letitsite lapho kungasetjentiswa khona linye nobe ngetulu kumathuluzi eCBP . Kufanele kube yinhloso yabo bonkhe basebenti . labatfutfukako ( hulumende , masipala , noma basebenti labalusito bangaphandle ) kwakha imimango uma ulawula imiklamo kuyo . Imimango ikhuliswa luhlobo lolukahle lwentfutfuko , ikakhulu uma ifaka sandla emiklameni letsintsa nayo . Uma ifundza kuphumelela ekutfutfukiseni ummango , imimango itawusebentisa leto tintfo letifundzile kuletinye tindzawo temphilo yayo . Itawufundza kuhlela kahle kakhulu kantsi nemakhono ebuholi atawukhula . Kutilandza - ingucuko esigabeni sekuphatsa emangweni ngeke itfolakale ngaphandle kwekutsi labamelele bantfu kuleso sigaba bative banenshisekelo yekukwenta loko . Inshisekelo yengucuko kufanele ikhutsatwe . Loku kungahle kudzinge imitamo yekubambisana ngaseKomidini yeliWadi lekungiyo lechaza kutsi ngikuphi kutiphatsa lokwemukelekako / lokungamukeleki , yini emazinga lasesigabeni lesiphansi ekufeza tinhloso nekutsi yini lefakiwe yekuvivinya uma kungafinyelelwa kulamazinga . UMBUTO 6 Tisetjentiswa njani ? Ngubani lotisebentisako ? Lungiselela kubhalwa kwelisu kusenesikhatsi njengobe loku kungadzinga kutsi kuhlelwe emalephuthophu nobe tisetjentiswa tekuthayipha . Kunciphisa kukhishwa kwegesi leyonakalisa imvelo kubuye kwentiwe ncono kusebenta kwemandla . Cinisekisa kutsi licembu livisisa umehluko emkhatsini ' kwekubaluleka ' kanye ' nekufinyeleleka ' . Lamagama angahunyushelwa elulwimini lwetfu lwendzawo . Kuniketa tinsitanchanti letitakwenta bantfu bakwati kutfutfukisa emakhono kute basebentise ematfuba lavelako eliveni , bakwati kufaka sandla emimangweni yabo ngekundluliselwa kwemali letfolakalao kanye nemakhono . Kusukela ngasekupheleni kwemnyakalikhulu weli-19 , iNingizimu Afrika isebentise umnotfo wetimbiwa ngekunaka kancane nobe ngekunganaki imvelo . Kudzingeka tingucuko kute kuvikelwe imvelo kube kwentiwa lelive lizuze kutimbiwa talo . Ngetulu kwekubaluleka kwemnotfo wetimbiwa tivuseleleka kabusha , imitfombolusito yemvelo yalelive ifaka ekhatsi tilwandle letakhelene nalo , umhlabatsi , emantii , imvelo nalokuphila kuyo , kukhanyisa kwelilanga kanye nasemngcengcemeni welugu . Kute tinsita tekungcebeleka eWadini A. Loku kuhlupha bantfu labasha labema emakoneni etitaladi , ngalesinye sikhatsi bayalwa baphindze bacabane . Emasontfo akulendzawo asabambe umhlangano wekutfola likhambi lalenkinga . Sebabikele neliKomidi leLiwadi . Lendzaba seyike yakhulunywa liKomidi leLiwadi , lelivumelene kutsi likhansela leliwadi liyimikise emhlanganweni wemkhandlu , licele umkhandlu kutsi ubambe umhlangano nabo bonkhe labatsintsekako , lokufaka ekhatsi ummango wemabhizinisi , emacembu alabasha , kanye netinhlangano tenkholo , njll . liKomidi leLiwadi lisite ngekuhamba libamba umhlangano nalabatsintsekako labehlukene kubabikela lenkinga kanye nesizatfu semhlangano walabatsintsekako . Umhlangano wabitwa , kwavunyelwana kutsi inkhundla yemidlalo kanye nendlu lencane yemacembu ingasita ekunikeni bantfu labasha indzawo yekuhlangana . Imimango yetenkholo yavumelana kutsi itawusebentisana ekuletseni tinhlelo nemisebenti bantfu labasha labangatibandzakanya nayo . Emakomidi eLiwadi kumele anikwe lwati njalo njalo njalo ngekuhamba kwetimali tamasipala . ' Kuhamba kwetimali ' kuphuma nekungena kwetimali esikhwameni sasebhange setimali tamasipala . Umsebenti 3 Khetsa kube kubili kelemibono yalokungentiwa loyibhale kuMsebenti 2 . Shano lotakwenta kusita liKomidi leliWadi lakho kufeza loku . Kungabi nekwetsembana - bahlali kungenteka bangabi nelitsemba kubaholi labakhetsiwe , EmaKomidini Emawadi kanye / nome kutikhulu tamasipala lekwetfula tinhlelo nemiklamo ngalokuyimphumelelo . Loku kungabangelwa nguloko lasebake bakubona ngaphambili nobe kungabi nelwati . Emalunga EliKomidi Emawadi kumele atfole tindlela tekukhutsata nekubuyisela litsemba kanye nekutetsemba kutsi kutibandzakanya kwemmango kunemphumela lomuhle nobe kunekubaluleka . Kutembusave letibonakalako , intsandvo yelinyenti yenta ingucuko leshiyanako . Ludlame lwakamuva lwaseNyakatfo ne-Afrika lusikhumbuto mbamba sebungoti bekungaphatsi kahle kanye netikhungo letibutsakatsaka letivumela labancono kutsi bagcogce umnotfo ngekutsatsela bantfu . Indlela lelandzelwe yelukhetfo kufanele ibhalwe phansi bonkhe bantfu bayibone bayihlaba lapho bangayihlaba khona . Gocota ngekufinyeta ngasinye sigaba . Bomakhelwane beNingizimu Afrika bakhungetfwe lizinga lelisetulu lebuphuya nekungabi khona kwemisebenti , nemisebenti lemincane kutekulima . Luhlelo lwelubandlululo lwaphocelela linyenti lebantfu base-Afrika kutsi baye etindzaweni tasemakhaya letingakhiciti . Umphumela waloko kwaba kutsi umkhakha wekulimela kutsengisa lohlukanisiwe wetsembele etisebentini tasemapulazini letihola kancane , letikhungetfwe buphuya , letimimango leminyene nematfuba etemnotfo lanemkhawulo kanye netinhlelo tahulumende letincane . Siphakamiso seKhomishini kusakhiwonchanti setemnotfo sifaka ekhatsi , kwelekelela ngetimali , kuhlela kanye nekulungisa . Loku lirekhodi letintfo tangaphandle ( tintfo licembu lemklamo lelingenamandla kuto ) letibalulekile ekuphumeleleni kwemklamo . KWEMUKELWA KWELIPHAKELOTIMALI SINYATSELO LESISEMBILI SEKUHLOLA KUTSI NGABE LETINCHUBO TE-IDP NECBP TINGENTEKA . Letinhloso letichazwe eluhlakeni lekwentiwa kwemisebenti , tihlanganiswe nemsebenti , tinsita ntinhlelo tetindleko , aniketa lwatiso lekusekela kuhlatiywa kwetindleko-nzuzo . Ummango uba banini bemiklamo leyentiwako . Loku kungaholela ekutseni ummango unakekele kakhulu tindzawo letinjengemapaki nobe takhiwo . IBatho Pele ihola emacebo ahulumende ekuhlela , tonkhe tigaba Teluhlelo lweKutfutfukisa loluBumbene , kulawula kusebenta kanye nekuphatsa lokuneluvelo . Ngalokunjalo kubalulekile kulungisa simo sekusebenta sawo onkhe emalunga emisebenti yahulumende . Imigomo lenemacebo lakhako ematiko ahulumende Kuvelonkhe kummel ente emacembo lakhako lakhako lakhako kanye nemibono yato tonkhe tifundza kanye nematiko abohulumende basekhaya . Ekugcineni baphatsi beTindzawo Temiphumela Lemcoka nabo kumele bente lokufanako . Linyenti letakhamuti lihlala etindlini letincane letakhiwa nguhulumende nobe emikhukhwini yangemuva kwemabala . Tindlu letinyenti kulendzawo atinaye gezi nobe emanti lageletako . Kulendzawo kunetikolo letintsatfu kanye nemitfolamphilo lemitsatfu kuphela . Kube khona kwenta ncono lokuzuziwe ekwetfulweni kwetinsita ngalokuphumelelisako esikhwameni sahulumende , lokucacile Sikhungo Sekugcogcwa Kwentsela saseNingizimu Afrika kanye nemiklamo levivinywako eTikweni Letasekhaya , Letemphilo neLetebulungiswa . Kuphatfwa kwekusebenta kanye neluhlelo lwekwenta ncono kube senkhabeni yalokuhlelwa kabusha , kantsi letimphumelelo kumele tiphindvwe nakuleminye imikhakha yahulumende . Lolu lwati loselutfolakele lukhombisa kutsi yini lengazuziwa uma baholi netisebenti batibophetele ekusebenteni ngekubambisana kute kwentiwe ncono kusebenta . Onkhe emaKomidi emaWadi kumele atsatse sincumo mayelana netinhlobo temakomidi lamancane kanye netikhundla lafunako ewadini lawo . Emalunga eliKomidi leliWadi aniketwa tikhundla letitsite . Liphakelo-timali akumeli libe yimfihlo ! Loku kutsatsa cishe li-awa nelicembu lelisembili lelihlanganisele lebelihlala kuleliwadi lokungenani iminyaka lelishumi . Kutakwenteka kanjani loku ? Insayeya lenkhulu yeNingizimu Afrika kubuyela emuva kubukwe buphuya nekungalingani . Kwenyusa emazinga ekuphila kute afinyelele ezingeni lelibuncane bekugcina lokuphakanyiswe eluhlelweni , kutawufaka ekhatsi inhlanganisela yekwenyusa ematfuba emsebenti , imiholo lesetulu ngekwandza kwemkhicito , tibonelelo tetenhlalo [ 1 ] kanye netinsita letiniketwa sive letisezingeni lelikahle . Tonkhe letinsayeya titawuholela ekwenyukeni kwemisebenti nemiholo , kantsi kukhula kwemnotfo lokunonophako kutawelula ematfuba abo bonkhe kuphindze kuletse imitfombolusito ledzingekako kute kwentiwe ncono temfundvo . Kwetfula Luhlelo Lwemtfombolusito Loluhlanganisako lwanga-2010 ( kutfola lokungenani ema-20 0 MW agezi etintfweni letivuselelekako ) kute kuncishiswe kukhishwa kwekhabhoni embonini yagezi kusukela ku-0.9kg ikhilowathi yeli-awa ngalinye kuya ku-0.6kg kukhilowathi yeli-awa ngayinye . Labamelele emaKomidi emaWadi bangahlanganyela kuMbutsano wekukhulumisana ngeLuhla lweNtfutfuko loluBumbene . LoMbutsano unika litfuba lalabaphatsekako kumasipala kutsi bamelele tifiso temmango . Uphindze unikete indlela lecondzile yekukhulumisana , kuvumelana , nekutsatsa tincumo kanyekanye emkhatsini wemmango namasipala . LoMbutsano uphindze unikete litfuba lekulandzelela kwakhiwa nekufezekiswa kweLuhla lweNtfutfuko loluBumbene . Umbono weKhomishini ngukutsi esikhatsini lesidze lesitako , basebentisi kumele bakhokhele bunyenti betindleko tesakhiwonchanti , lokutakuba nekuvikeleka kwemakhaya laphuyile . Indzima yahulumende kanye nemgcinimafa kuniketa ticiniseko letidzingekako kute kuphindze kukhokhelwe tindleko ngekuhamba kwesikhatsi , ngaleyo ndlela kulungiswe intsengo . Hulumende kumele ente kulawula lokufanele kanye netinhlaka tekuphatsa kute sakhiwonchanti sisetjentiswe ngalokuyiphumelelo kantsi nemali lekhokhwako ibekwe emazingeni lafanele . Sakhiwonchanti lesiletsa inzuzo , sikweleti lesenteke ngesikhatsi kwakhiwa kumele sibe ekhasini lekuhanjiswa kwetimali temabhizimisi embuso nobe etinkampani tangasese letenta umsebenti . Kumele kusetjentiswe ticinisekiso ngalokukhetsekile kute kuncishiswe tindleko kuphindze kutfolakale nemali tekusebenta kwesikhatsi lesidze . Kwelekelelwa ngetimali kwemakhaya laphuyile kumele kube sebaleni futsi kungagodli lutfo . Sakhiwonchanti setenhlalo lesingaletsi inzuzo - lesinjengetikolwa nobe tibhedlela - kumele tilekelelwe ngetimali teluphakemomali . Ummango kumele utibandzakanye nenchubo yekulandzelela , kukala nekubuyeketa kusebenta , ngoba masipala , emva kwekubonisana nemmango , kumele wakhe uphindze usebentise tinhlelo , uphindze ukhombe tinchubo taloku . Masipala angayisungula inkhundla yekutibandzakanya kwemmango , uma abona kutsi inganiketa kutibandzakanya lokungetulu kwemmango nekufaka sandla . EmaKomidi eLiwadi angabayincenye yenkhundla . Yindzima yekhansela kusungula lenkhundla yemmango . Tindleko ke letingabakhona ? Letinjongo teleka tinhloso letibekwe Endleleni Lensha Yekukhulisa Umnotfo . Uma ngabe kusebenta lokulindzelekile kungenteki , kumele kwentiwe imitamo yekusita umuntfu kute afeze tinhloso takhe . Uma ngabe kusebenta ngaphansi kwelizinga lelilindzelekile kuchubeka kungatsatfwa tinyatselo tekumisa sisebenti emsebentini , luhlelo lwekucondzisa tigwegwe kanye nekucedvwa kwenkontileka . Ekuhlatiyeni kwetinombolo ema-statistics ayasetjentiswa ekufinyeteni idatha nasekukhombiseni budlelwane , kusebentiswa indlela yekucabanga le-deductive . Ekuhlatiyeni idatha yelwati lwetimphawu kusetjentiswa kucabanga loku-inductive . Inductive uchaza kucabanga lokusuka entfweni lecondzile kuya ekukhulumeni ngelinyenti - ngalamanye emagama , kusho kusuka kulokubonako uye esiphetfweni lesikhuluma ngelinyenti . Kulandzelela inchubekelaphambili yemsebenti wesikhashana kubakulekile kucinisekisa kutsi lomsebenti uchubeka ngendlela lefanele nekutsi tikhubato letinsha nobe tingucuko tiyabonwa tiphindze tinakekelwe esigabeni sekusebenta lesilandzelako . Emacembu lenta umsebenti wesikhashana asebentisa tinkhomba tekufezeka kwesmebenti kulandzelela inchubekelaphambili . Tinkhomba lizinga leliphokophelwe lelikhombisa kutsi tinhloloso tifezekile . Ngalesinye sikhatsi Tihlaka tekuhlela indlela yekusebenta tibita tinkhomba ngekutsi ' tinkhomba leticinisekiseka ngeliso lekungakhetsi ' . Tinkhomba tidzinga kuba nguletifanele , letenetisako , leticacile , letikalekako , letongako naletitfolakalako . Cedzela ngesifundvo seliklasi lesitsatselwe ethebulini lelikhasi 90 . Lithebula liniketa eMakomidi eLiwadi luhla lwetintfo tekuhlola labangatibukisisa nalabangatisebentisa kukhankhasa emmangoni . IKhomishini Yekulingana Ngekwebulili kanye neLitiko Labomake , Bantfwana Nebantfu Labanekukhubateka ngekubambisana kumele batibekele imigomo yekuchubekisela embili emalungelo abomake baphindze baphike ngenchubekelembili leseyentiwe njalo ngemnyama . Kulesigaba umehluleli kumele asebentise umsebenti wekusombulula inking . Umklamo lomkhulu ( iproject ) ungachazwa njengendzima noma lokusibopho lokudzingeka kufezwe ngesikhatsi lesikaliwe . Kufanele uletse kubaluleka noma luntjintjo lolukahle ngandlela tsite . Umklamo ukalelwa sikhatsi awufanele utsatse sikhatsi lesidze , unjalo nje uba neliphakelomali lelikaliwe futsi kuvamise kutsi kube ngiwowodvwa umsebenti ngalesosikhatsi . Singabekisa nje , kubomasipala kunemiklamo lechubeka-njalo , njengekulungiswa kwemigwaco , emisebentini lenjengale loluhlelo loluchaziwe lungeke lulunge kufuneka kube ngulotawenta umehluko lobonakalako ngandlelatsite . Hlela kuhambahamba ewadini nifike etindzaweni tekuhleleka kwemhlaba letisembili . Njengobe nihamba , caphelani timphawu letisembili nekutsi ngabe tivele kuphi . Kubalulekile kutsatsa lemininingwane bese niyifaka esitfombeni semusho lesibonisa nobe ngutiphi timphawu telive nobe tekutfutfukisa kuleso naleso sicheme kanye nekuniketa ingcikitsi yeliwadi njengobe lesibonelo lesingentasi sibonisa . Sebentisa loLuhlu lwesicinisekiso lwesimondzawo kucinisekisa kutsi tonkhe tinhlangotsi tifakiwe . Kwakha luhlelo lwemshwalense wetemphilo kuyinjongo lebalulekile . Kunetintfo letine letifunekako kucala kute uphumelele : kwenta ncono luhlelo lwemshwalense wetemphilo , kwehlisa tindleko tekwelapha tangasese , kuheha letinye tisebenti leticeceshiwe emkhakheni wahulumende newangasese kanye nekutfutfukisa luhlelo lwelwati lwetemphilo lolwelulela betfuli betinhlelo tetemphilo bahulumende nebangasese . Lokuhlelwa kabusha kutawutsatsa sikhatsi , kudzinga kusebentisana emkhatsini wemkhakha wahulumende newangasese kanye nesidzingo semitfombolusito lebalulekile . Bhala timphendvula ephepheni lelibanti , ucele babambilichaza kutsi bachaze imigomo lemcoka yakunye ngakunye kwaletinchubo . Indlela lesihlangana nayo nekushayisana inemtselela ekutsini siphendvula njani . Kunetigaba letimbalwa letenta umjikeleto wekushayisana . Lomjikeleto ungabamuhle nobe ube mubi . Lomjikeleto ungumbalave losebentako wekucabanga ngetindlela kushayisana lokusebenta ngato etimphilweni tebantfu . Labangenele tifundvo bafundza leso naleso sigaba , ngakulolunye luhlangotsi umchubisifundvo angachaza leso naleso sigaba , acacise futsi achate uma kunesidzingo . Yini lokungangisita kutsi ngilalele ngalokuphumelelisako ? EmaKomidi emaWadi adzinga kwenta imitamo letiyile kucinisekisa kutsi onkhe emacembu ayahlanganyela etinchubeni tekutsatsa tincumo letitsintsa ummango nekutsi abakhona emihlanganweni yekwetfulwa kwemibiko , nekutsi imibono yawo ifakiwe , noma ngabe emacembu awabomake , imimmango yebantfu labadzabuka ngaphandle kwaleli , emacembu etinkholo , njalonjalo . Loku kungahle kudzinge luhlu lwekusebenta lolubonakalako lolwakhelwe ngco emacembu lashiyeke ngaphandle . Inchubo yeCBP yemukela kutsi emalunga emmango anelwati nelwatinchanti lesivelele mayelana nekutfutfukiswa kwawo futsi igcizelela kakhulu kuletinhlangotsi . Kulomsebenti lolandzelako tinkhulumoluholo nebantfu labayimitfombolusito lesembili tisetjentiselwa kutfola emasu mayelana netisombululo letingahle tibe khona . Lelicembu , liholwa ' bachubisifundvo ' , kumele lendlale imisebenti lesembili kanye nemiklamo lechubekako emmangweni walo kanye nekutsi ngabe baphakeli betinsita ngubobani . Mengameli Mbeki ugcizelela ' umzabalazo wekucedza buphuya kantsi kutfutfuka lokuphansi eliveni lakitsi kusisekelo ekufezeni inhloso yetfu kuvelonkhe yekwakha ummango lonakekelako nalogcile kubantfu . ' Lena yindlela lokumele sivisise ngayo IBatho Pele . Kulana kulelizinga lengucuko lebalulekile lapho IBatho Pele itakwenta khona umtselela lobonakalako . EmaKomidi emaWadi angenta tiphakamiso ngetindzaba letitsintsa liwadi kukhansela leliWadi , nobe ngemlomo welikhansela leliWadi , kumkhandludolobha lomkhulu nobe kumkhandlu wendzawo nobe emaKomidini emkhandlu . Loku lokungetulu tinkhomba tavelonkhe letakhishwa Yindvuna emva kwekubonisana nebaPhatsiswa emaMEC etifundza tahulumende wasekhaya neSALGA . Njengobe tinkhulungwane temacala tiphenywa , ambalwa laya enkantolo . Ematsimba lakhetsekile ebashushisi kanye netinkantolo letikhetsekile kumele kusungulwe . Kutfutfukisa Kwavelonkhe akumange kube luhlelo lolunekufana , kantsi neluhlelo lwekutfutfukisa ngete lwachubeka ngalokucondzile . Ngalokunjalo , siphakamisa kutsi kube neluhlaka lolutinhlaka letinyenti lwekuletsa umjikeleto lokahle wentfutfuko , lotakwenta kutsi inchubekelembili eluhlangotsini lunye yesekele indlela leya embili kulolunye luhlangotsi . Isayensi nethekhinoloji nako kungaba nemandla ekusombulula letinye tetinsayeya letinkhulu kutemfundvo netemphilo . Tincenye letinyenti te-Afrika letingamange tibe nenhlanhla yekuba netincingo tetintsambo tetfulelwa luhlelochumano lwabomakhalekhikhini labaniketa tinhlelo letahlukahlukene . Tinsita tekufundza tetfulwa ngendlela ye-elekthroniki etindzaweni tasemakhaya letikhashane . Isayensi icedza tivimbela ekulweni tifo nasekwehliseni tindleko tekuhlanta emanti . EMaKomidi eLiwadi angatfola lwati etindzaweni letinyenti letehlukene . Sibonelo , masipala anganiketa lwati ngelinani lemindeni yendzawo , nobe eMaphoyisa aseNingizimu Afrika anganiketa lwati ngetibalo tekwandza kwebugebengu . Futsi , liKomidi leLiwadi lingenta lucwaningo ngekuvakashela imindeni kutfola lwati . Tisebenti tentfutfuko yemimango nato tingasita ekutfoleni lwati lweliKomidi leLiwadi . Kuletsa kukhula kwemnotfo lokunonophako , kutjalwa kwetimali lokusetulu kanye nekwemukelwa kwetisebenti letinyenti emisebentini . Umsebenti ngamunye kufuneka uniketwe tonkhe tinsita letidzingekako ( sib. tindleko tetimali naletinye tinsita ) letitawudzingeka kucedzisa umsebenti . Letinsita letidzingekako kufanele tichazwe kahle . Bantfu baphendvula kushayisana kwemibono ngetindlela letehlukene . Kantsi labanye bangaphendvula ngendlela lefananako ngaso sonkhe sikhatsi , kepha bangasebentisa indlela leyehlukile kungaya ngesimo sekushayisana . Injongo lemcoka yekulawula kushayisana kusombulula kuhishana ngendlela yekutsi onkhe emacembu asuke kulencabano bativela kahle ngemphumela . Loku kwatiwa ngekutsi simo se ' WIN / WIN ' . Linani lemindeni lehola imali lengephasi kwa- 1 100 ngenyanga , letfola mahhala tinsita letibalulekile . Ngabe liKomidi leLiwadi liyidlalile indzima enchubeni yekwenta tincumo temkhandlu ? Imiklamo yemmango lesezingeni lelincane njengekutfutfukisa kudlala kwelicembu lebhola noma kutfutfukisa umklamo wengadze yekutilimela , nako kudzinga timiso tekulawulwa kwemklamo kute kucinisekiswe kuphumelela kwetinhloso . Esikhatsini lesifisha , inchubomgomo idzinga kuphendvula ngekushesha nangemphumelelo ekuvikeleni imvelo iphindze inciphise imitselela yesimo selitulu . Esikhatsini lesidze , ngemasu langiwo nalacinile nekusebentisana nemave emhlaba iNingizimu Afrika ingakwati kusingatsa kugucukela kumnotfo wekhabhoni lephasi ngesivinini lesihambisana nekucelwa kwahulumende sive , ngaphandle kwekulimata imisebenti kanye nekuhwebelana . Cala ngekucocisana ngalokulangatelelwako kanye nekugongonyeka ngeCBP , yetfule nekutsi ngabe ihlangana njani nenchubo ye-IDP yamasipala , indzima yelitsimba lekufundzisa kanye neliKomidi leliwadi . Phawula emacembu etenhlalakahle lahlukahlukene emmangweni . Ungasebentisa lokucilonga kwekusimama lokufana naloku lokukulesibonelo lesingentasi . Imboni yeLwati Lwemmango- Lihhovisi lamasipala lemmango yindzawo lefanele yekutfola lwati . Kungaba sebhodini yetatiso . Kulinganisa : Imimango nobe labayimele nabo bangadlala indzima ekulinganisweni kwebatfulimisebenti labalindzelwe , kubandzakanywa kwemimango ekuniketelweni kwemisebenti kanye nasekulandzelelweni kwebatfulimisebenti . Titsatse tincumo talamacembu , bese uyabuka kutsi ngutiphi tigaba labatisebentisile kucatulula lenkinga . Likomidi LeLiwadi liletsa inguculo yekwenta ummango ube yincenye yetintfo letiphatselene nemmango , ngalendlela lena lenta Tinkhombandlela letishiwo ku-1.1.1 tibe sibonakaliso . EmaKomidi eLiwadi angasebentisa tindlelasu letehlukene kuphendvula tidzingo temmango . EmaKomidi eLiwadi angenta loku ngekulekelela nekusita imimango kutsi ikhankhase . Kunetintfo letinyenti letitawusho kutsi ingabe umklamo ungenteka nekutsi ungachubeka uhlele kute ukhone kuwenta . Kunemathuluzi labekiwe latfutfukisiwe kute ukhone kutfola kutsi yini tinhloso temklamo nekutsi utawati njani kutsi leto tintfo tiphunyelelisiwe . Labangenele tifundvo basebenta ngemacembu alabane kuya kulabasihlanu bese kuphendvulwa lemibuto lengentasi . Uma licembu lifisa kufundzelwa umbuto , bafundzele lowo nalowo mbuto ngesikhatsi , unikete onkhe emacembu kutsi acocisane ngalombuto , bese udlulela embutweni lolandzelako . Uma usebentisa lishadi leliphendvulekako niketa lelo nalelo cembu imibuto lemibili . Khumbula kutsi kungenteka kutsi kube nemacembu langetulu kwalinye lanembuto lofanako . Tehlakalo letingadala kucabana tibekiwe kulelikhasi lelilandzelako . Luhlelo Lwekutfutfukisa Lwavelonkhe luluhlaka lwelisu lelibanti . Lubeka indlela lebumbene nalephelele yekubukana nebuphuya kanye nekungalingani lokweyeme etintfweni letisitfupha letichumene naletihamba embili letifinyetwe lapha ngaphasi . Umcondvo loyinsika ku-Batho Pele ngulewekutsi ' sakhamuti silikhasimende ' . Imigomosisekelo icinisa umbono walabatfola tinsita temmango njengemakhasimende , kungabi takhamiti nje kuphela . Ngalokunjalo tisebenti tahulumende akukameli tifihle umsebenti wahulumende , kodvwa tibeke embili emakhasimende ato . Lemininingwane legcogcwe kuluhlatiyo lwemazinga emphilo isetjentiselwa kuchuba iSWOT yemacembu etenhlalakahle . Imiphumela kanye nemiphumela lelangatelelwako yalelo nalelo cembu itawufinyetwa eshadini leliphendvulekako . Watini ngemaKomidi emaWadi ? Kulingana kuphatselene nekuphatsa bantfu ngekufana ngaphandle kwekutihlupha ngemiphumela . Kubhekise kulingana kwemphatfo ekusebentisananeni , emanani noma timfundziso . Kulingana kungaholela ekungalinganini kulawo macembu ebantfu lebebabekeke esimeni lesibucayi yindlela yekwenta tintfo lehluleka kunaka timo nekucabanga kwabo . Imphatfo lelinganako inekucabanga kutsi bantfu banemalungelo ekuba setimweni tekuhlalisana letifanako , umholo , netimo tekusebenta tebafati nemadvodza . Kwaze kwabekwa kutsi ngutiphi tinsita lekumele tengetwe nobe titfutfukiswe , tikhatsi letikhanyako netinhloso kumele takhiwe , khona masipala atoncuma tindlela letikahle tekufinyelela kuleyo migomo . Kumele ancume kutsi ngutiphi tinsita - temafa , imphahla yekusebenta , nobe emakhono - letidzingekako kufinyelela kulemigomo . Tibonelo temiphumela lekhombisa kutsi bululi bebubekelwe : ( a ) kukhula kwetinombili tebulili lobunganakwa bachubeke nesikolo ; ( b ) Kukhula kwematfuba ebesifazane ekutsatseni tincumo tekusetjentiswa kwemnotfo emakhaya ; ( c ) Kutsi besilisa nebesifazane bahlanganyele ngekulingana ekulwulweni kweminotfo yamdzabu . Khombisa kubona nekucondzisisa imiva yalomunye yeinftukutselo . Khumbula , kulungile inftukutselo . Kutjala imali kutekutfutsa tesive , lokutawuzuzisa emakhaya lahola kancane ngekwenta kutsi abe netintfo tekuhamba . Chaza kutsi inchubo yeCBP idzinga kutfutfukiswa kweLisu leliwadi njengobe Lisu leliwadi liluthuluzi lekucinisekisa kutsi imibono nabocalangaye betakhamuti kuyafakwa ku-IDP . Ngesikhatsi salomsebenti lolandzelako kuchutjwa tinkhulumo-luhlolo nebaphakeli betinsita kutsi kutohlolwa umtsamo webaphakeli betinsita labaphawulwe ngesikhatsi semsebenti lowengcile kutsi bafake ligalelo ekusebentiseni , kuhlola tinkinga labahlangabetana nato , kanye nekubafaka kunchubo yekuhlela . Loku kutawusita ekwakheni emasu lanembako nalatawuphumelela . Khumbula kuhlela letinkhulumo-luhlolo kusenesikhatsi lesihle . Kuchumana kancono , kwetsembeka nekutitfoba kwalabo labasetikhundleni kutawusita kakhulu ekwakheni ummango lokwati kusombulula tinkinga ngekubambisana nangekuthula . Tinhlelo temiklamo angeke tiphumelele nangabe imibono yalabasikati mayelana nekwakhiwa kanye nekucaliswa kwalemisebenti ingakatfolakali . Umsebenti 6 Beka embili tidzingo temmango wakho , khuluma ngetindlela tekwenta siciniseko kutsi tingenile ku-IDP . Lona ngumsebenti welicembu nelinani lelitsite lebahlali labamele ummango wonkhana lokufaka ekhatsi kudvweba nobe kutfutfukisa libalave . Tiniketeni ema-awa lamabili mayelana nemsebenti wekuhleleka kwelibalave . Timphendvulo tingase tifake ekhatsi : Kweswelakala kwekwesekela kwemmango kanye / nobe kwamasipala , umhlangano wekuhlelela kwangaphambilini uyahlelwa kantsi labangenele tifundvo abafiki , kweswelakaka kwemitfombolusito kutsi ummango nebachubisifundvo beliwadi bachube inchubo ngalokufanelekile . Umholi - Umchubi uyakhombisa alawule inchubo , aletse luhlelo emhlanganweni nobe inchubo , aphindze ente siciniseko ngemiphumela . Sigaba 2.3.2 se Siphakamisomtsetfo sa1998 sitsi kutfutfukiswa kwentsandvo yelinyenti kuhulumende wasekhaya kumele kubonwe njengendzima lebalulekile kuwowonkhe hulumende wamasipala . Sichaza imigomo lemine yekutibandzakanya , lokufaka ekhatsi kuvumela takhamiti , ngamunye nobe emacembu lamele lokutsite , afake sandla epolitikini yemmango nebamukeli betinsita babeneluvo kulendlela lekwetfulwa ngayo tinsita . Sigaba semmango yindzawo lapho khona takhamiti tingatibandzakanya ekutsatseni tincumo kugucula timondzawo lapho bahlala khona , basebentise baphindze belule emalungelo entsandvoyelinyenti . Yonkhe imitsetfo lesekelako ibhalwe naloku engcondvweni . Loku kusho kutsi emalunga eliKomidi leLiwadi kumele agcine lemibono engcondvweni umabacabanga ngekutsi batifeza njani tindzima tabo njengeliphayiphi lekuchumana emkhatsini kwemkhandlo kanye netakhamiti emmangweni wabo . Imphumelelo yalenchubo yesekeleke ezingeni leliphakeme lekubandzakanyeka kwemalunga ewadi ekuhleleni kwewadi . Loku kutawuniketa litfuba emmangweni lekutsi uchube tinchubo tawo tekuhlela esikhatsini lesitako , kube kuncishiswa kuncika kakhulu kubachubisifundvo bangephandle . IKhansela yeliWadi iba ngusihlalo weliKomidi leliWadi . Angamcela lolilunga leliKomidi lonebalandzeli labanyenti , nobe lilunga lanobe nguliphi liwadi kutsi lihole umhlangano esikhudleni sakhe . Yini luhla lweliphakelo lwetimali ? Ephepheni lekubhalatindzaba , bhalani luhla lwemacembu lehlukene emmango lekumele afakwe ekhatsi , ikakhulu lawo lahle anganakekelwa . Kukhohlisa - umkhandludolobha nobe inhlangano ' yenta shangatsi ' ibonisana nemmango kute itokwati kwenta luhlelo lolutsite lube semtsetfweni ngaphandle kwekutsi kube khona kubonisana mbamba . Ngekwesibonelo , inhlangano nobe inkampani nobe umkhandlu utsi ubonisene nemmango nekutsi ummango uvumile kantsi lokwentekile ngukutsi bantfu bavele batjelwa nje kutsi kunesehlakalo lesitsite lesentekako . Lamuhla tisebenti ( letineminyaka yebudzala leli-15 kuya ema-64 ) tenta emaphesenti langema-64 ebantfu bonkhe , lapho incenye letsite yebantfwana kanye nalabadzala babelana ngalokuncane . Emhlabeni wonkhe , timo tekubekwa kwebantfu letinjengaleti tivame kweyanyaniswa nekwenyuka kwemiholo , kukhula ngekushesha kwelizinga lekukhicita , konga lokusetulu kanye nemazinga ekuphila lanyukako . Encenye tingaholela esimeni lesikhungatsekisanako nalesicedza emandla lapho bantfu labasha bangakwati kutfola umsebenti , afake sandla eludlameni , ebugebengwini nasekungangasebentisini kahle tjwala netidzakamiva kanye naletinye tintfo letingakalungi enhlalweni . Umtselela wemphumelelo ngukutsi live lingakhona yini kubophela ndzawonye buhle bekuba nelinyenti lebantfu labasha labakwati nalabatimisele kusebenta . Kwenta njalo kusho kubanika imfundvo nemakhono nekusita labayekela sikolwa kutsi batfole umsebenti lovusa lutsandvo lwekuwenta nalatawukwati kufezekisa tinshisekelo tabo ngawo . Umkhandlu nelikhansela leliwadi batiphendvulela kanjani ? Kukhomba tidzingo - kwenta lucwaningo nobe kuhlatiya tidzingo kukhomba tintfo letibalulekile emmangweni mayelana nentfutfuko , liphakelotimali nekwetfulwa kwetinsita . Enteke - ngabe lelicophelo lingenteka ngetisebenti letikhona etikweni , libenemaciniso uma kubukwa kusebenta kwamanje nalokwendlulile . Kuphindze kube nendzawo yemikhukhu leyacala eminyakeni cishe lesihlanu lendlulile . Kulendzawo emanti aphuma etimpompini temmango kantsi kunetimpompi letintsatfu ngetawo wonkhe lommango . Linyenti letakhamuti kulendzawo lisebenta etimbonini letingakahleleki kahle kantsi labanyenti bebasebenta emapulazini badzimate batjelwa kutsi bahambe . Akunatikolo kulendzawo . Loluhlu lwekuhlola imphahla kungadzinga kutsi luhlelelwe kutsi lufaneleke nendzawo lapho leCBP ichutjwa khona ( sib. edolobheni , emaphandleni njll . ) . Letinyatselo letilandzelako titsatfwa nelicembu lelifanako lebantfu labangafika ku-12 . Ticala ngekulungiswa kwesitatimende semgomo macondzana nalowo nalowo nalowo mgomo wekusebenta . Lomsebenti utawentiwa ngemacembu lamancane , lelo libe linelilunga leliKomidi leliwadi kanye nebantfu labayimitfombolusito labafanele nebaphakeli betinsita . Kute kwetfulwe loluhlelo ngemphumelelo , lelive lidzinga kusebentisana kuwo wonkhe ummango kute kufezekiswe inhloso lefanako . Kwanyalo , iNingizimu Afrika inemazinga lasetulu ekungatsembani emkhatsini webadlalindzima labakhulu . Umjikeleto wekwakha kwetsembana nekuhlanganyela etinkhulumeni kute kubukanwe netinsayeya letinyenti kuyadzingeka - loyo lotsatsa umbono wesikhatsi lesidze . Tibekhona tindlela letehlukile ? Uma kunjalo betehlukene njani , yini futsi labayizuzile ? Usebentisa liphepha leluhlatiyo lwemazinga etemphilo leligcwaliswe ngesikhatsi semsebenti lowengcile cela labangenele tifundvo kutsi bente lithebula lelifana naleli lelingentasi . Kubona ngeliso letebulili kufanele kufakwe Kuluhlaka Lwekusebenta lolwakhelwe luhlolo lwemsebenti letindzaba letilandzelako kufute tilandzelwe , futsi lapho kudzingekile khona tibikwe kusetjentiswe tibalo ngekutsi bafati noma madvodza . Loku kutawucinisekisa kutsi kuyafinyelelwa ekuhloleni ngalokugcwele imiphumela yalaluhlelo . Kukhula nelutjalomali kwesikhatsi lesidze kudzinga umbononchanti lofanako , kwetsembeka nekubambisana emkhatsini wemabhizimisi , tisebenti nahulumende . Lamuhla , lizinga lekwetsembana liphasi , budlelwane betisebenti buyetfusa ( ngalesinye sikhatsi buneludlame ) . Akubonakali kutsi umnotfo utawugucuka ngendlela lekudzingeka ngayo umsebenti lomnyenti uma ngabe letimo tiyachubeka . Kukhutsata kukhula nekwakhiwa kwemisebenti lokunonophako kusho kubukana ngco naletimo tekungevani ngendlela letsembekile nalevulekile . Hulumende wentsandvo yelinyenti ukhetfwa bantfu elukhetfweni lolufaka wonkhe umuntfu , lolutimele nalolungavuni lcala lokuyintfo leyentiwa ngekuvota lokuyimfihlo . Niketa lwati umkhandlu lolubuya kUmmango , uma sebabuyeketile kutsi tindleko tasetjentiswa njani . EmaKomidi eLiwadi kungenteka angasebenti ngekocondza ngco nemisebenti yemeya , kepha njengemuntfu lobheke wonkhe umsebenti wemkhandlu , emalunga eKomidi yeLiwadi angenta siciniseko kutsi imeya iyatiswa ngetindzaba temmango . Yetama kubona kutsi loinftukutselo kucondziswe kuwe njengemuntfu . Labanyenti bantfu labakwatile bebanaleyo miva ungakefiki wena . Kungenteka ube sendzaweni lengakafaneli ngesikhatsi lesingakafaneli . Umhlangano ubitwe likhansela leliwadi neLiKomidi leLiwadi kukhuluma ngemklamo lophakamisiwe kutsi ufakwe ku-IDP lelungiswako . Lamanye emalunga emmango afuna umtfolamphilo wakhiwe lakukhona indzawo lenkhulu yemikhukhu , takhamiti temikhukhu atinayo imali yekugibela baye esibhedlela nobe leminye imitfolamphilo lekhashane nendzawo . Lelinye licembu letakhamiti lifuna i-IDP ifake kutfutfukiswa kwerenki yemakhumbi ngoba ayinato tindlu tangasese nobe indzawo yalabatsengisako . Licembu lesitsatfu lifuna kutfutfukisa lababutsa tibi kutsi bÃªte kabili ngeliviki edolobheni ngoba tibi tiyandza etitaladini . Emhlanganweni kuba nekukwatelana ngalinye lalamacembu litsi umklamo leliwufunako awubekwe phambili . Kubalulekile kutsi hulumende wentsandvo yelinyenti alondze emalungelo emuntfu ngamunye latfolakala kuMtsetfosisekelo . Imigomosisekelo ye Batho Pele icinisekisa kutsi luhlelo lweluhlelobusha lwemsebenti wahulumende kute uphendvule kutidzingo temmango luphindze lufeze nemalungelo abo . Ngekwenta loku imigomosisekelo iphindze yente kutsi kube nentsandvo yelinyenti eNingizimu Afrika . Kuhlela lokubandzakanyako nobe lokutinte eMmangweni kuhlomisa imimango kutsi isebentisane futsi ibukane-ngco netindlela letifanele tekulwa nebuphuya emimangweni futsi kumele kuholele kubuholi baSekhaya lobunconotiwe kanye nalamanye emasu etikhungo netinsita . Labangenele tifundvo bacabanga ngekutsi ngabe tindzaba letisembili teLisu leliwadi kumele kube ngutiphi . Rekhoda timphendvulo . Kutibandzakanya kwemmango kwenteka emazingeni lahlukene . Loluhlala lucondzise ' emazingeni lehlukene Ekutibandzakanya ' lasungulwe ngu Sherry Arnstein ( 1969 ) . Lamazinga akhombisa kutsi ungakhetsa sinye sinyatselo ngesikhatsi sinye . Licembu lelibanti lemmango liyahlangana cishe ema-awa lamabili , mhlawumbe ngeMgcibelo ntsambama , nobe uma kulungele labo labangenele tifundvo . Lelicembu litobuyeketa umbono , libeke bocalangaye bemigomo mayelana nalelo nalelo nalelo chinga lemgomo , tiphakamiso tetikhwama-mali tekutikhetsela kanye netetfulo ku-IDP . Kubalulekile kutsi yonkhe lemininingwane yendlalwe eshadini leliphendvulekako . Uma ninayo imitfombolusito lemininingwane ingathayishwa bese ikopelwa . Incenye lenkhulu yeluhlelo imayelana nekuhlelwa kabusha kwetikhungo lokudzingekako kute kuncotjwe butsakatsaka bemkhakha wahulumende , ikakhulukatilapho tinhlaka tahulumende tingakhoni khona kuhlangabetana netibopho tato kumimango lephuyile . Letiphakamiso timayelana nekutfutfukiswa kwetimphawu letidzengekako kute kwesekelwe loluhlelo . Kwacha emandla etikhungo kutsatsa sikhatsi nemtamo . Sehluko lesimayelana nekwakha umbuso lokhonako nalotfutfukisako sinika tinkhomba lokumele tilandzelwe . Tikhungo titfutfuka ngenca yekufundza lokuchubekako kanye netinyatselo tekukhula ; kubukana netinkinga letijulile , kutisombulula kanye nekuya kulokulandzelako lokusembili eluhlwini . Loku kudzingakuphatsa lokukahle , kutibophelela ekusebenti lokusetulu , kugcila ekutiphatseni lokungahlehleli emuva kanye nekutimisela kufundza kuloko losekwentekile . UMBUTO 3 Unalo yini liphakelo-timali lenyanga ? Letimphendvulo leti tingasebenta ngaletinye tikhatsi nobe tindzawo . Kepha esikhatsini lesinyenti , tivala kulalela futsi ticedza emandla kulabanye . Tisho kutsi : awulunganga ngalokwanele , awukahlakaniphi , awukacini ; Ngimi lowatiko . UMBUTO 6 Tisetjentiswa njani ? Ngubani lotisebentisako ? Ngabe nitawuliphakamisa njani Lisu leCBP ? Indzima yeliKomidi leliWadi iphindze ifake kusita nekusekela imitamo yemimango yekufezekisa tinhloso temisebenti yesikhashana lehlele kuyenta ngekwayo . Emacembu ekusebenta nobe emakomidi angazuza ngelwati lolusisekelo lwekulawula umsebenti wesikhashana . INingizimu Afrika idzinga baholi kuwo wonkhe ummango kutsi basebente ngekubambisana . Njengobe kusuka elubandlululweni bekusisombululo sekuncoba kanye kunekutsi kube ngumzabalazo wemandla wesikhashana , imphi yekulwa nebuphuya nekungalingani itakuba netinzuzo kuwo wonkhe umuntfu - lomnyama nalomhlophe , lophuyile nalonjingile . Nakubukwa umlandvo wangaphambili wekwehlukana kulelive , baholi ngalesinye sikhatsi bamela tikhundla letimele tinshisekelo letimfisha netesikhatsi lesifisha ngekutsatsela luhlelo lolubanti nelwesikhatsi lesidze . Kubalulekile kucedza lomjikeleto , nebaholi labatimisele nalabakwatiko kutsatsa sibopho lesikhulu sekulungisa tinsayeya teNingizimu Afrika . Kulalela ngekutimisela nguletinye yetintfo letimcoka kakhulu etinhlangotsini tekuchumana . Bantfu badzinga kuva kutsi beviwe futsi bacondzisiswa . Loku kudzinga kulalela ngeluvelo . Kulalela ngeluvelo kusho kubona live ngemehlo alomunye umuntfu . Kufaka ekhatsi kulalela ngekucondzisisa nekuva imiva emva kwemagama . Sehluko 3 sesekelwe kuKuhlela lokutinte eMmangweni kanye ne-IDP , iNkhomba 2 : INkhomba yebaChubisifundvo bekuHlela lokutinte eMmangweni kanye neNkhomba yebaTsatsi betiNcumo letfutfukiswe be-AICDD nemiSebenti yekuTfutfukisa . Ngakulolunye luhlangotsi , kushayisana kungakha bunye belicembu ngekucacisa kungeva kahle nekucacisa tinkholo . Kungaba sisekelo sengucuko , kungakha nebudlelwane lobusha , ngesikhasti banftu batfola , nekufundza kutsi yini imbangela yekushayisana . Imiklamo ingumjikeleto ngendlela ingayo ngako-ke idzinga kuhlala ihlolwa ibuye ihlelwe kabusha ngalesikhatsi yentiwa . Lesilulumagama sekulawulwa kwemklamo singagucula kuye ngemchubisifundvo lowenta umsebenti . Emakomidi emawadi amele tifiso temimango emiklameni letsintsana nayo futsi kufanele kutsi badlale inzima lenkhulu kulenchubo . Letinchubo tekusebenta tekulawulwa kwemklamo tibaluleke kakhulu emiklameni lemincane nalemikhulu ngalokulinganako . Kutfunywa kulikhono leliyinsika ekuphumeleleni kwe Batho Pele lapho bonkhe baphatsi netisebenti kumele bevisise . Kubaphatsi kusho kuniketa emandla abo kulabanye kute bakwati kwenta ngekutimela bangeyami kumphatsi , kodvwa kuphendvula uma kunetinkinga kusala nemphatsi . Umsebenti wekucinisekisa kutsi bantfu baba nemakhono kanye nekucecesha lokungiko usala nemphatsi . Kusisebenti loku kusho kuhlonyiswa , litfuba lekusebenta ngekutimela , kukhutsata kutetsemba encenye kuphindze kunikete ematfuba ekutfutfuka emsebentini . Tinhlelo tetenhlalakahle kumele telulwe , nemfundvo kanye nekuceceshwa kwetisebenti tetenhlalakahle kubuyeketwe nekwelekelelwa ngetimali kwetinhlangano letingasebenteli inzuzo . KUBUYEKETA KUSEBENTA NJALO NGEMNYAKA ; Umkhandlu kumele ubike ngetikhatsi letibekiwe eMakomidini eLiwadi nemimango ngeliphakelo-timali nekubuyeketwa kwekusebenta , njengencenye yemihlangano nemimango . Umangabe ikomidi yakho ingatfoli umbiko njalo njalo njalo lobuya kumkhandlu , yatisa imeya kutsi liKomidi leLiwadi libheke kusebenta lokuncono lokuvela kuhulumende wasekhaya wentsandvo yelinyenti . Kweluleka hulumende nebalingani kutenhlalo mayelana nekwetfulwa kweluhlelo . Linani leliphakelo-timali lamasipala lelisebente ekwenteni luhlelo lwemakhono asemsebentini . Hulumende ubeka indlela yekutiphatsa yawo wonkhe ummango . Uma ngabe inkhohlakalo ibonakala yemukelekile kuhulumende , itakuba nemtselela endleleni ummango lotiphatsa ngayo . Loku kwenta kubaluleke nakakhulu kutsi hulumende atsatse tinyatselo tekulungisa emazinga lasetulu enkhohlakalo etikhundleni takhe . UMBUTO 1 Yini injongo yekulalelwa kweliphakelo-timali ? Kuvisisa tebulili nekwenta luhlatiyo lolusisekelo ngetebulili kumathulusi labalulekile ekutfutfukisa Emakomidi Emawadi . Awudzingi nekutsi ute ube sikhulumeli senkhululeko nekulingana kwalabasikati kute usebentise luhlatiyo lwetebulili . Wonkhe muntfu losemmangweni losebentela intfutfuko , nalonesifiso sekwenta ncono timphilo tebantfu , kufanele akwati kusebentisa lamathulusi ekuhlatiya ngetebulili . Ngekwati kutsi besifazane , ikakhulukati labasesigabeni 15 kuye ku-24 ngeminyaka , basengotini lenkhulu yekutfola ligciwane le HIV ne AIDS , imiklamu netinhlelo temmango kufanele ikunakisise loku . Emaphepha emcondvo angulahlolako , kepha kumele anikete imininingwane leyenele kutsi masipala avisise kutsi umklamo uyini kanye nekutsi ngabe ufanele kutsi unakisiswe . Kwaze kwabekwa kutsi ngutiphi tinsita lekumele tengetwe nobe titfutfukiswe , tikhatsi letikhanyako netinhloso kumele takhiwe , khona masipala atoncuma tindlela letikahle tekufinyelela kuleyo migomo . Kumele ancume kutsi ngutiphi tinsita - temafa , imphahla yekusebenta , nobe emakhono - letidzingekako kufinyelela kulemigomo . LiKomidi LeliWadi lingenta luhlolo lwemnyaka lwekuhlola kwenetiseka kute libasite ekwenteni umsebenti wabo . luhlolo kumele luphatfwe ngemalunga EliKomidi LeliWadi ewadini ngaphansi kweliso lelikhansela leliWadi nangekusitwa ngumasipala kutekuphatsa . Timo temsebenti letilungiswe yiKhomishini tiphakamisa kutsi linyenti lemisebenti lemisha kungenteka liniketwe emabhizimisi alapha ekhaya , kanye netimbonini letincane naletisemkhatsini . Njengobe imisebenti ingakheki ngco etimbonini letitfumela imphahla ngaphandle , imikhakha lehwebelana nemave emhlaba ivame kuba nemandla ekuvusa kulandzelwa kwemkhicito . Nakubukwa lizinga leliphasi lekonga eNingizimu Afrika kanye nesidzingo sekusisa ngelizinga lelisetulu , kubalulekile kukhulisa umkhicito lotfunyelwa kulamanye emave kanye nekwandzisa umkhicito kuleyo mikhakha . Umlandvo wekuhweba weNingizimu Afrika awukafezekisi nayinye yaletinjongo kuleminyaka leli-15 leyengcile . Kuchubekela embili kutabe kusho kucinisa kuba khona kwalelive emaveni emhlaba emikhakheni lencintisanako , kube kwakhiwa sakhiwonchanti kanye nemakhono ladzingekako . Bani nesiciniseko kutsi emakhansela ayayati imimango yawo , bayayivakashela kaningi , balalele tinkinga netidzingo temmango . Luhlu lwesicinisekiso lolungentasi lungasita ekuhleleni kucocisana nemmeleli webaphakeli betinsita njengobe lemininingwane itawabelwa nalabanye . Kuphawulwa kwetinyatselo leticinile naletiphatsekako kusinyatselo lesimcoka . Loku kungafaka ekhatsi imisebenti lapho ummango ubandzakanyeka-ngco khona ; nobe imisebenti lengasekelwa ngetikhwama-mali tekutikhetsela etimalini letivela kumasipala . Bhala ligama ' kushayisana ' eshadini lelikhulu , bese utjela babambi lichaza bacabange ligama lelichamuka emcondvweni wabo lekucala uma beva ligama ' kushayisana ' . Timphendvulo letinyenti ngeke tibetinhle . Bakhombise kutsi kushayisana kwemibono akukubi ngaso sonkhe sikhatsi . Kungaba lihlahlandlela lengucuko , kusente sicabange ngetintfo lesingatikhetsa nekutsi sentanjani . Insalela kulawula lokushayisana kwembono . Kukhuluma ngemdlandla nobe ingcondvo levulekile - lomuntfu lona utsakasela imibono lemisha netiphakamiso , ulalela ngekutimisela , akehluleli , uyakwati kutsatsa sincumo , uneletsemba , wenta bantfu bakhululeke . Kufanele kubhalwe phansi emagama alabo labakhona emhlanganweni . Ikhansela yamasipala ingalibhidlita likomidi leliWadi nalehluka kufeza imigomo lelibekelwe wona . Kwesibili , ngekucinisekisa kutsi labangenele tifundvo kunchubo yeCBP bamelelwe kumicimbi ye-IDP ngaphasi kwetakhiwo netinchubo letivele tiniketwe indzawo kundlela ye-IDP lecuketfwe kuMculu weNkhomba ye-IDP , ikakhulukati kusiGungu sekuMelela se-IDP kanye nematsimba ekusebenta emiklamo . Kunika ummango lwati netimphendvulo nekucela ummango kutsi ufake sandla ngulomunye wemisebenti yelilunga leKomidi yeLiwadi . Loku kungabita kutsi lilunga leKomidi yeLiwadi likhulume emhlanganweni . Kwetfula inkhulumo emhlanganweni kungaba sehlakalo lesikhatsatako , ikakhulu uma ngabe loku kudzinga kutsi lowetfulako asebentise imishina lenjengema overhead projector nobe imibhobho yekukhuluma . Kunesidzingo lesibalulekile sahulumende welubambiswano kanye nekubambisana kwetimboni . Lemibandzela yakhelwe kwenta siciniseko sendzawo yetigungu levumela kwetfulwa kwetakhiwonchanti tamasipala , letakhela etingungwini indlela yekubambisana . Kubuyeketwa kwekusebenta kwemnyaka : Umkhandlu kumele ubike njalo EmaKomidini Emawadi nasemimangweni ngekubuyeketwa kwemcombelelotimali nangekusebenta , njengencenye yemihlangano yemmango . Uma liKomidi lakho lingatfoli njalo umbiko wekusebenta loveka kumkhandlu wakho , yatisa sodolobha kutsi LiKomidi LeliWadi lakho lilindzele kusebenta lokuncono kuhulumende wasekhaya wentsandvo yelinyenti . Ibhodi yemincele yaMasipala yimboni lenemagunya letimele lekamba iminyele yamasipala . Lelidolobha linetimboni letimbalwa kakhulu kantsi ligcwele emalunga emmango lamanyenti lasebenta emapulazini . Kunelizinga lelisetulu lekweswelakala kwemsebenti . Kunemapulazi lamatsatfu lanebanikati labahlanganyele kantsi basebenti bakulawo mapulazi batfola litfuba lekwabelana ngenzuzo . Ngabe imisebenti leyentiwa kuloluhlelo ikhonile kucinisa kuhlanganyela kwabomake kutsi batfole iminotfo / tinsita ( ( ( imfundvo , kuceceshwa , timali nalokunye ) ? Nekwabobabe ? Kulandzelela inchubekelaphambili yemsebenti wesikhashana kubakulekile kucinisekisa kutsi lomsebenti uchubeka ngendlela lefanele nekutsi tikhubato letinsha nobe tingucuko tiyabonwa tiphindze tinakekelwe esigabeni sekusebenta lesilandzelako . Emacembu lenta umsebenti wesikhashana asebentisa tinkhomba tekufezeka kwesmebenti kulandzelela inchubekelaphambili . Tinkhomba lizinga leliphokophelwe lelikhombisa kutsi tinhloloso tifezekile . Ngalesinye sikhatsi Tihlaka tekuhlela indlela yekusebenta tibita tinkhomba ngekutsi ' tinkhomba leticinisekiseka ngeliso lekungakhetsi ' . Tinkhomba tidzinga kuba nguletifanele , letenetisako , leticacile , letikalekako , letongako naletitfolakalako . Kumela ummango etinkhundleni tekubonisana - LiKomidi leLiwadi kumele libenelwati lwesikhatsi samanje ngetindzaba temmango , litiphakamise letintfo etinkhundleni tekubonisana . Iminotfo yemave ase-Afrika lamanyenti ikhule ngesivinini lesikhulu kulomnyakalishumi lowengcile , yanciphisa kakhulu buphuya kwekucala esikhatsini lesisigamu semnyakalikhulu , kantsi nelivekati litentele kutsi libe nelivi lelivakalako etinkhungweni temhlaba . Cedzela ngesifundvo seliklasi lesitsatselwe ethebulini lelikhasi 90 . Lithebula liniketa eMakomidi eLiwadi luhla lwetintfo tekuhlola labangatibukisisa nalabangatisebentisa kukhankhasa emmangoni . Kutfola lokungenani 20 0 MW agezi lophindze usetjentiswe nga-2030 , kungenisa gezi lovela kulamanye emave kulesigodzi , kuyeka kusetjentiswa kwesiphehlagezi lesingema-11 0 MW lesesisidzala kutjalwe kusiphehlagezi lesisebenta ngalokuphumelelisako . Bani neluvelo nemuntfu nobe licembu lokhuluma nalo nesihloko lokhuluma ngaso . Sibonelo , labanye bantfu abakhululeki ngekukhuluma ngendzaba lefana ne HIV ne AIDS , ngakoke lendzaba idzinga kukhulunywa ngebunono . Tinkhomba letibalekako ngelinani ticondzene netinombolo nemaphesenti ebesifazane nebesilisa noma tinhlangano lahlanganyela noma latsintsekako kulelo nalelo-cembu . Tinkhomba letibalekako tisuselwa etinhlelweni nemibhalo lehlukanisa bulili , yaphindze yahlolwa nakusentiwa luhlelo lwemsebenti lomkhulu . Kubakhona kwelwati ngebunganani betintfo nakusacalwa , kutakwenta kutsi tinkhomba tivele ticondzane-ngco . Kubekisa nje : Bomake bakha 33% wemalunga elikomidi lemantsi nakuphela umnyaka wesibili . Ngabe tinkhombandlela tiyimitsetfo yini ? Tihlahla tenhloso tilithuluzi lelilusito lelibuka tinhloso , kunetinkinga kute kutfutfukiswe luhlelo lwemklamo . Sihlahla senkinga siyaguculwa sibe sihlahla senhloso ngekugucula yinye yetimbangela ibe sitatimende lesivumako . Bubanti , luhlelo lwemsebenti kanye nekulandzelela kugucula kwetindleko : Kulandzelela tingucuko kuwo wonkhe umklamo . ' Kwenaba kwebubanti ' kwenteka uma kuba netingucuko letincane letinyenti letiholela ebubantini lobuhluke kakhulu kuloko bekulindzelekile futsi kuvamise kuba yimbangela yekungaphumeleli kwemklamo . Esikhatsini lesinyenti kubalulekile kutsi unciphise tintfo tibe ngulelinani lelihleliwe . Ekupheleni kwaleseshoni yalowo nalowo mphumela lobekwe njengacalangaye kutawuba nelicoco lemininingwane lehlanganiswe kabusha letawusetjentiselwa kuhlela . Hulumende wasekhaya ubukene netinsayeya letinyenti , letifaka ekhatsi kubate kwemakhono , tinhlelo tekuphatsa letibutsakatsaka , kungenelela kwetembusave lokungadzingeki ekutsatfweni kwetincumo temisebenti netekuphatsa , kanye nemandla emgcinimafa langalingani . Ikhomishini ikholwa kutsi ngekhatsi eluhlakeni lweMtsetfosisekelo , kusenesikhala sekwabelana ngalokufanako kwemandla nemisebenti nesekwehlukanisa kwekutsi tintfo letihamba embili letitfutfukisako titawetfulwa kanjani . Kute kutfolakale loku , kudzingeka emasu esikhatsi lesidze , lafaka ekhatsi kubukana nekubate kwetisebenti , kuvumela tindlela tetikhungo tekuhlola kanye nekusebenta ngekubamisabana nahulumende wavelonkhe kanye newesifundza . Nakayokhona utjelwa kutsi akasiso sakhamuti saseNingizimu Afrika ngako akanalo lilungelo lekukhonona . Kwenta lucwaningo ngetindzaba letibalulekile letitsintsa intfutfuko yesikhatsi lesidze . Ngemuva kwekuhlola emanotsi esifundvo kusukela emakhasini 65 kuya ku-67 bachatele kutsi kulomsebenti batawusebentisa imininingwane labayigcogce kuluhlatiyo lwemazinga emphilo kutsi bachube iSWOT yemacembu etenhlalakahle . Imiklamo angeke itinake tisusa tebungoti letifaka ekhatsi bulili , kungalingani ekuhlaleni kwebantfu kanye netindlela lesetakhekile ngekungalingani ngetebulili titawuhlala tingakanakwa . Hamba ngaphandle kwendlu uchazele bo-B kutsi abacabange indzaba labafuna kuyitjela umlingani wabo . Kungaba kuchaza lokudlile emini nobe kusihlwa , itolo entsambama , kungaba yinkinga lebavelele esikhatsini lesisandza kwendlula emsebentini , nobe ekhaya . Kutibophelela lokweyeme kusandvulelo seMtsetfosisekelo kumele kutfutfukiswe kuphindze kusetjentiswe emithantazweni yasetikolweni . Lokutibophelela kumele kubekwe kubonakale kuto tonkhe tindzawo temsebenti . Cishe kuto tonkhe tincenye temphilo , kunenchubekelembili leyentiwako yekwakha ummango lohlanganisa wonkhe umuntfu , kubuyisela emuva sitfunti semlandvo kanye nekwandzisa ematfuba . INingizimu Afrika iphumelele ekwakheni tikhungo letidzingekako embusweni wentsandvo yelinyenti nalogcugcutela ingucuko . Umtsetfosisekelo uvikela kuhlonishwa kwemalungelo uphindze ube nembononchanti wentsandvo yelinyenti lenenchubekelembili , lengabandluli ngekwebuhlanga , lengabandlululi ngekwebulili naleyebantfu bonkhe . Kupholisa emanceba esikhatsi lesengcile nekulungisa kungalingani lokwabangwa kukhishelwa ngaphandle kwetinhlanga letitsite lokwatsatsa emakhuluminyaka kuyintfo lebalulekile kumtsetfosisekelo . Kufinyelela kutinsita kwentiwe kwaba banti , umnotfo usimeme kantsi nemmango longakhetsi ngekwebuhlanga sewucalile kubonakala . Tigidzi tebantfu lebebancishwe ematfuba ngaphambilini setiyakwati kutfola emanti , gezi , temphilo , tindlu kanye nekuvikeleka kutenhlalo . Cishe letinye tigidzi letintsatfu tebantfu tiyasebenta lamuhla nakucatsaniswa na-1994 , lizinga lebuphuya lehlile kantsi imalingena lesendzimeni leholwako ichubekile nekwenyuka ngalokubonakalako . Kulandzelela kulawulwa kwenhlekelele : Kuphendvula lokubangwa tingucuko tenhlekelele ngalesikhatsi salomklamo . Inhlekelele itawugucula noma ivele kungakalindzeleki ngesikhatsi umklamo usachubeka . Leluhlelo lekulawula umklamo kutawufuneka kutsi luguculwe ngalesikhatsi loku kwenteka , kutawubese kudzingeka kutsi umlawuli wemklamo atise bonkhe labatsintsekako . Kufinyeleleka - ngalokunjalo lamanye emalunga emmango kungenteka angafinyeleli malula kutekutfutsa kantsi uma indzawo nobe imihlangano yekubikela ummango ingafinyeleleki kamalula abakwati kuhambela umhlangano njengobe tekutfutsa tiyabita kantsi nesikhatsi sekufika endzaweni yemhlangano kungabavimbela ekutsaneni bawuhambele umhlangano . Lelithebula lelisekhasini lelilandzelako likhombisa tindlela letehlukene tekutibandzakanya teMakomidi eLiwadi etigabeni letehlukene tenchubo yekuphakela timali . Bacele kutsi bahlele lemiphumela lemitsatfu lengubocalangaye eshadini leliphendvulekako njengobe itawusetjentiswa kumsebenti lolandzelako . Leminye imitsetfo , njenge , Umtsetfo waVelonkhe weKugucula Kutfutsa Kwemhlaba ucindzetela lamanye ematiko emikhakha kutsi ahlanganise tinhlelo tawo nemiklamo kanye ne-IDP , kantsi leminye imitsetfo yemikhakha ayisho lutfo ngaloku . Kute tinkhundla tekusebentisana tahulumende nobe tinhlangano letakhelwe inchubo yekubuyeketa i-IDP . Letinkhundla letikhona letingetulu betisetjentiswa . Kwetfula tinchubomgomo letisebentako temakethe tetisebenti kanye nalokukhutsatako kwekukhulisa ematfuba emisebenti , ikakhulukati kubantfu labasha kanye nasemikhakheni lecashe bantfu labanemakhono laphasi . Kufundza kuba neluvelo akusiyo intfo yekufundza timphendvulo ' letilungile ' kepha kufundza kuba khona ngemaciniso kubo . Kubakhona kusho kuniketa sonkhe sikhatsi kulomunye umuntfu nekuva kwabo , ubeke eceleni imibono yakho , tento netehlakalo . Kubakhona kutigwema bunguwe lobunemphilo . Yati kutsi lawa ashicilelwe kuphi , wente siciniseko sekutsi emalunga emmango ayawavisisa . Indzima Yekhomishini Yemsebenti Wahulumende kuchuba tinkhambiso nemazinga kantsi kumele kuciniswe luhlelo lwekucapha kuhehwa kwetisebenti . Ngabe ngutiphi tingucuko letikhona tesikhatsi semnyaka ekusetjentisweni kwemitfombolusito ( umdvwebo wetikhatsi temnyaka ungasita lapha ) ? Kuze kufike 1970 , i-Seymour kwakuyindzawo lenemphucuko yekulima . Umnotfo wawusimiswe yinkapani yemapulango , neyekwenta lugwayi mango edolobheni . Lugwayi , emazambane netitselo betilinyelwa kutsengiswa kulendzawo . Ungatibandzakanya njani ummango ku-IDP ? KuneKomidi yeliWadi lekhutsele emmangweni wakho . Imvamisa imihlangano ibanjwa nga 6 entambama emalangeni latsite evikini . Ngesizatfu sekutsi ngemhambo bamake ngibo lababhekeke kutsi babone bantfwana baphindze balungiselele imindeni yabo kudla ngaletotikhatsi , lining labo aliphumeleli kungenela imihlangano . Labanye balobomake bayakhatseteka kutsi sebatawuhamba ngetinyawo , noma bagibele ematekisi kantsi sekumnyama . Labanye babo banetikhalo tekutsi noma bayile emihlanganweni tindzaba netinkinga letiphatselene nabo atinakwa ngalokwenele . Kantsi labanye bakhala ngekutsi emadvodza abo ayabatsetsisa , atfukutsele , abahlukubete ngekutsi baye emhlanganweni bangeti ekhaya . Kungunyalo tinkhulumo ngekutftutfukiswa kwetindzawo tekuhlala tiyachubeka emkhatsini weliKomidi lemaWadi nahulumende waSekhaya , kodvwa bomake basele ngephandle . Ngalesosizatfu , sebafuna kusungula inhlangano yabomake letawubuka loku . Bobabe abavumelani naloku , batsi akukadzingeki kutsi bomake bahlangane bodvwa , ngoba bobabe bangatetfwala tonkhe tindzaba letiphatselene nemmango . Umkhandlu lokhetsiwe yinkhundla yekugcina yekwenta tincumo mayelana neLeluhlelo LweKutfutfukisa loluBumbene . Indzima yentsandvo yelinyenti lebandzakanya wonkhe kwatisa , kukhulumisana nekuphawula ngaleto tincumo , ngesikhatsi kuhlelwa / eluhlelweni lwekwenta tincumo . Hulumende wente sincumo sekuhlangabetana netidzingo temphilo tato tonkhe takhamiti . Liphepha Lelimhophe Lekugucula Kwetfulwa Kwetinsita Nguhulumende , 1997 , liniketa sakhiwo senchubomgomo yekugucula kwetfulwa kwetinsita nguhulumende , kanye nelisu-ndlela lelingasetjentiswa . Lifuna kuletsa indlela lensha yekwetfulwa kwetinsita . Kumcoka kutejwayeta ngeMtsetfo weTakhiwo taMasipala , 1998 , neMtsetfo weTinhlelo taMasipala , 2000 , neMtsetfo waMasipala weKuhlela neKulawula 2001 . Kusebentisa imali lenyenti elutjalwenimali sinyatselo sekucala . INingizimu Afrika kumele futsi itfutfukise lizinga lekusebentisa imali ngekuhlela lokuncono , tinhlelo tekukhipha imisebenti letivakalako kanye nekucudzelana lokukhulu emnotfweni . Kunesidzingo sekusebenta kahle kakhulu kuyo yonkhe imikhakha yemali lecitfwa nguhulumende , ngobe imali yonkhe lekhona kungenteka ikhule kancane kulesikhashana lesitako . Kumele kunakwe kakhulu ekuphatfweni kwemali yemiholo yahulumende , kwentiwe imitfombolusito ibe khona kuletinye tintfo letihamba embili . Loku kutawufaka ekhatsi kulinganisa tingcindzeti letinjengekwenyuswa kwelinani letisebenti , kuholela ngalokwenele tisebenti leticeceshiwe letinemakhono kanye nekwenta ncono timbuyeketo . Ngabe umkhandlu wakho unayo iPMS ? Uyacelwa kuyichaza . LiKomidi LeliWadi lingaveta kunganetiseki ngekubhalaela lihhovisi lesikhulumi samasipala ngekungasebenti kahle kwelikhansela leliWadi . Umkhandlu ungendlulisela tibopho letitsite emaKomidini Emawadi . Liphepha lemcondvo wemklamo kumele ligcwaliswe macondzana nalowo nalowo nalowo mklamo lodzinga kwesekelwa nguhulumende , emaNGO nobe umkhakha wangasese . Leliphepha lemcondvo ligcugcutela umklamo ngekuchaza timphawu tawo futsi liphindze libe nemsebenti ekulandzeleleni inchubekelembili kanye nekuphocelela bantfu kutsi babe nekutiphendvulela . Ekuhlanganeni hola tinkhulumiswano letimayelana ne Batho Pele endzaweni yemsebenti . Buta imibuto lengentasi bese ubuka timphendvulo letikuliphephabhuku . Ngekusho kwesivumelwano , baletsi msebenti betsembisa kwetfula tinsita letitsite tamasipala , esikhundleni samasipala ngetikhatsi letibekiwe , liphakelo-timali netinhloso . Lometfuli tinsita angasebenta kwetfula tinsita kuwo wonkhe ummango nobe incenye yEMMANGO . Angasebenta kwetfula tonkhe tinsita nobe incenye yaleto tinsita . Sibonelo , inhlangano lesebenta nemmango ingenta sivumelwano sekubutsa tibi etindlini nasetitaladini , itibutsise etindzaweni lapho emaloli emkhandlu atatibutsa khona . Kutibophelela etindleleni tekukhishwa kwemisebenti yesive neyangasese letitawuheha timboni tasekhaya kwakhe nemisebenti . Kusungula nekutfutfukisa budlelwane bamasipala-ummango etinhlelweni tekwetfulwa kwetinsita . Khumbula kutsi tincumo teliKomidi leLiwadi atibopheli likhansela leliwadi . EmaKomidi eLiwadi ete emandla emtsetfo ngekutsatfwa kwetincumo ngumkhandlu . Ngakoke LiKomidi leLiwadi kumele lakhe buhlobo bekubambisana nelikhansela , lisebentise ematfuba labhalwe ngetulu , kwenta siciniseko kutsi liphimbo lemmango liyevakala . Umtsetfo sisekelo neMtsetfo weTakhiwo taMasipala neTinhlelo taMasipala umisa luhlaka lwekutsi imikhandlu yamasipala iyishaya njani imitsetfo . Indzima yeCDM mayelana nemsebenti wamasipala wendzawo ekufakeni ekhatsi i-HIV / AIDS . Kubonisana nemacembu emikhakha - Sibonelo , tinhlangano tebalimi kutfola imibono yato yetinhlelo tekwenta imakethe lensha . Imicabango nguletintfo letichamuka ngaphandle letingaba nemtselela etinhlosweni temklamo . Tintfo lesingeke sikhone kutilawula , futsi kudzingeka kutsi sitinake ngoba uma sitiyekela tingabanga kuhluleka kwemklamo . Sibonelo , uma lisuku selibekiwe lekwakha ifawundeshi yesakhiwo bese kuna imvula malanga lambalwa , loku kubanga kusalela emuva kuyo yonkhe inchubo , kodvwa akusiyo intfo lesingayilawula ngekwetfu . Ngakoke , tindlela tekwenta tintfo kudzingeka tifake ekhatsi imihambo nekungenelela kwesikhashana kutotonkhe tigaba kute kucinisekise ingucuko lehlelekile , lephelele , nalecabangisisekile . Letindlela kufanele tifake ekhatsi tinyatselo tesikhashana tekwenta tingcuko etigabeni temuntfu ngamunye , temacembu , tenhlangano kanye nasemmangweni . Emakomidi eLiwadi kumele anikwe lwati njalo njalo njalo ngekuhamba kwetimali tamasipala . ' Kuhamba kwetimali ' kuphuma nekungena kwetimali esikhwameni sasebhange setimali tamasipala . Kwengca kubonisana nekutibandzakanya kuya ekwakheni budlelwane bekulingana lobusimeme , ngekusungula budlelwane lobuchubekako , kanye nekubambisana lokunenhlakanipho lokufaka ekhatsi labanengi labadlala indzima . Tinsika teNkhomba Msebenti ( emaKPI ) titinhloso letivakalako , letikalekako tisebenti letivumile kutitfola esikhatsini lesitsite . Sisebenti ngasinye kumele sibe nenkontileka lelawula kusebenta kwaso lecuketse emaKPI . , kantsi lenkontileka ingasetjentiselwa kutsi tisebenti titiphendvulele ekwetfuleni tinsita ngekwalamaKPI . Kwakhiwa kwenchubomgomo yendlelasu nenchubomgomo yetindzawo temisebenti yeHIV ne-AIDS . Indlelasu yekuchumana - Bomasipala batfutfukisa tindlelasu tekwenta siciniseko kutsi kuchumana kucabangisisiwe , kunemasu , phindze kuyincenye yetinchubo letinyenti tamasipala . Iminyakalishumi letako , njengobe iminotfo lesacala yenyusa sabelo sayo sekuhwebelana nemhlaba kanye nelutjalomali , kuwa kwesisindvo semnotfo waseMelika , eYurophu naseJapan kutakuba nemtselela lohambisanako neligalelo kutembusave netemphi tawo lamave . Loku kungaholela ekuhlelweni kabusha kwendlela yebuncusa nekuphatsa kwemave emhlaba , kukhombise tikhungo letinsha letifaka ligalelo . Lomdvwebo lokulelikhasi lelilandzeko ukhombisa kutsi esigabeni semuntfu ngamunye , kulawula kungenelela kwekuhlukahlukana kufanele kugcile ekuboneni kutsi kwehluka kwemuntfu ngamunye kukutsintsa njani kubona kwetfu , imicondvo , tifiso , tidzingo kanye netento tekutiphatsa . Loku kutawubuketa likhono lemuntfu ngamunye lekugucula tinkholelo takhe , imicondvo yekubukelana phansi kanye nekucabanga lokungakakhelwa ecinisweni . Kungenelela kufanele kuhlelwe esigabeni selicembu khona kutovinjelwa imicondvo yekubukelana phansi nalengakakhelwa ecinisweni nekubona netikhinyabeto letitfolakala emasikweni lakhona , emigomeni , etimisweni tekusebenta nasetinchubeni letibekiwe . Tjela bo-A baphume endlini . Chazela bo-B kutsi sengibo labatawulalela . Kepha kumele balalele ngekuba neluvelo . Loku kusho kutsi kumele babuke umuntfu , babute imibuto yekucacisa , bakhombise umlingani kulalelisisa . Kugucugucuka kubalulekile ekuphumeleleni kwekubandzakanyeka kwemmango . Imimango ingatfolakala kuphela ngetikhatsi letitsite kungenteka kube nesidzingo sekwenta tinhlelo nobe setinhlelo letintjintjiwe kuye ngetidzingo tebantfu labatsintfwa ngulesosehlakalo , sib . Luhlelo Lwemkhicito nemali lengenako ebhizinisini : kuhlela kukhulisa imali lengenako yemkhicito netinsita esikhatsini lesiniketiwe .
