Bachubisifundvo kumele bacinisekise kutsi bameleli bemacembu lasebucayini bayincenye yemacembu ekusebenta kanye nekutsi banelivi kulamacembu . IMSA , 2000 yendlala tinhlelo tangekhatsi tabomasipala letitawubasita kutsi baphumelelise imigomo yeSiphakamisomtsetfo . Sigaba 74a na b seMtsetfo weTakhiwo taMasipala , 1998 sichaza imisebenti nemandla emaKomidi eLiwadi , ngekugcizelela sibopho semaKomidi eLiwadi emmangweni , kutsi atsatsele ummango tindzaba letitsite . EmaKomidi emaWadi angenta imitamo lekhetsekile kucinisekisa kutsi bafati bamelelekile emihlanganweni yekwetfula imibiko nekutsi imibono yabo iyatfolakala iphindze ifakwe ekukhulumisaneni emkhatsini welibandla lemakhansela kanye nelikhansela leli wadi . Kumele kwemukelwe indlela yekuphatsa lecondzile ekucashweni kwemazinga laphasi , netikhulu tinikwe emandla lagcwele ekucasha tisebenti ematikweni ato . Budlelwane nelikhansela leliwadi - emaKomidi eLiwadi kudzingeka akhe budlelwane bekubambisana nekusebentisana nelikhansela leliwadi labo , ngoba emakhansela eliwadi akha umkhandlu . EmaKomidi eLiwadi kumele asungule inchubo lehlelekile , yekubamba imihlangano ngetikhatsi letibekiwe nelikhansela leliwadi kutjela likhansela tindzaba temmango , ngemihlangano yeKomidi yeLiwadi , nangekwenta siciniseko kutsi imihlangano iyabanjwa kwatisa sive tintfo lotentako umkhandlu ngalesosikhatsi . EmaKomidi eLiwadi kumele aphindze ente siciniseko kutsi kutsintsana njalo njalo njalo kuhlala kukhona nelikhansela leliwadi kufaka sandla ekulawuleni kusebenta , liphakelotimali , nenchubo yeluhlelo lwekutfuftukisa lolubumbene . Chatela labangenele tifundvo kutsi ngemuva kwekutsi ummango uvumelane ngembono , kumele kuphindze kuvunyelanwe ngemigomo bese kwakhiwa nemachinga macondzana nalowo nalowo nalowo mgomo . Bukisa emanotsini esifundvo emakhasini 44 na-45 kutsi akusite . Sigaba B sabomasipala , nobe bomasipala bendzawo : laba bomasipala labanemandla lasetulu ekulawula umtsetfo babambisene nabomasipala besigaba C nobe bomasipala betigodzi . Bonkhe bomasipala bendzawo bangephansi kwamasipala wesigodzi . Noma kute budlelwane lobucondzene nesikhulumi , emalunga eKomidi yeLiwadi angatsintsana naso ngemihlangano yemkhandlu kanye netigigaba . Niketa emaminitsi langu-30 ekwenta liphakelo-timali lekusebenta lalomasipala . Kumele bakhe luhla lwetintfo letingenisa UMHOLO LEKUSEBENTA neluhla lwetintfo letakha kusetjentiswa kwemali . Kumele badvwebe lelithebula lelilandzelako eshadini leliphepha bese bayaligcwalisa . Kusuka ekucocisaneni kuya ekuhlomiseni kugcugcutela bunikati bekutfutfukiswa kwetindzawo taSekhaya kuphindze kucedze nemkhuba wekuncika . Kuceceshelwa umsebenti kwalabadlala indzima ngekufaka sandla enkhundleni yalabamelele ku-IDP , kute bente luhlelo nenchubo yekusebenta ngemphulelo . Luhlelo lwekusebentisana kwabohulumende baseNingizimu Afrika lunkimbitekile , kepha lensayeya ngete yavikelwa ngenca yekungalandzeleleki kwekwentiwa kwemisebenti . Kusungulwa kweLitiko Lekucapha Nekuhlola Kusebenta kusinyatselo lesikahle sekucinisa luchungechunge lwekutiphendvulela . IKhomishini iphindze ibite kutsi banini bemasheya emabhizimisini ahulumende nasetivumelwaneni tekusebenta letentiwa etiNdvuneni teKhabhinethi kutsi kwentiwe kwatiwe esiveni . Kwecwaya - kwecwaya kushayisana kwembono yimphendvulo lejwayelekile , letsemba kutsi uma ukwecwaya kuhishana ' kutawuphela ' . Kubhekana nekushayisana ngendlela lenhle kudzinga likhono , kutati nesifiso sekudlala indzima . Kuphika yindlela leyejwayelekile yekwecwaya kushayisana . Nobe singeva shengatsi siphendvula kahle , kwecwaya kushayisana kungaba nemphumela webantfu labakhatsatekile , labakwatile , lababuhlungu nalabanenzondo , nekutsi kungenteka kuhishane kuphindze kuvele . Loku kunemphumela wesimo sekuluza / uluze kuwo onkhe emacembu labhekene nekushayisana . Cabanga ubuyele emuva ngekukhula kwakho ukhumbule senteko lesitsite lapho wacala kubona khona kutsi kwehluka ebafaneni , uma ngabe ningemantfombatana , , nakanjalo bafana , kwakusho kutsi benibhekeke kutsi nitiphatse ngekwehluka nekutsi beniphatfwa ngendlela lehlukile . Kufanele nigcile emehlukweni locondzene nekutiphatsa , hhayi umehluko locondze nesimo semtimba . Cocela umlingani wakho lendzaba yakho . Hulumende wasekhaya kumele ancume kutsi itawusetjentiswa kanjani imali lengenako kanye netimali letitfoliwe tetinsita nemiklamo lehlose kwetfulela ummango . Loku kulukhuni kukugadza , nangabe emaphakelo etimali akakamiswa ngendlela , njengekutsi kube nemali lecondzene ngco nemisebenti ' yebesilisa ' naleyo ' yebesifazane ' noma ke ' yetebulili ' . KWENTIWA NCONO KWEKWETFULWA KWETINSITA TEMMANGO KUYACHUBEKA NEKUBA YINCABHAYI LEDZINGA KUTIBOPHETELA KWATI TONKHE TISEBENTI TAHULUMENDE LOKUHLOSE KUNGAFEZI KUPHELA TINHLOSO TAHULUMENDE KODVWA KUPHINDZE KWENETISE TIFISO TEMALUNGA EMMANGO TEKUFINYELELA ETINHLELWENI LETISEZINGENI LELISETULU KANYE NASEMPHILWENI LENCONO YAWO WONKHE UMUNTFU . AKUKHO LOKUMELE KUFAKAZELE KWEHLULEKA KUHLANGABETANA NALETIMFUNO , NJENGOBE TINGULETIFANELE NALETINESITFUNTI . Njengobe bocalangaye bacala kuvela , kungaba yintfo lenhle kumema baphakeli betinsita labahambelana nalemiphumela ekuhleleni kwelilanga lelilandzelako . Emaminitsi emkhandlu emhlangano aniketwe ummango . Kwakha simo lesivumela kuniketwa kwetinsita - ku-1.2 sikhulume ngetinkhomba tentsandvo yelinyenti kanye nemalungelo eluntfu lasisekelo . Emalungelo awahambi wodvwana kodvwa ahamba netibopho . Kukhutsata ummango kutsi utibophetele etintfweni latentako kute emalungelo lacinisekiswe Kumtsetfosisekelo Nasemculwini Wemalungelo atokhuliswa futsi akhutsatwe . Sibonelo , lilungelo lendzawo yekuhlala lecocekile nesibopho sekuba bahlali bakhokhele timali tentsela yelidolobha kute kutokwetfulwa tinsita . Kumele kuphindze kwentiwe luhlelo lwekuniketela ngetibopho nemisebenti kubantfu labatsite nekubeka tikhatsi temnyakato ngamunye . Kubuyeketa sibonelelo setindlu nekwelekelela ngetimali kute kucinisekiswe kutsi tintfo letisetjentiswako tihambisana netingucuko letikahle kunchuobomgomo yekuhlaliswa kwebantfu . Kutfutfukisa lizinga lemfundvo kudzinga kuphatsa ngekucophelela , kwesekela lokuvela kuwo onkhe emacembu lanenshisekelo kanye nesikhatsi . Ngekuya kwelucwaningo lwanga-2010 [ 1 ] lekuhlelwa kabusha kwetinhlelo temfundvo letingema-20 emahlabeni wonkhe , tindlela letivakalako ticala kukhicita imiphumela eminyakeni lesitfupha ngemuva kwekucalwa kwemitamo , nemivuzo lesimeme ibonakala ngemuva kwesikhatsi lesidze . Kuphawula tinhlangano letehlukahlukene emmangweni nekuhlelisa kubaluleka nekufinyeleleka kwetinsita tato . Loluhlelo luyayisebentisa ngalokuphelele imibona yebesilisa nebesifazane , emakhono abo , nalabangakhona kukwenta ? Nangabe tinombolo ativumi , ciniseka kwekutsi ' unelitsamo ' lebesifazane nebesilisa ( lokungenani 30 % ) . Lomsebenti ucedziswa licembu lemmango lelincane leliniketwa umtfwalo wekubhala Lisu phasi lekugcina . Licala ngesikhatsi seliviki lekuhlela kantsi kumele letame kutsi libe licedzile evikini lelilandzelako . Kulalelwa kwemibono yemmango ivamise kubanjelwa tintso letitsite . Sibonelo , kulalelwa kwemibono yemmango kumtsetfo lophakanyisiwe . Loku kusho kutsi liKomidi LeLiwadi lingumgwaco longasetjentiswa yimimango kufaka tikhalo nekuveta tindzaba nekukhomba tidzingo letitsite . EmaKomidi eLiwadi asebentela ummango , ngakoke atsatsa leto tikhalo atimikise kumkhandlu ngendlela lephumelelisa kakhulu . EmaKomidi eLiwadi akatsikameti kusebenta kwemkhandlu , loku kufaka ekhatsi kunganiketi umyaleto etisebentini letisebenta kwenta tincumo tenchubomgomo yemkhandlu . Kepha , banendzima lemcoka lekumele bayidlale yekuchumanisa emkhatsini kwemmango kanye nemkhandlu . Cinisekisa kutsi lababandzakanyekako bafaka ekhatsi baphakeli betinsita labatinte emmangweni . I-GEP inetindlela letinyenti Tekungenelela Kusita Kuhlela letitakusita kutsi wakhe tinkhombandlela tekulawula ibhizinisi yakho nekutsi ubone butsakatsaka lobungadzinga kutsi ubutsatsele tinyatselo . Ungajaki kubeka umbono wakho phambili . Mela kuva kutsi labanye bantfu bacabangani , ungabese uyawetfula wakho umbono . Bomasipala bakhipha imali lencane yekwesekela kusekelwa masinyane kwekusetjentiswa kweLisu leliwadi kute kungatolahleka umdlandla lovela kunchubo yekuhlela . Tincumo mayelana nekuphakelwa kwetimali kumele tivele kunchubo yekuhlela , inchubo yekuhlunga kumele ibe selubala kantsi nemmango kumele utfole imibiko ngemiphumela . Lomsebenti lolandzelako uchaza kutsi ngabe uliphakelotimali ungatfutfukiswa njani macondzana naletikhwama-mali teliwadi . Ikhansela yamasipala ingalibhidlita likomidi leliWadi nalehluka kufeza imigomo lelibekelwe wona . LeSehluko siniketa ngeluhlakamsebenti lokumele kuhlela lokutinte emmangweni kwenteke ngaphasi kwalo . Labangenele tifundvo batawuhlola imigomo , imiphumela lephatsekako yekusebentisa iCBP , lingemuva lemigomo kanye netinchubomgomo talendlela . LeSehluko siniketa labangenele tifundvo sisekelo sekusukumisa iCBP . Indlela yekusebenta emkhatsini wemakhansela nemalunga emaKomidi emaWadi , ingetiwancono nangabe akwati kukhulumisane ngendlela lefanele . Kusombulula-tinkinga- lena yincenye leyinselele kakhulu yenchubo yekwehlulela , ngoba kukulesigaba lesi lapho khona sisombululo kuvunyelwana ngaso . Umehluleli usita emacembu ekutfoleni emasu lakhona , kuhlela ngebumcoka tiphakamiso nekutfola sivumelwano lesijatjulelwa ngiwo onkhe emacembu . Umehluleli kungedzingeka asebentise emacebo lehlukene kwenta onkhe emacembu efike endzaweni lapho bavumelana khona ngalabakufisile . Loku kungafaka ekhatsi kuniketa emacembu litfuba lekubamba imihlangano lemifisha awodvwa , linye ngalinye , bese uyawahlanganisa , nekubhala sivumelwano lesenetisa onkhe emacembu . Ngesikhatsi selizinga lekuhlela labatibandzakanyako batawubonakala nekufundzisa lokubalulekile kwetisebenti kufanele kwenteka kute kucinisekiswe imphumelelo yekusetjentiswa kwemklamo . Kulesinye sikhatsi lilunga lelicembu lemklamo litawutfola kubalulekile kusungula licembu lekusekela kute kutfolakale imiphumela yemisebenti lebukene nabo . Sibonelo , kute ukhone kuhlela inkhofa , emalungiselelo ekuhamba kwemalunga kufanele entiwe . Umlawuli wemklamo angabese wakha licembu lekusekela lelibukene ngco nekuhamba . Lelicembu lekusekela litawuniketwa licembu lemklamo luhlu lolufinyetiwe lwetintfo letitawenteka letifaka ekhatsi tikhatsi , lokutawenteka , imisebenti kanye neliphakelotimali . . . Letinye timali tekwebolekwa ngaphandle titfolakala etimakethe tesicalo njengemabhange emabhizinisi . Labanengi bomasipala abakwati kweboleka , lokwenta kube lukhuni kutsi bangaboleka imali . Hulumende kusamele atfole tindlela tekuncoba letinkinga leti . Kuhlatiya tebulili lithulusi lelibalulekile ngoba lishabalalisa kubukelana phansi , livete emakhono lavame kunyatselwa , liphindze lente siciniseko kutsi tinhlangotsi tonkhe tekunakekelwa kwemvelo ngekwehlukana kwato tiyanakelelwa , kantsi netinhlangano letisekela ummango tigcina setatiwa ngumuntfu wonkhe . Khumbula , kumcoka kuba nenkhulumo-mibuto nalabetfula tinsita kuva imibono yabo etindzabeni letitsintsa ummango kanye netinsita tabo khona kutekuhambisana kubuye kwesekele ligalelo lelifakwa emmangweni ngendlela lefanele . Emalunga emaKomidi emaWadi kudzingeka kutsi agadze kusebentiseka kwetimali kute abone kutsi ukhona kangakanani masipala kuhlangabetana netinhlelo letise Luhlwini lweNtfutfuko leBumbene . Kukhahlameta - Umuntfu lochumana ngekukhahlameta ukholwa kutsi ' ngimi lowatiko ' , ingcondvo ivalekile , akakwati kulalela , nguye yedvwa loba nelitfuba , utenta umphatsi , ukhuluma ngeliphimbo lelisetulu , uyetfusa , akakwati kuma . EMakomidi eLiwadi anelilungelo lekubuta imibuto kutsi ' kuhamba kwetimali ' kuhlelwa njani , kulandzelelwa njani nekutsi somafa ulandzela njani nobe baphatsiswa nobe likomidi lemeya . Behlukanise badlali beme emalayini mabili ( lilayini lingeci kubantfu labalishumi , nangaba banyenti yenta emalayini abe matsatfu ) . Badlali abeme munye emva kwalomunye . Chaza kutsi utawuniketa losekucaleni umusho lekutawudzingeka awuphindze atjele lomlandzelako , naye kanjalo kute kufike kulesekugcineni . Gcizelela kutsi umlayeto utawushiwo kanye awuphindvwa . Nasebaniketene bonkhe , losekugcineni anitjele lokuvile . Ciniseka kutsi umlayeto uviwa nguloyo loniketwa lomlayeto . Badlali labanye abangeva kutsi umlayeto utsini . Imibiko yeliphakelotimali kufanele iniketwe kanyekanye ngalesikhatsi sembiko wekugadza , kubuyeketa nekuhlola . Ikhombisa kutsi umklamo usondzelene njani neliphakelotimali lokuvunyelwene ngalo nekutsi tinyatselo tekulungisa tintfo kufanele titsatfwe . Yini indlela lesetjentiswe ngumkhandlu , yini indlela lesetjentiswe ngummango ? Kahlehle luhleloluhlelo lwetinsita lulwabiwotimali . Kwaba timali kumcoka njengoba kungasho umehluko emkhatsini kweMphumelelo nekuhluleka kwemklamo . Uma liphakelotimali luluncane kuchaza kutsi leminye imisebenti angeke yentiwe . Uma tindleko tinesilinganiso lesingetulu kutawubalukhuni kutfola timali tekwenta umklamo . Nyalo-ke sikhatsi sekubona nkinga tinkinga letimcoka netihibe esimeni lesikhona , timbangela tato kufanele tivisiswe nendlela letinemtselela ngayo kuletinye tintfo . Lwati lweNingizimu Afrika lwekuchumana kwemave emhlaba lufaka ekhatsi tinzuzo letibonakalako kanye nebunkimbonkimo lobenyukile . Insayeya lekhona kusebentisa lamatfuba lavelile kube kuvikelwa bahlali baseNingizimu Afrika - ikakhulukati labaphuyile . Kwenta sibonelo , iNingizimu Afrika inelizinga lekonga leliphasi kantsi itsembele emalini levela ngaphandle kute yesekele lutjalotimali lwayo . Kweyama emalini lengenako levela ngaphandle kwenyusa ingoti yekugucugucuka emnotfweni wangekhatsi . Kukhula lokuhamba kancane emaveni latfutfukile bekuhambisana nekufuna ngemandla lokuvela emaveni lasatfutfuka , lokufaka sandla ekwemukeleni kulinganiswa futsi kwempahla yalelive letfunyelwa kulamanye emave . Kepha lenkhambiso iphindze iphose insayeya kubenti betinchubomgomo nakubakhi bemphahla , ngobe sidzingo sanyalo setimakethe letisacala sibukwa ngempahla kanye nemphahla nemkhicito longakahlutwa , kunekutsi ubukwe ngemikhicito leminyenti leyahlukahlukene ledzingwa ngemave latfutfukile . Ludzaba lolubucayi lwekutsi ingabe iNingizimu Afrika ingakwati yini kuhlanganisa bantfu labangasebenti kutsi bangene ekukhiciteleni timakethe letitfumela imphahla kulamanye emave . Labanye baphawula kutsi umnotfo awucudzelani ekwakheni lokusebenta kakhulu ngobe tindleko tisetulu kakhulu , lizinga lekutsengiselana alikasimami , sakhiwonchanti asikaneli kantsi nemakhono anemkhawulo kakhulu . Kepha iNingizimu Afrika ingacudzelana etigabeni letahlukahlukene uma kwenteka lokukhatsateka kulungiswa - kantsi encenyeni lenkhulu , tingalungiswa . Kungasimami kwelizinga lekutsengiselana kudala sivimbela sekuphumelela kantsi luhlelo luphakamisa kutsi kusombulula tindleko tetinsita tasekhaya kanye nekuba khona kwemakhono kutakuba nemtselela losimeme etindlekweni . Njengelive lelingenisa imali lesemkhatsini , iNingizimu Afrika kumele icudzelane ngalokuhamba embili ngemikhicito netintfo ledvume ngato kanye nekungena ngemphumelelo emigudvwini yekutfunyelwa kwemave emhlaba . Loku kudzinga kutibophelela lokukhulu kutelucwaningo netentfutfuko kanye netentsengiso tayo , inkhundla lefanele yekuhlelenjiswa kwetintfo kanye nebudlelwano nemave emhlaba lobuphumelelisako kutemnotfo . Kumele kwetfulwe luhlelo lwekuheha labaneticu kanye nelisu lekutfutfukisa emakhono abohulumende basekhaya kute kuheheke labafuna umsebenti labasezingeni lelisetulu . Kutfutfukisa ngesikhatsi lesifanele , tinhlelo temanti letinyenti letinsha kute kuphakelwe tindzawo tasemadolobheni nasetikhungweni tetimboni , luhlelo lolusha lwekunisela kubheseni wemfula Umzimvubu kanye neMakatini Flats , kanye neluhlelo lwekulondvolotwa kwemanti kute kwentiwe ncono kusetjentiswa kwemanti kahle . Kakhiwa kwetindlu : Sicelo setimali eBhodini yeTindlu yaVelonkhe kucedza tinkinga tekweswelakala kwetindlu kulendzawo siphasisiwe . Kepha , kubambelela kukhipha imali , tikhalo temhlaba endzaweni yekwakha nekwenta kancane kwekukhiswa kwemhlaba wahulumende uye emmangweni wenta lomklamo ungakhoni kuphumelela . Kutaba nekuncipha kwematfuba ekutsi labasikati bahlanganyele , futsi babe baholi . Emasu ngeke abuke-ngco kuniketa emandla kumake njengoba abukele kutfutfukiswa kwetinsinta kutenhlalakahle , tinhlelo tekusekela bantfwana , tindzawo tekuhlanganyela kwalabasikati kanye netindzawo letiphephile . Sebentisa indlela yekubuta imibuzo kute utewutfola kuchazeleka ngalokushiwo ngulomunye . Chaza kutsi inchubo yeCBP idzinga kutfutfukiswa kweLisu leliwadi njengobe Lisu leliwadi liluthuluzi lekucinisekisa kutsi imibono nabocalangaye betakhamuti kuyafakwa ku-IDP . Bhala emaphuzu labalulekile emakhadini nobe kubhukwana khona utowasebentisa . Ngaphandle kwetincwadzi tetimali letihamba kahle , linyenti lemabhizinisi aseNingizimu Afrika alitjali timali ngobe umnotfo wemhlaba solomane ubutsakatsaka . Bemabhizimisi nabo bakhatsatekile ngetingucuko kunchubomgomo nasesimeni sekulawula lesingenyusa tindleko . Kufinyelela kulelinye lizinga , lutjalomali loluphasi kuphindze kube ngumphumela wesakhiwonchanti lesingakeneli lesiniketwa ngemabhizimisi ahulumende . INingizimu Afrika idzinga kucedza lomjikeleto wekukhula kancane newekusisa lokuphasi . Hulumende unendzima lokumele ayidlale ekwakheni kwetsembeka nekutetsemba kute akhutsate lutjalomali lwesikhatsi lesidze . Bemabhizimisi nabo banendzima lokumele bayidlale - uma wonkhe umuntfu atjala kakhulu , inzuzo yetemnotfo itawenyuka emkhakheni wangasese . LESEHLUKO SIBUKETA BADLALI-TINDZIMA LABEHLUKENE nebudlelwane babo ekusebenteni kweKomidi yeLiwadi . Siphindze sibukete emachinga ekuchuba lafanele langasita emaKomidi eLiwadi ekusebentisananeni nebadlali-tindzima . Niketa umgomo kuleyo naleyo pheya ( kungahle kudzingeke kutsi unikete umgomo lofanako kumapheya langetulu kwayinye kuye ngekutsi unelinani lelingakanani lalabangenele tifundvo ) bese uhlola kutsi ngabe bebangayisebentisa njani lemigomo emmangweni wabo . Uma lelizinga seliphotfuliwe lomklamo kufanele uchazwe kahle . Uma tindleko , imisebenti , lokucala phambili nemashejuli sekuvisisiwe nabobonkhe labatibandzakanyako kufanele bavisise kutsi imphumelelo itawukalwa njani nekutsi bufakazi butawutfolakala njani . Indzima yeLuhlelo Lwekutfutfukisa Lwavelonkhe kweluleka hulumende kanye nelive etindzabeni letitsintsa intfutfuko yalelive yesikhatsi lesidze . Lolu luhlelo lwalo lonkhe live , tonkhe tigaba temmango kumele tibe nesibopho sekulwenta lusebente . Kute kwetfulwe loluhlelo ngemphumelelo , iKhomishini ikhombe luchungechunge lwetimphawu letibalulekile temphumelelo . Buyela emuva kulemibuto bese uyabukusisa kutsi lakho liKomidi leliWadi lite yini timphawu tekungalingani emkhatsini wemacembu etenkholo , tinhlanga , nalamanye nje emacembu ? Kubonisana - ummango uniketwa lwati mayelana nemklamo nobe ludzaba lolutsite bese ucelwa kutsi uphawule ngalo . Kuphawula kungentiwa ngeluhlolo loluchutjwa ngumkhandlu nobe lomunye lobandzakanyekako kumklamo nobe ngekubamba umhlangano wemmango . Imphendvulo : Emalunga emkhandlu akhiye umnyango uma abona sicumbi sita baphume ngemnyango wangemuva . Kutawuphindze kusite EmaKomidi emaWadi kufeza tibopho tawo njengobe luchumano emkhatsini kwemmango nemkhandlu nelikhansela labo leliWadi uma ngabe baneluhlaka lwekutibandzakanya . KUTE KUBE NESICINISEKO KUTSI INTFUTFUKO IHLALA SIKHATSI LESIDZE , kumcoka kutsi sikwati kubaluleka kwalabasikati nalabadvunaa njengetidalwa letidzinga kusebentisana ngaso sonkhe sikhatsi . Kumcoka futsi kutsi siwuhloniphe umbono wekutsi bomake nabobabe ngekwehlukana kwabo , banendzima lelinganako nakufika ekutsini kuphiliswana njani . Indlela labadvuna nalabasikati labacatjangwa nalabaphatfwa ngayo emmangweni , ngiyo sisekelo semphilanjani kutembusave , netemnotfo emmangweni , kantsi futsi indlela lokwentiwa ngayo loku kuba ngiyona nkhomba lebonakalako . Lesahluko sibuketa buhle bekulandzela timiso teluhlelo lwebulili nekulingana emisebentini lemikhulu yentfutfuko . Lesahluko sigcina ngekucoca kabanti ngetinkinga letingakhungatsa iNingizimu Africa nayidzembesela kulandzela lomhambo wetebulili nekulingana . Kugcila kutemphilo tabomake netebantfwana . Inchubo lehlelekile lapho khona licembu lesitsatfu lisita ngekwenchubo kutfutfukisa kuchumana emkhatsini kwemacembu , imvamisa emhlanganweni . Loku kwentiwa ngekuhambisa ingcikitsi , kulungisa kuniketana lwati , nekusita kuchuba inchubo ngendlela letakwenta umsebenti lotsite wenteke ngebumatima lobuncane . Niketa umgomo kuleyo naleyo pheya ( kungahle kudzingeke kutsi unikete umgomo lofanako kumapheya langetulu kwayinye kuye ngekutsi unelinani lelingakanani lalabangenele tifundvo ) bese uhlola kutsi ngabe bebangayisebentisa njani lemigomo emmangweni wabo . LiKomidi lebaphatsiswa nobe likomidi lemphatsidolobha nebaphatsiswa litfola tiphakamiso letibuya emakomidini esicheme nebaphatsi bemkhandlu letitawubese tenta luhlelo lwemhlangano wemkhandlu . Ngabe ngutiphi tigameko letisembili nobe imikhuba leke yenteka kulommango wakitsi kuleminyaka lengu-30-50 leyengcile ? Kulandzelelwa kwelizinga : Kubuka imiphumela yemiklamo letsite kute ubone kutsi iyahambisana yini nemabanga etimiso lafanele nekubona uphindze usebentise tindlela tekucedza timbangela temisebenti lengagculisi . Indlela yekwelapha kwekucala kutemphilo yesigodzi iyincenye yesigaba sekuvivinya kusebenta kwemshwalense wavelonkhe wetemphilo . Kute lendlela ibe yimphumelelo , luhlelo lwetemphilo ludzinga letinye tisebenti ( letifaka ekhatsi tisebenti leticeceshiwe kanye nebaphalali ) , tinhlobo letinsha tekuphatsa , kanye netakhiwo temtsetfo leticinisiwe letitawumela ummango . Kutsatsa sikhatsi lesingakanani emalunga eKomidi yeliWadi angakacali kusebenta ngekungatikhandli esigabeni lakuso ? INingizimu Afrika idzinga kwetfula tintfo letihamba embili ngalokuyimphumelo kunchubomgomo yetemnotfo wayo . Kuhluleka kubambisana , kutiphendvulela lokuhlukanako kanye nekwelekana kwaloko letfunywe kona kuvimbela kwetfulwa kwetinchubomgomo letikhona njengamanje . Kucocisana kwelicembu nelitsimba lekuhlela , LiKomidi leliwadi nobe emacembu ekusebenta lacocisene ngekutfutfukisa emaphepha emcondvo wemklamo mayelana nemiklamo ledzinga kwesekelwa kwangephandle . Kunganaki - kuchumana ngekunganaki kusho kuvuma konkhe lokushiwoko , kungatsatsi sincumo , kukhuluma ngeliphimbo leliphasi , ucabanga kutsi angeke ukhone kwenta lomsebenti , kungakhoni kubhekana nebantfu nanobe kunguwe locinisile . Indlela yeCBP iniketa bomasipala ngetindlela tekuhlomisa emasu ekubandzakanyeka ku-IDP . Ngalendlela ICBP isita bomasipala kutsi baphumelelise timfuno teSiphakamisomtsetfo neMtsetfo wetiNkhambiso taboMasipala , 2000 kancono . Kufuna ngemandla ematfuba ekuchubekela embili , ekufundza newekutfola lwati . Kungasimami kwenchubomgomo kuyintfo lekhatsatako . Njengobe kunetehlakalo lapho inchubomgomo kumele iguculwe khona , hulumende uvame kubukela phasi umtselela lowonako wekuguculwa kakhulu kwenchubomgomo ekwetfulweni kwetinsita . Kumele kube nekulinganisa kantsi kwanyalo loko kulinganisa akukho . Hlela kuhambahamba ewadini nifike etindzaweni tekuhleleka kwemhlaba letisembili . Njengobe nihamba , caphelani timphawu letisembili nekutsi ngabe tivele kuphi . Kubalulekile kutsatsa lemininingwane bese niyifaka esitfombeni semusho lesibonisa nobe ngutiphi timphawu telive nobe tekutfutfukisa kuleso naleso sicheme kanye nekuniketa ingcikitsi yeliwadi njengobe lesibonelo lesingentasi sibonisa . Sebentisa loLuhlu lwesicinisekiso lwesimondzawo kucinisekisa kutsi tonkhe tinhlangotsi tifakiwe . Balingani betinsita tamasipala ( MSP ) sivumelwano emkhatsisini wamasipala nebetfuli tinsita . Umetfuli tinsita kungaba ngulomunye umkhakha wemmango ( njenge libhodi lemanti nobe masipala wendzawo ) , inkapani yangasese , inkapani letimele ( NGO ) nobe inhlangano lesebenta nemmango ( CBO ) . Umsebentil Khetsa linye licembu lesive emangweni lonelwati lolutsite nalo - khetsa njenge ; balimi , takhamiti tetindzawo tekuhlala lengakahleleki , bosomabhizinisi labancane , njalonjalo . Umtsetfo loshayiwe uniketa tindlela letehlukene temmango tekutsi uhlanganyele kutekuphatsa ngisho nangemuva kwelukhetfo . Tinkhunda letinjemitimba lengamele tikolo , emakomidi emawadi , tinhlangano leticapha ummango kanye nemakomidi emitfolamphilo aniketa bahlali lwati kanye nematfuba ekulungisa kahle tikhungo letisedvute nabo . Imimango nayo ingahlanganyela ekwakhiweni kweluhlaka lwetinhlelo tahulumende wasekhaya . ngaphandle kwaletindlela , kuneligebe leliya ngekwandza emkhatsini webahlali nahulumende . Kubhedvuka kweludlame kuleminye imishuco yemmango kukhombisa kuphelelwa sineke kungabi mayelana nekwetfulwa kwetinsita kuphela , kepha nekukhatsateka kwekutsi imimango ayilalelwa kahle . Babambilichaza baphendvule imibuto lengephasi kwesigaba lebaniketiwe . Titsatse tincumo talamacembu , bese uyabuka kutsi ngutiphi tigaba labatisebentisile kucatulula lenkinga . Ngaphansi kweMtsetfo weSakhiwo saMasipala [ Sigaba 32 ] , umkhandlu ungendlulisela emandla latsite emaKomidini eliwadi . Nanobe kubalulekile kubandzakanya emaKomidi emaWadi eluhlelweni lwekubonisana lokungaba nemtselela kutincumo letitsatfwako , kwendluliselwa kwemandla kuphatfwa ngekucaphela . Tincumo temkhandlu kumele tentiwe ngumkhandlu lokhetfwe ngentsandvo yelinyenti , longagodli nalotiphendvulelako . EmaKomidi emaWadi akasito tinhlaka letitimele ngekwemtsetfo langakhona kwenta tivumelwano nobe ayiswe enkantolo ngenca yemaphutsa , kungasebentisi kahle timali nobe inkhohlakalo . Nobe ngutiphi tinkinga letibangwe tincumo letingakafaneli titawusala tisemahlombe emkhandlu ngalokusemtsetfweni . Kutawudzingeka ishejuli letibe kakhudlwana leyendlala imininingwane yalowo nalowo mcimbi , kuboniswe nelinani lemalanga , ( lokuvetwa kulenyanga yeshejuli yonkhana ) lowo nalowo msebenti lokumele wenteke macondzana nalowo mcimbi , lizinga lekubaluleka kwalowo msebenti , kanye nekutsi ngabe kudzingeka kubanjisanwe nabobani kute lowo msebenti uphumelele . Sihlalo kufanele avule umhlangano bese uwuchuba ngekulandzela luhla lwetihloko tetindzaba ngetigaba letilandzelana ngato . Kufakwa kweHIV neAIDS ku-IDP . Imiphumela yetemphilo yesikhatsi lesidze ilawula timphawu letingaphandle kweluhlelo lwetemphilo : indlela yekuphila , kudla lokukhetsekile kanye nemazinga ekudla lokondlako , temfundvo , kutiphatsa kutemacansi , kutivocavoca , tingoti temgwaco kanye nelizinga leludlame . IKhomishini yenta tiphakamiso kumkhakha ngamunye walena lesebaliwe . Imikhakha lehamba embili lefaka ekhatsi imfundvo ngetemacansi , kudla lokunemsoco , kutivocavoca kanye nekulwa nekubhema nekungasebentisi tidzakamiva ngalokufanele . Lena yimisebenti yetenhlalo ledzinga kubukisiswa ngibo bonkhe bahlali , iphindze ikhutsatwe yimindeni kanye netikhungo . UMtsetfo weNchubo yaMasipala wa2000 , ufuna kutsi bomasipala bakhe tindlela tekulawula lizinga lekusebenta . Imimango lengaphansi kwemaWadi netinhlangano tasemmangweni ticinisekisa kutsi masipala usebentisa imphahla lanayo kwetfula tinsita letimcoka letibawulwe takhamuti . Nanobe inchubo yekuhlela isukunyiswa futsi ihlelenjiswa ngumasipala , kute Lisu liphumelele , lidzinga kutsatfwa njengemntfwana weliwadi , lemelelwe liKomidi leliwadi . Bomasipala bahlomisa emakhansela nemaKomidi awo kutsi ahlelembise inchubo yekuhlela letawukhona ' kuniketa litfuba kulelo nalelo Komidi Komidi Komidi kutsi Lisukumise imvume-mgomo lecondzene nesikhatsi salo ehhovisi ' . Ezingeni laSekhaya tiNkhundla taboHulumende waSekhaya tibanjwa ngaMashi kantsi tihanjelwa tiGungu tekweNgamela taboMasipala kanye nebaphatsi kuteute balungise luhlelo lwemnyakatimali . Hulumende waSekhaya uphindze acale ngekutfutfukisa i-IDP legabanca iminyaka lemitsatfu . Kutsatsa sikhatsi lesingakanani emalunga eKomidi yeliWadi angakacali kusebenta ngekungatikhandli esigabeni lakuso ? Itawubukeka kanjani iNingizimu Afrika nga-2030 ? Lelive selifinyelele esigabeni sengucuko yetinkhambiso tekubekwa kwebantfu lapho emazinga ekubeleka ehla khona kantsi linani lebantfu liya ngekusimama . Lengucuko inemitselela lejulile esimeni sebunyenti bebantfu , lizinga lekukhula kwetisebenti kanye netidzingo tetinsita letinjengemfundvo netemphilo . Umkhandlu weAIDS waseMphumalanga Kapa utawesekela kubekwa kwemhlelembisi weHIV / AIDS . Tinkhomba letisezingeni lelisetulu timncoka . Akukeneli-nje kutsi kutsiwe besifazane bayahlanganyela emisebentini : lizinga lekuhlanganyela nelwati , kungaba sesigabeni semihlangano yemmango , emakilasini etikolwa letiphansi nome njengalabasebentisa tinsita tebantfu , konkhe kumncoka . Labaningi bantfu bavame kucabanga kutsi kwehlukahlukana kusho umehluko lokhona ebantfwini labavela emasikweni lahlukene . Bantfu baphindze babuke kwehlukahlukana nemehluko lophatsalene nebulili noma budzala . Kantsi , kwehlukahlukana , kufaka lokungetulu kwemehluko emkhatsini webantfu lophatselene nemasiko , bulili noma budzala . Bantfu bayehlukana ngetinhlobonhlobo tetigaba letifaka ekhatsi budzala , inkholo , emasiko , kufundza , lwati lwemphilo , simo semphilo , indzawo yekuhlala , umholo , simo sebutali , simo seligciwane lembulalave , simo sekusebenta kwemtimba njalonjalo . Umkhandludolobha umemetele kutsi kuklama kabusha indzawo lesedvutane nendzawo yekuhlala lenendzawo yeligaluvu kute kwakhiwe tindlu letingabiti kakhulu . Bahlali bendzawo abakajabuli ngetinhlelo njengobe batsi loku kutawuba nemtselela emananini emhlaba nemakhaya lakuwo . Ummango lohlelelwa lokwakhiwa kwetindlu ufuna luhlelo luchubekele embili njengobe kunekuswelakala kwetindlu kantsi nendzawo labahleti kuyo igcwele kakhulu . Lelizinga lekwenta lifaka ekhatsi kubuyeketa , kugucula tinhlelo nekwetfulwa umbiko lokuhlala kwenteka . Akusho kutsi ngoba luhlelo seluyasebenta tonkhe tintfo lebekucatjwangwa kutsi tinjalo ekucaleni kwemjikeleto wemklamo titawuhlala tinjalo kusosonkhe sikhatsi semklamo . Kubalulelile kutsi kuhlale kwentiwa kucondziswa nekutfulwa kwembiko kubo bonkhe labatibandzakanyako . Tonkhe takhamiti kumele tiphatfwe ngekunakekela nekuba neluvelo . Kuphendvula - Ngabe lamacophelo aphendvula tidzingo tetakhamiti letizuza kuleto tinsita ? Ummango lowehlukene - imimango yehlukene ngetinshisakalo , imibono nangemicabango . Kumele kube netindlela tekusombulula kungevani kute lokwehlukana kube ngulokwakhako kuphindze kufake sandla engucukweni nakunchubekelembili lekahle . Loluhlelo lolusha lutibophelele ekusebenteleni takhamuti , emacembu kanye nemimango ekwenteni ncono timphilo tabo . I-IDP iphindze igcwalise tidzingo letibekwe kumtsetfosisekelo , nekushaywa kwemitsetfo lelandzelako ( njengeLiphepha Lelimhlophe laHulumende , 1998 ) kutsi boMasipala bakhe , baphindze baphatse kusebenta , umcombelelotimali nenchubo yekuhlela , kanye nekutsatsela etulu tidzingo temphilo yemmango nekutibandzakanya kuvelonkhe nasetinhlelweni tentfutfuko tetifundza . Imihlangano lebanti yemmango kanye nemacembu lamancane lokufaka ekhatsi liKomidi leliwadi lapho kucocisanwa khona ngemetriksi yeLisu lekusebenta kanye nesifinyeto semiklamo ( lokungabhalwa eshadini leliphendvulekako bese kuvetelwa wonkhewonkhe ) . SINGAFINYELELA KULENHLOSO YETFU KUPHELA UMA BANTFU NGAMUNYE , IMIMANGO KANYE NETINHLANGANO TETEMBUSAVE , NGISHO NALABO LABANETIFISO LETEHLUKILE , BAKHOLELWA FUTSI BESEKELA TINKHAMBISO TETIKHUNGO " INKHULUMO YAMENGAMELI MBEKI LAYETFULELA UMHLANGANO WEMNYAKA LOVAMILE WENKHUNDLA YABOKHOMISHANE BELUKHETFO KUSADC , EDAR ES SALAAM , ETANZANIA , INYONI 1999 . Cela munye umuntfu kutsi aphatamise lenchubo , lomunye afake sandla lesakhako , lomunye angahlanganyeli bese lonye abute tinchazelo njalonjalo . Labanye labatsatfu akube ngemalunga eKomidi . Leminininingwane idzingekitsi kutsi kuphawulwe tidzingo temmango . Lemininingwane ifaka ekhatsi tibalobalo nemibiko , lokuniketa lingemuva ngeliwadi . Umsebenti 5 Niketa tibonelo letibonakalako tetindlela letingasetjentiswa ngummango wakho kufaka sandla kulesigaba lesi se-IDP , netakhiwo letikhona tekukhutsata kutibandzakanya kwemmango . ICBP ifaka ekhatsi kuphawula kanye nekucecesha bachubisifundvo kutsi basebente nemimango ekuyisiteni nasekuyesekeleni ekubandzakanyekeni ekuhleleni emmangweni wayo . Ngabe ngutiphi tigameko letisembili nobe imikhuba leke yenteka kulommango wakitsi kuleminyaka lengu-30-50 leyengcile ? Imiphumela , Tinkhomba kanye Netindlela Tekucinisekisa ( imisebenti , tinsita netindleko ) iniketa luhlakamsebenti lwekulungiselela imibiko yekuchubeka kwemklamo ( kucatsanisa loko bekuhleliwe naloko lokuzuziwe ) . ICBP yinchubo lehlelenjiswako lehlose ekucinisekiseni kutsi imibono yemmango iyafakwa ekutfutfukiseni ummango . Litsimba lelisenkhabeni lelinebachubisifundvo lokungenani lababili ngeliwadi basebentisana neliKomidi lendzawo leliwadi yindlela lenemphumela lomuhle . Lelitsimba kumele lifake ekhatsi lokungenani munye umchubisifundvo lovela ewadini namunye lovela kumasipala , kantsi uma kungaphumeleleka nalomunye umchubisifundvo lovela kulenye iwadi . Ngalokuhle bachubisifundvo baMasipala kumele batsatfwe emikhakheni leyehlukahlukene , kute kutawucinisekiswa kutsi kunenhlobonhlobo yemikhakha yamasipala letfola lwati ngeCBP , bese kumiswa nemuntfu lokuchunyanwa naye ngeCBP kulelo nalelo tiko lemkhakha . Kucocisana kweliKomidi leliwadi ngemetriksi yeLisu lekusebenta kanye neLisu lekusebenta langaphambilini . Lomcondvo weBafati macondzana neNtfutfuko ugcile ekubukeni kutsi bafati bangambandzanyeka njani kancono kulesimo semphilo lesikhona ' lesakhiwe ngemadvodza ' kanye nasemisebenti yentfutfuko lesunguliwe . Lomcondvo ucondziswe emsebentini webafati wekukhicita , lokungafaki ekhatsi umsebenti wekutala nekukhulisa bantfwana , futsi ubonakala ngekucamba imisebenti lemincane yekwakhela bafati imali ngaphandle kwekucondzana netisusa tekungalingani ngebulili letiyimihambo leyakhiwe . Siphakamisomtsetfo saboHulumende baSekhaya , 1998 ngumculu wenchubomgomo losukumisa luhlelo lolusha lwahulumende waSekhaya lonekutfutfukisa . Loluhlelo lolusha lwesekeleke ekusebenteni netakhamuti , emacembu kanye nemimango ekuniketeni lizinga lemphilo lelemukelekile kanye nekuhlangabetana netidzingo tetenhlalakahle , tetemnotfo nalokuphatsekako kwemmango . Loku kusho kutsi bomasipala kumele bahlele takhiwo futsi baphatse tinchubo tabo teliphakelotimali nekuhlela bese babeka bocalangaye betidzingo temmango letisisekelo . Intfutfuko emhlabeni wonkhe nasesifundzeni inemtselela ngetindlela letahlukahlukene eNingizimu Afrika . Umbono wetfu kutsi ngalokulinganako , tinkhambiso temhlaba tingaba nemtselela lomuhle entfutfukweni yeNingizimu Afrika , kungabekelwa eceleni bungoti lobunyenti lobungahle bube khona . Kuvisisa nekuphendvula ngendlela lefanele kutinsayeya temhlaba letimankimbonkimbo ngumsebenti wekucala wekuhlela . Emandla nemisebenti kuchaza lamandla bomasipala labanawo kuhlela nekubukela lokwentiwa etindzaweni tabo , kanye naleminye imsebenti yekwegamela labanayo . Labatibandzakanyako kufuneka banikete tizatfu ngekulandzelanisa lemisebenti ngekubhala ngendlela yeluhlelo , lishadi le-bha noma ngekuniketa tibonelo . Kuhlela lokutinte emmangweni kungaphindze kuholele etingucukweni ngetindlela bomasipala betfula ngato tinsita . Kwenta sibonelo masipala angacabanga kusungula lidlelandzawonye nelicembu lelitsite lemmango kutsi atokwetfula luhlobo lolutsite lwensita . Kubandzakanyeka kwemmango ekwetfulweni kwetinsita sekuvele kuyachubeka etindzaweni letifana neKaZulu-Natali naseMphumalanga Kapa lapho ummango umatasatasa ekwetfuleni emanti , tekutfutsa emangcoliso kanye netekuvakasha . Ngesikhatsi sesigaba sekucala seMvila-balave weCBP litsimba lekuhlela ligcogca liphindze lihlatiye imininingwane kanye nelwati loluvele lukhona emmangweni ngekusebentisa luchungechunge lwetinkhulumo-luhlolo kanye nekusebentisa emathuluzi lahlukene eCBP . Kuhlatiywa lokujulile kwalemininingwane kuniketa litsimba lekuhlela ngelingemuva lelibanti nalelijulile mayelana nesimo semmango , tinkinga , emasiko , imikhuba , tinhlelo kanye nemagugu awo . Tinkhulumo-luhlolo letihleleke ngalokungenelelekako letibanjwa nebaphakeli betinsita labaphawulwe kumdvwebo weVenn . Letinkhulumo-luhlolo titsatsa cishe 1 kuya ku-1.5 ema-awa . Sigaba 152 - tinhloso tahulumende wasekhaya kukhutsata kubandzakanyeka kwemmango kanye netinhlangano temmango etindzabeni tahulumende wasekhaya . Tjela babambi lichaza bacedzele umsebenti longentasi . Kucinisa kusebenta kwemboni yetisebenti kute kukhutsatwe kutfolakala kwemakhono , kuchumanisa labafuna imisebenti netikhala temisebenti letivulekile kanye nekunciphisa kungevani . Khumbuta labangenele tifundvo kutsi sisebentisa lomsebenti kwenta labangenele tifundvo bakwati kutfola tinsayeya tekusukumisa Lisu leliwadi kanye nekutsi asinaso sikhatsi sekuhlolisisa leso naleso sigaba kabanti , ngaloko-ke sitawukhona kuniketa kuphela imizuzu lengu-10 kuya ku-15 kulesinyatselo , kepha emacembu kumele avele nembono singakapheli lesikhatsi lesibekiwe . Uma bangaphumeleli kucedza umbono wabo bangachubeka badzimate bafike lapho labangafinyelela khona . Kuphatfwa nekutfutfukiswa kwamasipala kuyinchabhayi futsi kufaka ekhatsi tindzaba letimatima letibanti . Njengoba kakhulu kufaka bantfu , tidzingo tabo , kukhatsateka kanye netimfuno kumele kuphatfwe ngendlela letakwenta kutsi kuzuzwe kakhulu futsi kuzuza bantfu labanyenti kakhulu . Nanobe kunjalo ummango wakhiwe ngemacembu lahlukene naletinelutsandvo lwetintfo letingafani kantsi akusiwo onkhe emacembu latawenetiseka ngesikhatsi sinye . Kute kusitwe tikhulu tamasipala kanye nebaholi labakhetsiwe kutsi benanele ngalokukahle kutakhamiti tendzawo yabo , kutibandzakanya kwemmango kudzingekile . EmaKomidi emaWadi adlala indzima lebalulekile ekwenteni kutsi loku kwenteke . Uva kunjani kuwe uma ukhuluma nemuntfu lova ngatsi uyakulalela ? Umuntfu lokuchunyanwa naye nemininingwane . Ezingeni lelive , emakhono labalulekile afaka ekhatsi letinye tikhungo , sakhiwonchanti ( tekuchumana , emanti , emandla netekutfutsa ) , luhlelo lwemfundvo nekucecesha , kuphatfwa kwemvelo lokusimeme , tinhlelo tekucamba kabusha kanye netindlela tekutfutfukisa indzawo . Emakhono ebantfu afaka ekhatsi imfundvo , temphilo , kuvikeleka kutenhlalo kanye nekuphepha kwemmango . Umvikeli weMmango udlala indzima lemcoka ekulweni nasekuphenyeni kutiphatsa lokungakafaneli kumkhakha wahulumende . Lihhovisi leMvikeli weMmango linemandla ekuphenya noma ngukuphi kutiphatsa etintfweni tahulumende , nobe kuphatfwa kwemmango kunobe nguluphi luhlangotsi lwahulumende lolungalunganga nobe lolugcinela ekwenteleni phasi , kubika loko kutiphatsa nekutsatsa tinyatselo tekulungisa letifanele . Kusetinshisekelweni temabhizimisi futsi kutsi lizinga lekungalingani lincishiswe . Kungalingani kwenyusa tindleko tekwenta ibhizimisi , kumise kabi kuma kwetimakethe ekugcineni kuletse imikhawulo ematfubeni ekukhula . Kuphindze kwandzise kungatsembani nekungevani . Kuhola kakhulu kwalabasetulu kwakha kancane ummango lohlanganisa konkhe lapho wonkhe umuntfu ativa khona kutsi unesabelo etitselweni tenkhululeko . Nanobe kushaywa kwemtsetfo wemiholo kungenteki kalula , buholi budzingeka kucinisekisa kutsi bemabhizimisi benta ngalokufanele . Inchubo yeCBP yemukela kutsi emalunga emmango anelwati nelwatinchanti lesivelele mayelana nekutfutfukiswa kwawo futsi igcizelela kakhulu kuletinhlangotsi . Kulomsebenti lolandzelako tinkhulumoluholo nebantfu labayimitfombolusito lesembili tisetjentiselwa kutfola emasu mayelana netisombululo letingahle tibe khona . Kutiphendvulela kubalulekile entsandvweni yelinyenti . Kunebutsakatsaka lobunyenti eluchungechungeni lwekutiphendvulela , kanye nelisiko lekususa kugceka kulomunye kunye kulomunye . Luchungechunge lwekutiphendvulela kumele luciniswe kusukela etulu kuya phasi . Kucala nje , kutiphendvulela kwephalamende kubutsakatsaka , iPhalamende yehluleka kufezikisa indzima yayo lebalulekile yekubeka liso yonkhe indzawo . Imiphumela yemfundvo ngete yentiwa ncono ngaphandle nje uma kutiphendvulela kuciniswa ngeluhlelo , kusukela kumiphumela yebafundzikuye ekuhanjisweni kwetincwadzi tekufundza . Lelinani lelenyukako lemishuco yekwetfulwa kwetinsita likhombisa kutsi umbuso nawo udzinga kwenta kube malula kutsi bahlali bavete kukhatsateka kwabo . Nabangena esakhiweni sahulumende , bahlali kumele bakwati kubona kutsi ngutiphi tinhlelo labangatilindzela , kutsi kumele baye kuphi kanye nekutsi bangakhuluma nabani uma bangakanetiseki . Tinkhombandlela teBatho Pele titawusita eMaKomidi eLiwadi ekuphendvuleni emalunga emmango labangasho umbono wekutsi tinsita labaniketwa tona tisebenti atisito telizinga leliniketwa Tinkhombandlela teBatho Pele . Kulandzelela Luhlelo Lwekulawula Kusebenta - iPMS kumele yakhiwe ngibo bonkhe bomasipala kute kuchazwe ngekusetjentiswa kwetinsita tamasipala , kutfutfuke kuphumeleliswa nalokuphumelelisako kwetinhlangano , kukhonjiswe nekuzuzwa kwemiphumela . Masipala kufanele abeke tinkhomba letibalulekile tekusebenta kukala umsebenti , kumele aphindze afake ekhatsi ummango . LiKomidi leLiwadi lithulusi lekufaka ekhatsi ummango . Ngesikhatsi salomsebenti lolandzelako kuchutjwa tinkhulumo-luhlolo nebaphakeli betinsita kutsi kutohlolwa umtsamo webaphakeli betinsita labaphawulwe ngesikhatsi semsebenti lowengcile kutsi bafake ligalelo ekusebentiseni , kuhlola tinkinga labahlangabetana nato , kanye nekubafaka kunchubo yekuhlela . Loku kutawusita ekwakheni emasu lanembako nalatawuphumelela . Khumbula kuhlela letinkhulumo-luhlolo kusenesikhatsi lesihle . Sigaba C sabomasipala , nobe bomasipala besigodzi : laba bomasipala labengamele bomasipala labanyentana bendzawo . Kute kunonophiswe inchubekelembili , kujuliswe intsandvo yelinyenti kuphindze kwakhiwe ummango lohlanganisa wonkhe umuntfu , iNingizimu Afrika kumele igucule inkhululeko yetembusave ibe kuphila kahle kutemnotfo kwawo wonkhe umuntfu . Kusetandleni tabo bonkhe bahlali baseNingizimu Afrika kutsi balungise likusasa labo , kusukela lamuhla . Umnumzane Nkosi uhlala esabelweni lapho khona impompi seyifakiwe , ngoba akusiyo yonkhe imiti lenemanti etindlini . Impompi ibekwe embi kweligede lakhelangembili . Bantfu labasebentisa lempompi abayivavali kahle ihlala ivuta emanti . Loku kwenta lendzawo ibe neludzaka , kugcwala netimbuzulwane . Umnumzane Nkosi sewudziniwe kuba nendzawo leneludzaka embi kwendlu yakhe , wase uncoma kunweba fenisi wakhe khona impompi ivaleleke eyadini lakhe bese ukhiya ligede . Bantfu besabelo bakwate bÃªte batokhala . Batsi bantfu Umnu Nkosi akacabangelani , utikhandza ancono kunebantfu basesabelweni . Umnu Nkosi uvangatsi bantfu bendzawo abacangi bakhombisa kubabete luvelo , ngoba yena nemndeni wakhe abaphatseki kahle ngoba abayivali lempompi . Ngabe tikhona tindzawo lapho kutfolakala khona tinhlobo tetihlahla netilwane letisebucayini ? Bahlukanise bafundzi ngemacembu alabatsatfu bantfu . Licembu ngalinye licele licabange bese libhala phansi kutsi iyinye ngayinye yaletingoni tisebantani . Abekwente loku bacabange ngalokwenteka kubomasipala babo . UMSEBENTI 1 Cabanga ngemisebenti yeKomidi yeLiwadi lengamikiswa eSigabeni Sekucala senchubo yekuhlela , yenta siciniseko kutsi imimango ifaka sandla kulenchubo . Bhala imibono kulelishadi leliphepha . LoKomidi leliWadi linato yini tindlela letihleliwe tekwakha emakhono alabasebentako kutsi bangalwenta luhlatiyo lwetebulili ezingeni lemitsetfo , tinhlelo , kanye nakuleso sigungu sonkhe labakuso , nanekutsi banawo emakhono ekuchuba tinhlelo letisekela kulingana ngetebulili ? Babobani bona ? Emazinga enkhohlakalo lasetulu acedza emandla likhono lemmango lekusebenta kahle nangalokuphumelelisako , kanye nelikhono lahulumende lekwetfula intfutfuko latfunywe yona . Ngekuya kweluhlolo Lwekungagodli inkhohlakalo Kwemave Emhlaba , emkhatsini wa-2001 na-2010 , lizinga lenkhohlakalo lenyukile . Inkhohlakalo ivame kufaka ekhatsi bemkhakha wahulumende kanye newangasese . Umcondvo lowakhekile wemazinga lasetulu enkhohlakalo emazingeni lasetulu ahulumende wenta kulwa nenkhohlakalo kube matima kakhulu . LiKomidi leliwadi nebachubisifundvo beCBP basebentisa iSWOT yemazinga emphilo emacembu kanye nemininingwane yeSigaba 1 ekucocisaneni kwelicembu lokutsatsa ema-awa lasitfupha . Umsebenti 5 Niketa tibonelo letibonakalako tetindlela letingasetjentiswa ngummango wakho kufaka sandla kulesigaba lesi se-IDP , netakhiwo letikhona tekukhutsata kutibandzakanya kwemmango . Kwakhela etikwemininingwane legcogcwe ngesikhatsi sesigaba sekucala , sigaba sesibili sibandzakanya luhlatiyo lolutibile kanye nekuhlanganiswa kwalemininingwane . ESigabeni 2 imininingwane legcogciwe iyahlatiywa bese kucocisanwa ngayo emacenjini lamancane . Lenchubo ihlanganise kuhlatiywa kwemazinga emphilo emacembu etenhlalakahle lahlukahlukene , emathuluzi eCBP ( emabalave , iVenn , kugabanca , kuhambisana nesikhatsi semnyaka nemncamulajucu wesikhatsi wemikhuba yesikhatsi-dze ) , kanye nemiphumela yetinkhulumo-luhlolo nebaphakeli betinsita kanye netebantfu labayimitfombolusito lesembili . Ekupheleni kwalesigaba ummango utfola litfuba lekubuyeketa , uhlolisise uphindze ucinisekise lemininingwane lehlanganisiwe . Loku-ke kube sekwetfulwa ewadini bese kulindzeleka kutsi kubekwe bocalangaye labasembili bemiphumela lesihlanu yenchubo yekuhlela . Sigaba 39 seMtsetfo weTinhlelo taMasipala , 2000 unika umsebenti umphatsiswa loyimeya , likomidi letiphatsimandla nobe likomidi lelisipesheli lemakhansela kuphatsa kwakhiwa kwePMS nekuyimikisa kumkhandlu . IPMS kumele isho ngalokucacile imisebenti nalokubhekekile kumunye ngamunye lodlala indzima . Ingabe ummongo weluhlatiyo lwemklamo uyakufaka yini kubuyeketa kwesimo sabomake kutemtsetfo , tekuhlalisana netemnotfo ? Tindzaba letiyimivuka yemaminitsi emhlangano wangaphambilini sihloko lesiphatsa tindzaba letadzingidzwa emhlanganweni lowendlulile lekufanele emalunga eKomidi atfule umbiko ngato . Kuvame kutsi tibonakale tindzaba letiyimivuka ngekutsi kubukwe tinyatselo lebekumele titsatfwe bantfu labatsite . Ngabe tinsita letikhona tiyafinyelela kulamacophelo ? Umkhakha wetisebenti lophendvula kakhulu kumatfuba etemnotfo lavelako . Loku kudzinga kufundza kwemphilo yonkhe nekwentiwa ncono kwemsebenti ; kusimamisa simo setisebenti ; kucinisa tikhungo tekusombulula kungevani ; kubuyeketa imisetfo leshayiwe kanye nemazinga emabhizimisi lamancane nalasemkhatsini ; kulungisa tekuchumana emkhakheni wetisebenti tahulumende ; kucinisa kusetjentiswa buncane bemazinga emkhatsini webacashi , tikhungo kanye nababafunela bantfu imisebenti ; kucinisa tinchubomgomo tetimakethe letisebenta kahle nekucondzaniswa kwemisebenti ; kanye nekwenta kutsi tisebenti letinemakhono tikwati kutsutseleka kuletinye tindzawo . LeLisu Lisukunyisiwe kepha lidzinga kutsi liguculwe libe Lisu lekusebenta kute litosetjentiswa . Nayi indlela yekwenta loko . Kwenta tiphakamiso nganobe nguluphi ludzaba lolutsintsa liwadi ngekutfumela ngesandla sekhansela yeliwadi tiye kumasipala . Kulomzuliswano wangaphambilini wema-IDP , beluleki bebadlala indzima lenkhulu kakhulu - esikhatsini lesinyenti lokuhambisana nemiphumela leyinkinga . Beluleki be-IDP kanye nebahleli bamasipala bavamise kuba bosonjiniyela nobe bahleli bemadolobha , kantsi-ke ngaloko baceceshelwe kubukana netindzaba tesimo , tesakhiwonchanti nobe tekuhleleka kwemhlaba , hhayi tinchubo-ngco nobe kuchumana nemmango . Lenkinga yemukelwa ngalokubanti yi-dplg kantsi kuceceshwa kwema-IDP lokwentiwa nga-2001 kwetama kwenaba kuvisiswa kwekutfutfukisa uma kucatsaniswa nekuhlela ngekwesicu . Sigaba B sabomasipala , nobe bomasipala bendzawo : laba bomasipala labanemandla lasetulu ekulawula umtsetfo babambisene nabomasipala besigaba C nobe bomasipala betigodzi . Bonkhe bomasipala bendzawo bangephansi kwamasipala wesigodzi . Umtsetfosisekelo waseNingizimu Afrika uneMculu wemaLungelo locinisekisa kuvikelwa kwemalungelo . Tonkhe takhamiti tinelilungelo lekuvikelwa kwemalungelo eluntfu . Lamalungelo afaka ekhatsi indzawo yekuhlala ' lengenabungoti emphilweni nobe ekuphileni kwabo ' kanye ' nekutfutfukisa kusimama kwendalo nekusetjentiswa kwetinsita temvelo lokuphephile ngakulolunye luhlangotsi kube kukhutsatwa kutfutfuka kwemnotfo nekwetenhlalakahle ' . Umculu wemaLungelo sigatjana 24 . EmaKomidi emaWadi adlala indzima lebalulekile njengemgudvu wekuhambisa timfuno temmango kute tetfulwe eLuhlelweni LweKutfutfukisa loluBumbene kanye nekucinisekisa kutsi tinhlelo tetenhlalo netemnotfo teliwadi tihambisana netimfuno temmango wonkhana . EmaKomidi eLiwadi anebudlelwane lobukatsatfu nemmango , kokucala njengalabamele ummango , kwesibili ngekwakha budlelwane nemmango , kwesitsatfu , ngekutiphendvulela . Kuphendvula - Ngabe lamacophelo aphendvula tidzingo tetakhamiti letizuza kuleto tinsita ? Kukhutsata kutibandzakanya kwemmango ngekukhutsata tibopho nekutentela kute batokwesabela etimfunweni temamango . Loku kungafaka ekhatsi kulungisa emaphephatatiso latisa ummango ngetehlakalo letitsite . Umsakato wemmango nawo uyindlela leyimphumelelo yekubandzakanya ummango etindzabeni letiwutsintsako . Ngekwesibonelo , emalunga EmaKomidi emaWadi angabutwa imibuto ngetehlakalo letentiwa emmangweni , nobe umsakato wemmango ungasetjentiselwa kwatisa ngesehlakalo nobe kufuna imibono ngemklamo lohlelwako . Sebentisa Luhlu lwesicinisekiso ekucocisaneni lokuvulekile mayelana nemazinga emphilo elicembu . Rekhoda timphendvulo . Lesibonelo seLuhlu lwesicinisekiso timphahla singakusita kulomsebenti kucinisekisa kutsi unayo yonkhe imininingwane loyidzingako . Sigaba 1 siniketa kwendlaleka kwemininingwane lefinyelelekako kumfundzi njengendzawo yekucala kunchubo yekuhlela . Sebentisa i-PowerPoint uma une-data projektha , kantsi uma ingekho ungabhala leso naleso sigaba eshadini leliphendvulekako uphindze ukhombise labangenele tifundvo umdvwebo losekhasini 35 emanotsini esifundvo . Luhla lwemininingwane yemmango - yakha luhla lwemininingwane yetinhlangano letisemmangweni , kanye nemininingwane yekubatsintsa nemuntfu lowengamele kute wente siciniseko kutsi bonkhe labatsintsekako bayatiswa ngalokwentekako kumkhandlu . Kutimisela kutembusave kubalulekile ekulweni nalesihlava . Kutimisela kutembusave kulinganiswa ngekuhlola imali lesetjentiswe ekulweni nekhohlakalo , emandla emtsetfo tikhungo tekulwa nenkhohlakalo letinawo , kutimela kwetiphatsimandla tekulwa nenkhohlakalo ekutsaneni kungabi nekungenelela kwetembusave kanye nekungagucuki kwendlela umtsetfo losetjentiswa ngayo . Kutsamba emacaleni lamancane nobe kucina enkhohlakalweni lokufaka ekhatsi betembusave , kusho kungasetjentiswa ngalokufanako . Yakha simondzawo lesisekelako lesenta bantfu bakhululeke babukane netintfo . Umtsetfosisekelo , 1996 usungula hulumende wasekhaya njengeluhlangotsi lwahulumende lolusebenta kwetfulwa kwetinsita . Imimmango yetfu ifaka ekhatsi bantfu labatinhlobo letehlukene , labanetimfundziso letehlukene , tindlela tekuphila , tinkholo , tilwimi , tindlela tekutsandzana , tindlela tekugcoka nekubukeka ngesicu semtimba . Uma sikubuka ngendlela lekahle lokwehlukana singatsi , ' kwenta imphilo ibe ngulechazanako kuphindze kuphelelise imphilo yetfu ' Kuphila nekwehlukahlukana kuyinsayeya futsi emaKomidi emaWadi adzinga kuhlangabetana naletinsayeya ngendlela lekahle . Emacembu lasemmangweni anetidzingo letehlukene , tindlela letehlukile tekutfola tinsita kantsi futsi lebakulindzele kwehlukile . Njengaloku emaKomidi emaWadi anemitfwalo yekucinisekisa kutsi tidzingo temmango tifakiwe ekuhleleni kwamasipala kanye nasetinhlelweni , adzinga kutsi awati emacembu lahlukene lakhona emmangweni yawo , aphindze acinisekise kutsi emacembu atibona ayincenye yekutsatsa tincumo . Umsebenti 2 Tinyatselo tini letingatsatfwa liKomidi leliWadi lakho kubhekana nekungalingani lenikutfolile nisacocisana ? Yetama kucabanga kunye nje lokungentiwa kumunye ngamunye walemibuto . Khutsata lomunye umuntfu kutsi akhulume ngeinftukutselo yakhe , kute kungababusi - kepha kumele babuse loinftukutselo . Imethrikhs yeluhlaka lwekwentiwa kwemisebenti imiculu lekhombisa tincenye letibalulekile teluhlelo lwemklamo ngendlela lecondzile . Imininingwane yelizinga ngalinye iyagcwaliswa kulomsebenti kanye ntinhlelo tetinsita ( lekutawukhulunywa ngawo esigabeni lesilandzelako ) lahambisana neluhlaka lwekwentiwa kwemisebenti . Bhala luhla lwetimphawu temuntfu lonelikhono lekukhuluma nalabanye . Sigaba Sekuvala - sekuciniseka kutsi yonkhe imigomo yalomklamo iyafezeka , labatsintsekako " bayavumelana " nayo , lomsebenti uyafika emaphetselweni ngekutsi lwati ngawo lusakatwe nekuts tivumelwano lebetikhona kulabebasebenta netindzaba lebetisele tingakabukwa tiyacedzelwa . Kulawulwa kwalemiklamo kusime kulendlela leyatiwako yekuchuba imisebenti lemikhulu letsi akubukisiswe tonkhe tingoni talomsebenti kusuka usacala uze uphetse . Loku kusho kutsi tingucuko kanye netinkhinga tiyafakwa nakwakhiwa kuphindze kuhlelelwa sigaba lesilandzelako . Kuhlela lokutinte emmangweni akuvele kutentakalele . Kuhlela akusiyo intfo leyentiwa nguchwepheshe . Kwesekeleke ekubandzakanyekeni nakutinchubomgomo tentsandvo yelinyenti kutembusave . Kubandzakanyeka kudzinga kutsi bonkhe babambimsuka bamenywe kutsi babandzakanyeke , lokufaka ekhatsi hulumende , ummango , betemabhizinisi , basebenti kanye naletinye tincenye temmango jikelele . Khutsata kuvuleka - ungabehluleli bantfu uma ngabe basho imbono yabo . Ingehluka kweyakho . Kubalulekile kuncuma ngembi kwesikhatsi kutsi ngabe bocalangaye bemacembu labekelwe ecadzini bawuniketwa bucalangaye lobutsite . Kwenta sibonelo , kungabe kuvunyelenwe kutsi munye wemiphumela lesihlanu kumele avele kulamacembu . Yini labayentako leyenta kubemelula kuwe kutsi ukhulume nabo ? Kubamba imihlangano nemimango letsintsekako nalabo labatsintsekako . Bomasipala bangahlanganyela njani netimphiko tahulumende waSekhaya newelive lonkhe . Bachubisifundvo : ICBP idzinga litsimba lebachubisifundvo labatinikele nalabaceceshiwe labavisisa kahle lenchubo futsi labangayisebentisa ngalokufanelekile nangemphumelelo . Mema emacembu lehlukene kutsi akhombe lotawakhulumela , tjela sikhulumi sitetfule sisho nekutsi simele bani . Lomele liKomidi leLiwadi nelikhansela leliwadi bayatetfula nebalingani babo . Bavumelane ngemitsetfo yenchubo nawo onkhe emacembu . Sibonelo : vumela ngalinye licembu lichaze sicelo ; likhulume ngemvume yemehluleli ; kubete lowetfuka lomunye njll njll njll . Budlelwane netinhlangano tematekisi endzawo nelusito lwekwatisa ngemhlangano lotoba khona kuletinye tetindlela budlelwane lobungasota ngato kukhutsata kulalela imibono yemmango . Lilunga noma emalunga eliKomidi leliWadi angacabanga kutsi tonkhe takhamuti letihlala encenyeni letsite yemango batigebengu ngakoke noma ngusiphi sincomo lebasentako macondzana nekwetfulwa kwetinsita noma imisebenti yesikhashana kumele ingashaywa mkhuba . Emakomidi lamisiwe acondzane nematiko amasipala , angasungulwa ngumkhandlu uma adzingeka . Kwakha likhono lembuso lekudlala indzima letfutfukisako naleguculako . EmaKomidi emaWadi kanyenti akhetfwa emhlanganweni wemmango lokuba sikhatsi semnyaka nobe nobe nobe lemibili . Uma lilunga lehluleka kuhambela imihlangano , kungafakwa lelinye endzaweni yalo . EMalunga eliKomidi leliWadi akhetfwa ngalokungafani etindzaweni tasemakhaya netasemadolobheni . Umhlangano ubitiwe , likhansela leliwadi liyachaza kutsi lesisicelo samanje lesisakhulunywa , nekutsi imihlangano yemmango itawubanjwa . Waphindze wachaza tizatfu talokutfutswa lokuphakamisiwe , letifaka ekhatsi kutsi lendzawo lapho kwakhiwe imikhukhu leminyenti khona ayivumeli kutsi kungakhiwa indzawo yemangcoliso , ngakoke lendzawo angeke itfutfukiswe njengendzawo yekuhlala sikhatsi lesidze . Kwamanje , takhamiti letinyenti tibanjwa ngumkhuhlane longapheli . Takhamiti letinesifuba angeke tisindze naleto letiphila ne HIV / AIDS angeke tikhone kutsatsa imitsi ngendlela lefanele ngoba tinsita tiyashoda . Ingucuko yesimo selitulu seyivele inemtselela kuNingizimu Afrika , ngekugucugucuka kwemazinga ekushisa newemvula kanye nekwenyuka kwemazinga elulwandle . Hulumende utawubukana nencenye lenkhulu yetiphakamiso letikuloluhlelo . Kute etfule letiphakamiso , utawudzinga kucinisa luchungechunge lwakhe lwekutiphendvulela , kwenta ncono emandla ache , atimisele kutsatsa tincumo letimatima aphindze asebentisane nalabanye emangweni kute kusonjululwe letinsayeya . Loku kusho kuchumana nemmango ngekwetsembeka nangekutitfoba , kube kwentiwa kutsi bahlali batiphendvulele ngetinyatselo tabo . Baholi , ikakhulukati kuhulumende , kumele babukane netincumo letimatima kanye nekuguculwa kwetintfo . Buholi lobunemandla bumayelana nekutsatsa tincumo letinjalo nangalokuyimphumelelo letikhutsata ummango kutsi kulandzelwa indlela lencono . Simo semafa kumasipala . Babambi lichaza babuka emanotsi lachaza tisusa letehlukene tekushayisana . Bomasipala bacancatsa kumakhono emmango . Imimango inemakhono nelwati lolwehlukehlukene lolungasita masipala . Kungongela masipala imali njengobe lamakhono atfolakala ngaleso sikhatsi . Kuvuselela tindzawo tekuhlala letingakahleleki emhlabeni losendzaweni lefanele . Kubuyeketwa kwelizinga lekusebenta ngemnyaka - Libandla lemakhansela kufanele letfule umbiko weluhla lwemaphakelo kanye netinhloso temusebenti . Sigaba sekusungula -siholela kutsi umklamo uvunywe ngibo bonkhe labatsintsekako . Kuvumelana angeke kudzingeke kuphela nakusacala lomsebenti kodvwa kuto tonkhe tigaba tawo . Kwesekela lokubanti kuyo yonkhe imimango kuyadzingeka ekwetfulweni kwaloluhlelo ngemphumelelo . Entsandvweni yelinyenti lekhombisa kukhutsala lokwesekela ngete kwangaba nekuhlatiywa . Tinkhulumomphendvulwano letinemandla tiyadzingeka ekwakheni kuvumelana kanye nebunini lobubanti baloluhlelo . Tinkhulumomphikiswano letakhako nato tifaka sandla ekwenteni bahlali baseNingizimu Afrika babe nekuvisisa lokuncono baphindze itsatse buniyo lobuhlanganyele betintfo letisembili eluhlwini . Tincenye teluhlelo letehlukene tekwenta ngebunyenti kanye nekutinikela kwemikhakha leyehlukene . Nakwenteka kuba khona kungahambisani , kubalulekile kutsi tizatfu tekungavumelani tikhulunywe futsi tichazwe ngalokucacile , kute kube nekuvumelana lokubanti mayelana nendlela leya embili . Luhlelo Lwekutfutfukisa Lwavelonkhe lungasebentisa emandla alo ekubitela ndzawonye kute kuhlanganiswe ndzawonye badlalindzima kutsi bachube tinkhulumiswano baphindze bete netisombululo . Nanobe inchubo yekuhlela isukunyiswa futsi ihlelenjiswa ngumasipala , kute Lisu liphumelele , lidzinga kutsatfwa njengemntfwana weliwadi , lemelelwe liKomidi leliwadi . Bomasipala bahlomisa emakhansela nemaKomidi awo kutsi ahlelembise inchubo yekuhlela letawukhona ' kuniketa litfuba kulelo nalelo Komidi Komidi Komidi kutsi Lisukumise imvume-mgomo lecondzene nesikhatsi salo ehhovisi ' . Kubuyeketa kwekusebenya kwemnyaka - Umkhandlu kumele ubike emakomidini emawadi ngemcombelelotimali wawo nangetinhloso tekusebenta . LiKomidi LeliWadi lingatisa sodolobha nalingatfoli imibiko njalo . Tintfo letingaphandle kwemklamo tingagucula noma kuphi ngako-ke kubalulekile kutsi kwentiwe luhlolo lwenhlekelele kuwo wonkhe umjikeleto wemklamo . Imitsetfo ye-MP&PM , 2001 isondzelene neMtsetfo weTinhlelo taMasipala 2000 , yakhiwa emvakwekubonisana nemphatsiswa wahulumene wasekhaya , nenhlanganyela yahulumende wasekhaya lemele hulumende wasekhaya welivelonkhe . Lemitsetfo isebenta kuniketa imininingwane lengetekile etintfweni letibekwe ku-MSA , 2000 . Ezingeni laSekhaya tiNkhundla taboHulumende waSekhaya tibanjwa ngaMashi kantsi tihanjelwa tiGungu tekweNgamela taboMasipala kanye nebaphatsi kuteute balungise luhlelo lwemnyakatimali . Hulumende waSekhaya uphindze acale ngekutfutfukisa i-IDP legabanca iminyaka lemitsatfu . LiKomidi leliWadi lingaphakamisa lizinga lentfutfuko yemnotfo wemmango ngekutsi yatise ummango njalonjalo ngemisebenti lesunguliwe kanye namatfuba lakhona . Lingabikela emakhansela ngetinkinga letihlangana nato takhamuti letifuna kucala emabhizinisi lamancane . Kute kunonophiswe intfutfuko , iNingizimu Afrika idzinga kwesekela lokukhutsatako kwabo bonkhe bahlali , buholi kuto tonkhe tinhlaka letihambisa embili tinshisekelo talelive ngekuhlanganyela , tinjongo tesikhashana kanye nekusebenta kwahulumende lokutfutfuke kakhulu . Kuletinye tincenye , kungenteka kudzingeke kuguculwa kwenchubomgomo , kepha emikhakheni leminyenti kumayelana nemalungelonchanti , kwetfulwa kwetinhlelo tahulumende , kutsi bantfu batiphendvulele ngetento tabo baphindze batfole tisombululo leticanjwe kabusha tetinsayeya letimankimbonkimbo . Emacembu aniketwa umsebenti . Emacembu aniketwa cishe emaminitsi langu-10 kuya kulangu-15 kutsi akhulumisane ngemsebenti wawo aphindze abelane ngetimphendvulo tawo ehlanganweni . EMakomidi eLiwadi kanye nebantfu lebamelwe banelilungelo lekubheka kwetfulwa kwetinsita . Kumele kukhunjulwe kutsi imimango inemsebenti ekwenteni siciniseko sesimo lesihle nelinani letinsita lokuchazwa emacophelweni etinsita . Sibonelo , kumele banikete lwati lolungemaciniso , bachaze simo sabo ngekwetsembeka , bancume kutiphatsa ngenhlonipho , nangekunakekela kubaletsi bemsebenti , nalabanye . EMakomidi eLiwadi adlala indzima ekwenteni siciniseko kutsi tidzingo temmango tatiswa ngalokuphumelelisako nangemaciniso . Kumele aphindze ente siciniseko kutsi emalunga emmango ayatiswa ngelwati , kutsi lukuphi nekutsi lutfolakala njani . Yengamela kwetfulwa kwemibono ngendlela yekutibandzakanya kwemmango kumasipala , netakhiwo letibekelwe kutibandzakanya kwemmango , njengekutsi , emaminitsi emkhandlu kumele atfunyelwe emakomidi emawadi . Yakhani saga lesihehako semmango wenu lesingasetjentiswa kumaphosta , tatiso nalokunye . Labangenele tifundvo baniketwa litfuba lekwengeta imininingwane lesele ngesikhatsi sekuhlanganisa kwekucala . Tinhlangano letiphawulwe kuSigaba 1 ticatsaniswa nalemiphumela lebekwe ngabocalangaye . Umhlangano uphindze utfole litfuba lekwengeta imininingwane levela kutinkhulumo-luhlolo nebaphakeli betinsita kanye nemisebenti uphindze uhlole ubuye uhlolisise imiphumela uma kucatsaniswa nesifinyeto se-IDP , kusimama kwemacembu etenhlalakahle kanye neliphepha lemininingwane yesimondzawo nekuhleleka kwemhlaba . Kuchumana - loku tincwadzi letitfunyelwe ekomidini nobe leto letibhalelwe likomidi . Yonkhe imibhalo yekuchumana kufanele ibonwe likomidi isatfunyelwa ngeligama lalo . EmaKomidi emaWadi akasito tinhlaka letihlelekile tahulumende letinemandla . Ngemakomidi lalulekako lakhiwe bantfu labati kahle indzawo nalabangasita likhansela kutsi likwati kubonisana , kubikela kanye nekwatisa bantfu kanye nekutsatsa tincumo letincono emkhandlwini . Emakhansela emawadi awatiphendvuleli ngekwemtsetfo emaKomidini emawadi abo - atiphendvulela kumkhandlu , kubalingani babo kanye nasemmangweni . Ummango kumele utfole litfuba lekubeka imibono kulekhophi i-IDP ingakaphasiswa . Emakomidi EmaWadi amcoka ekusebenteni kahulumede waSekhaya . Ngiwo lasebenta nalabaphetse tembusave , emakhansela , kuciniseka kutsi masipala wenta lutfo ngetidzingo temimango nekutsi futsi uyatifeza tindzingeko temmango ngalokuanele . Inchazelo ! Ngalokuhle , linyenti lalemininingwane kumele ngabe ihlanganiswe kusenesikhatsi ngubochwepheshe beCBP , kepha hlola leKomidi yeWadi kanye nekhansela kutsi ngabe ayikho yini leminye imitfombo lebalulekile lengahle isetjentiswe . Imihlangano yesive iniketa litfuba lekutfola timphendvulo nekushiyelana lwati kepha ngoba ivamisa kubanjwa nelinani lelinyenti lebantfu , mancane ematfuba etinkhulumo letinemininingwane naletijulile etindzabeni . Ilungele kubika imisebenti yemkhandlu nobe tintfo letike taphakanyiswa emhlanganweni lowendlulile . Sebentisa indlela yekubuta imibuzo kute utewutfola kuchazeleka ngalokushiwo ngulomunye . Emakomidi emawadi ngekwawo angeke akhone kulawula imiklamo lemikhulu yekwetfulwa kwetinsita emawadini awo , loku kungena ngaphansi kwemsebenti wabomasipala . Kufaka sandla kwalabo labatfola lolusito nako kubalulekile ekucinisekiseni imphumelelo yekwetfulwa kwetinsita nasekuchubekiseni intsandvo yelinyenti . Etigodzini lapho bantfu babanyenti nobe bahlala bagcagcene , emakomidi lamancane angakhiwa kuye ngetikhundla-msebenti letikhona . NgaLeyo ndlela emaKomidi emaWadi angatfola letfuba lekusebenta ngalokujulile tindzaba temimango . Loku kungenta kuhlanganyela emkhatsini wemmango nemaKomidi emaWadi nakwentiwa tincumo kucine . Ngaphandle kwetakhiwo / tinkhundla letejwayelekile tekubonisana nemmango njengeMaKomidi eLiwadi , neTinkhundla Letimele i-IDP , masipala unelilungelo lekukhulisa luhlelo lwekubonisana nekuchumana nemmango endzaweni yawo lesemtsetfweni . Angasungula tigungu talabatsintsekako lapho khona bahlanganisa ndzawonye labatsintsekako labasuka emacenjini etintsandvo letehlukene , ngekulandzela luhlelo lwetigungu lolushaywe emitimbeni leyehlukene . Emakomidi esicheme - bani neluhla loluphelele lwemakomidi ephothifoliyo yemkhandlu wakho nemininingwane yekutsintsana nemalunga ekomidi yesicheme kute utobaniketa lwati loluvamile nalokufakwako etintfweni leticondzene nekomidi yabo . Cela emakhophi alemitsetfo kumasipala wakho uma uyidzinga . Kuphetsa - lesi sigaba lesibalulekile enchubeni yekwehlulela , umehluleli kumele ente siciniseko kutsi sivumelwano sirekhodiwe ekwenetiseni nasekusayindweni ngiwo onkhe emacembu . Liphepha Lelimhlophe liphindze liphakamise kutsiboMasipala kumele bakhe emacebo kute kucinisekiswe kubandzakanyeka emitameni nasekwakhiweni kwenchubomgomo , kanye ne M&E yekutsatsa tincumo nekwenta . Beluleki besithekhiniki bangadlala indzima lebalulekile njengobe baniketa emakhono nebuchwepheshe ummango longenako , ngaloko-ke kubalulekile kuletsa beluleki besithekniki / baphakeli betinsita labavela emazingeni laphakeme kuhulumende waSekhaya , emaNGO nobe umkhakha letimele wangasese . Kubandzakanyeka kwebeluleki besithekniki kumele kusite inchubo ngekuniketa ngeligalelo lelifanele , ngaphandle kwekubeka imiphumela ngaphambilini . Kwenta sibonelo kubandzakanyeka kwebeluleki besithekniki kuyasita uma imimango ikhetsa emasu nemiklamo yekuzuza imigomo yawo , lokusho kutsi ngelusuku lwesine kunchubo yekuhlela . Kuhlanganiseka - kwemitamo kanye nelizinga lelisetulu lekuchumanisa kundzingekile kucinisekisa kutsi kufakeka kwebulili kusebenta njengendlela lephelele lecondze ekuguculeni timiso letibanga tiphindze tibhebhetelise kungalingani ngebulili , kunekutsi kugcilwe ekwenteni tintfo ngemancozuncozu . Letinye tintfo letifana nebuhlanga / buve , sikhundla sasemmangweni / sigaba sekutsatseka esiveni kanye nebudzala nako kunemtselela endleleni lebaphatseka ngayo bafati . Kungalingani ngekwebulili angeke kunakekeleke ngalokwenele ngaphandle kwekutsi kungalingani lokusukela kuletinye tingoni nako kunakekeleke . Lisu liyinchubo , nobe indlela , lokutawufinyelelwa ngayo kumigomo . EmaKomidi emaWadi adzinga kucinisekisa kutsi onkhe emacembu netinhlangotsi temmango timbazdanyekekile kute kutociniseka kuhlanganyela kwesive . Kushayisana kungabonakala kuyintfo lembi , kungakha netimo letiyingoti kubantfu . Sibonelo , simo sekushayisana singabanemphumela webudlova , bantfu balimale , kwakhe inkhatsato nekwesaba . Kutibandzakanya kwemmango kuyadzingeka kufeza tidzingo temtsetfo letimiswe kuMtsetfo weTinhlelo taMasipala , 2000 , nakuMtsetfo weTakhiwo taMasipala , 1998 . EmaKomidi eLiwadi asebenta njengendlela yekuchumana emkhatsini kwalabatsintsekako , ngakoke kumele babenelwati nenchubo yekuchumana lokuphumelelisako . I-PMS yamasipala kumele ifake ekhatsi tintfo letikhonjwe ngumkhandlu , leticondzene ngco netindzawo letibalulekile tekusebenta tamasipala wawo . Ema-IDP amasipala akhomba imiklamo netinsuku tekuwacedza leticacile netinkhomba tekuchubeka . Emakhansela anendzima lemcoka yekulandzelela kusebenta kwamasipala mayelana naletetfulo letibalulekile . EmaKomidi eLiwadi kumele ente siciniseko kutsi atejwayete emaKPI netinhloso tekusebenta letibekwe ku-IDP yamasipala wabo khona batokhona kuhlola inchubekelaphambili . Letitinchubo tifaka ekhatsi kubuka nekukala inchubekela embili kute kucinisekiswe kutsi tinhloso temklamo tiyenteka , kubona lokwehlukile eluhlelweni kute kutsatfwe tinyatselo tekulungisa letifanele . Iphindze ifake ekhatsi tindlela tekuvikela tinkinga letingahle tivele . Loku kufaka ekhatsi kucatsanisa kusebenta lokungiko kwangengempela kanye nekusebenta lokuhleliwe . Ngubani lokhokhela sakhiwonchanti setemnotfo ? Letinye tinhlobo tesakhiwonchanti tiletsa inzuzo lebanti kutenhlalo nakutemnotfo . Kepha kudlala umdlalo wekuvala sikhla kusho kutsi imali lebitwako kumele yenyuke kwesikhashana kute yenta tinhlelo tetimali tihambe kahle . Liciniso lekutsi siphehlagezi sinye lesisha ( lesikhicita 4 800MW wagezi ) sibita kabili kunesamba sonkhe sekwehla kwelinani lemphahla yesiphehlagezi lesikhona njenganyalo ( lesikhicita 40 0 MW ) likhombisa incabhayi . Ngetulu kwaloko , emazinga lasetulu ekungabi khona kwemisebenti kanye nekungalingani kwenta letinye taletinhlelo tibite kakhulu kulinyenti lebantfu ngaphandle uma belekelelwa ngetimali . Tincenye tetenhlalo letinemandla tidlala indzima lefaka sandla . Imicondvo leyakhekile yekutsi sakhiwo semnotfo asikalungi , kungalingani kwemnlandvo kanye nekuhlela kabusha lokusha kwekuhlomisa lokuhlomise labo labasondzelene nabetembusave kubhebhetsekise lisiko lapho inkhohlakalo iphumelela khona , kuhulumende nakumabhizimisi . Letinkinga tetenhlalo letibalulekile kumele tilungiswe njengencenye yekulwa nenkhohlakalo . Niketa emacembu sikhatsi lesinu 15 wemaminithi kusebenta lesibonelo . Kutawudzingeka umhlengikati losatsetse umhlalaphansi nemphatsi kuncedza kulomklamo baphindze babuke kuniketwa kwalamanye emaphasela ekudla emindenini lehluphekako . Kufanele kusayindwe uma uniketwa emaphasela ekudla kuphindze kubekwe luhlu lwekuvakasha lokwentiwa banakekeli . Sinyatselo 2 - Yakhani luhlelo lwekulandzelela kusebenta ( faka : emacophelo etinsita , sisusa sedatha , indlela , umuntfu lobhekeke kusebenta , liphakelo-timali lekucokelela idatha , tikhatsi tekucokelela idatha neluhlelo ) . Labatsintsekako bafaka ekhatsi emakhansela eliwadi , tisebenti tamasipala , tisebenti tentfutfuko yemmango , emalunga emmango nemacembu lanenshisakalo . Kumsebenti 3 kungabamcoka kukhombisa babambilichaza i-POWERPOINT C. Indlela lesuka etigungwini iniketa litfuba lemikhakha lehlukene nobe emacembu kutsi ahlangane asebentele umgomo lofanako . Imikhakha leyehlukene nemacembu ayahlangana kubambisana kumklamo lotsite . Yini lekudzingeka siyigucule kute kwenteke ? EmaKomidi emaWadi kufanele alawule kwehlukahlukana kwetimo letiningi , kusukela ekwehlukahlukaneni emkhatsini wemalunga eKomidi yeliWadi kuya ekwehlukahlukaneni lokusemmangweni wonkhe . Letifundvo leti tigcila ekwehlukahlukaneni lokusemmangweni nendlela lokutsintsana ngayo nentfutfuko . Bonkhe labatsintsekako ekuphatfweni kwabohulumende basekhaya kumele babe nelwati lolusisekelo ekuphatfweni kwetindzawo tasekhaya , tinhloso , tindzima nemisebenti . EmaKomidi emaWadi angasita kuniketela ngalolwati emmangweni . Yini lokwentako lokwenta kube malula kutsi bakhulume nawe ? Emakhansela leti lolwati atsembele kulabanalolwati kubasita kwenta tincumo letisem'tsetfweni nem'gomeni wamasipala . Emakhansela kufute atihlolisise tincomo letetiwa tisebenti kute abenesiciniseko kutsi tiyahambelana netifiso , netidzingo temmango . Uma ikhansela seyivumelene , tisebenti setingachubeka tente lokuncunyiwe ngendlela lengiyo futsi letakonga . Lamacembu etenhlalakahle kumele abe aphawulwe ngesikhatsi sekuhlelela kwangaphambilini aphindze acinisekiswa emhlanganweni wekwetfula emmangweni , kepha emacembu langetiwe angaphawulwa ngesikhatsi sekuhlela . Lihhovisi lentfutfuko : loku kungenteka kube kwakungumphumela lomcoka kakhulu wekucala iMasincedane Development Corporation . Masincedane uletsa intfutfuko netinsita tekwelekelela ummango , lokufaka ekhatsi lihhovisi lelincane lebhizinisi , inkhundla yalabelekelela tingadzi emmangweni , nenkhundla yekuyala leniketa lusito loluhambisana nemtsetfo netenhlalakahle . Simo sayo njengenkapani yeSigaba 21 kuyente yagcugcutelele kutfola timali ngemphumelelo , kuphatsa tinsita , nekwetama kutfutfukisa timo tebantfu bendzawo . Kwengeta , lokutsi sakhiwo sayo sisekhatsi edolobheni , kwenta kutsi kube yindzawo yekutsatsisa yetinhlangano tentfutfuko tangephandle nemmango wendzawo . Nhlanhlalembi , tinkinga tetimali eminyakeni lesandza kwendlula kuyisebentisa kabi . Kufanele kubhalwe phansi emagama alabo labakhona emhlanganweni . Kwenta inchubekelembili lesheshako nalesimeme ekunciphiseni buphuya nekungalingani kuleminyakalishumi lemibili letako , iNingizimu Afrika idzinga kulungisa sikhatsi lesitako kusukela lamuhla . Loluhlelo luchaza indlela yekutfutfukisa lensha ledzinga kuhlanganyela nemimango , lusha , tisebenti labangasebenti kanye nalababambisene emabhizimisini nembuso lokhona kwenta . Inhloso yaloku kutfutfukisa emakhono ebantfu ngamunye kanye nawelive , kusungula ematfuba awo wonkhe umuntfu . Ngalokuhlatiyako , loluhlelo lugcizelela sidzingo lesiphutfumako sekunonophisa inchubekelembili etincenyeni letinyenti kute kuncishiswe buphuya nekungalingani ngalokusimeme . Kwetfula imibono - imibono ingentiwa kukhansela yeliwadi nobe ngekucondza ngco kumkhandlu mayelana netidzingo temmango letitsite . Uma ukholwa kutsi ufake sandla esisuseni seinftukutselo , ungachazi , ucolise nobe uphendvule ate lomunye umuntfu avete lulaka lwakhe . Kungakenteki loku , kungenteka ningakhoni kubanenkhulumo lebhadlile . Lubanjiswano - ummango kanye nemkhandlu basebenta ngekubambisana bafake sandla ekuhleleni nasekutsatseni tincumo . Ekugcineni ngumkhandlu lonelivi lekugcina . Bhala phansi kutsi laba lababhalwe kuloluhla yini umsebenti wabo . Usakwenta loku , cabanga ngamasipala wakini . Tikhumbute ngetikhatsi temisebenti letitawutsikameta emawadi abo . Kutsatsa sikhatsi lesingakanani emalunga eKomidi yeliWadi angakacali kusebenta ngekungatikhandli esigabeni lakuso ? Kwenta luhlelo lwemaphoyisa lube ngulolusebenta ngalokuceceshekile . Indlela yekutiphatsa kwemaphoyisa kumele ichunyaniswe nekukhushulwa kanye nekutiphatsa kahle emsebentini . Luhlelo lwekuheha bantfu kumele luhehe bantfu labaceceshiwe labakhonako kwenta umsebenti nalabanemakhono labaceceshiwe ngeluhlelo lolumikhakha mibili ; munye wetisebenti leticashelwe kuba tikhulu nalomunye wetisebenti letingakacashelwa kuba tikhulu . Kungenelela kwelusito lwetebuchwepheshe lwe-GEP kutakusita wente tilinganiso letitsite mayelana nelikusasa lebhizinisi yakho . Loku kufaka ekhatsi kwenta lucwaningo loluhlelekile nalolulandzela tinchubo letitsite lwawo onkhe emaciniso lafanele kanye nedatha , uhlanganise idokhumenti yetemtsetfo ledzingekako ubuye futsi uhlole tingoti letiphatselene nekuchuba ibhizinisi yakho ngemphumelelo . UMBUTO 1 Yini injongo yekulalelwa kweliphakelo-timali ? Kumele kwentiwe kukhetsa lokumatima . Kute kutfutfukiswe kwakhiwa kwemisebenti leminyenti , kusebenta kwemkhakha wetisebenti kumele kwentiwe ncono . IKhomishini yenta siphakamiso lesihlose kusita bantfu labasha kutsi bangene emisebentini , kwentiwe lula imitsetfo yemabhizimisi lamancane , kuncishiswe kungcubutana nekungevani kuphindze kucaciswe tinchubo tekucosha nekungatiphatsi kahle . Kumele kuphindze kunakwe kakhulu kunikwa kucecesha lokuchubekako etisebentini letivele tisemsebentini kuphindze kunikwe tonkhe tisebenti imigudvu yemisebenti . Hulumende wasekhaya kumele abikele ummango kutsi imali labanayo bayisebentisa kanjani . Benta loku ngekukhipha titatimende tetimali letihloliwe . Umcondvo longenamaciniso ngumucondvo lofananisa licembu lelitsite lebantfu noma sehlo lesitsite . Nomangisiphi sisho lesimayelana neluhlangotsi lolutsite lwebantfu kuvame kutsi sibe ngumcondvo longemaciniso . Imicondvo lengemaciniso ayisimibi ngasosonkhe sikhatsi futsi labaningi bantfu bayakholelwa kuleminye yalemicondvo lenjena . Umsebenti lomkhulu wemakhansela kuchumanisa labo lababamele namasipala . Kufanele batati tidzingo tebantfu bese bayatibika kukhansela . Emakhansela emaWadi wona aphoceleke kutsi abike konkhe lokwentekako kubantfu labahlala emaWadini abo . Emakhansela lamele emacembu wona kufute amele leto tibopho netifiso temacembu awo . Emakhaya nemimango . Kudla lokunemsoco lokufanele kanye nekudla lokukhetsekile , ikakhulukati kwebantfwana labangaphasi kweminyaka lemitsatfu , kubalulekile kute kutfutfuke umtimba nengcondvo ngalokuvakalako . IKhomishini yenta tiphakamiso mayelana nekudla lokunemsoco kubantfwana , kusita batali nemindeni kucedza umjikeleto webuphuya kanye nekulungiselela bantfwana labancane lokuhamba embili - lokufaka ekhatsi kutsi wonkhe umntfwana kumele lokungenani abe nemfundvo yeminyaka lemibili ngembi kwekuya esikolweni . UMBUTO 3 Unalo yini liphakelo-timali lenyanga ? Bonkhe labantfu labatsintsekako bafaka sandla ekutfutfukiseni tinsita nemphumelelo yekwetfula . Kepha-ke , munye ngamunye lodlala indzima kumele acondzisise kutsi yini lakuletsako kulowomklamo jikelele . Kubalulekile kutsi imisebenti yabo irekhodwe eluhlelweni lwentfutfuko . Ngesikhatsi sesigaba sekucala seMvila-balave weCBP litsimba lekuhlela ligcogca liphindze lihlatiye imininingwane kanye nelwati loluvele lukhona emmangweni ngekusebentisa luchungechunge lwetinkhulumo-luhlolo kanye nekusebentisa emathuluzi lahlukene eCBP . Kuhlatiywa lokujulile kwalemininingwane kuniketa litsimba lekuhlela ngelingemuva lelibanti nalelijulile mayelana nesimo semmango , tinkinga , emasiko , imikhuba , tinhlelo kanye nemagugu awo . Kulesigaba umehluleli uyayephetsa lenchubo . Singeniso - injongo yalesigaba kutfutfukisa kwetsembana nekukholwela emacembu kulenchubo . Ngalesigaba lesi , onkhe emacembu ( lokufaka ekhatsi umehluleli ) bavumelana ngemitsetfo letawulandzelwa kusachubekwa . Sibonelo , emacembu ayavumelana kutsi uma lelinye licembu letfula luhlangotsi lwawo lwendzaba , kute lotakubaphazamisa . Umhluleli - umchubi ngumenti , kungadzingeka angenele kwenta siciniseko kutsi lenchubo igcinela emiphumeleni lefisiwe . Umchubi uphindze asombulule kushayisana kwemibono . Sigaba 195 ( e ) - ngekuya kwetintfo letatiswako kanye nemigomosisekelo yekuphatfwa kwebantfu nguhulumende - tidzingo tebantfu kumele tifezwe , kantsi nemmango kumele ukhutsatwe kutsi utibandzakanye ekwakhiweni kwetinchubomgomo . Emalunga eliKomidi leliwadi nebachubisifundvo beCBP labacedzele emaphepha eluhlatiyo lwemazinga emphilo kumele babe nemhlangano welicembu . Kulandzelela nekukala kusebenta kwekwetfulwa kwetinsita , yinchubo yekuhlola imetamo yekufinyelela emigomeni lebekiwe , kudzingekile kuyinye ngayinye imboni yevoti yeliphakelo-timali ngeSigaba 27(4) se-PFMA . Tinhloso tekusebenta timeselwe kutfutfukisa konga tindleko , nemphumelelo yekukalwa kwekwetfulwa kwetinsita konkhana . Inchubo yekuhlola umsebenti ingasetjentiswa njengelithulusi lekutihlola , kumisa imigomo , kulandzelela inchubo nekwengamela kuchumana nemakhasimende langephandle . Sigaba 3 sibukelele ekwakhiweni mbamba kweLisu . Uma kusahanjwa ngekwenchubo yesinyatselo ngesinyatselo , ummango utsatsa imininingwane lehlanganisiwe bese ubeka bocalangaye bemiphumela uphindze uyilumbanise iba ngumbono , sitatimende semgomo , emachinga , imiklamo nemisebenti yekukwenta nconokwenta ncono imphilo yemmango . Kwandzisa tinhlelo temisebenti yesive kufinyelela esigidzini sinye nga-2015 nasetigidzini letimbili nga-2020 . Kungabese kuncishiswa tinhlelo temisebenti yesive uma sekwandza umkhakha wemisebenti lehlelekile nalengakahleleki . Ngesikhatsi salomsebenti lolandzelako kuchutjwa tinkhulumo-luhlolo nebaphakeli betinsita kutsi kutohlolwa umtsamo webaphakeli betinsita labaphawulwe ngesikhatsi semsebenti lowengcile kutsi bafake ligalelo ekusebentiseni , kuhlola tinkinga labahlangabetana nato , kanye nekubafaka kunchubo yekuhlela . Loku kutawusita ekwakheni emasu lanembako nalatawuphumelela . Khumbula kuhlela letinkhulumo-luhlolo kusenesikhatsi lesihle . Kuniketa timphendvulo : kukhombisa kutsi tinsita tisetjentiswa kahle nangendlela lephakanyisiwe yekusebenta kwemklamo kanye neyetivumelwano tetimali . LiKomidi leliWadi linelikhansela leliWadi kanye nabantfu labalishumi lababavoti ewadini labakhetfwa ngummango kutsi babamele . Emalunga eliKomidi leliWadi kumele amelwe ngalokubanti tincenye temmango letahlukene ( bomake , labasha , imimango lenganakwa , njll ) . Emacembu etembusave labawesekelako akukameli abukwe ekukhetfweni kwabo . Emalunga eliKomidi leliWadiatibandzakanya ngekutitsandzela .
